# CHANGELOG

- **ADR-079 Skill routing optimization (`apps/api`, `apps/runtime`, `apps/web`, `packages/runtime-contract`; routing cost/latency 2026-05-01):** added per-chat auto Skill routing state so an active Skill can be reused without calling the routing LLM on every turn. New chats get early background checks, active Skill state is persisted on `assistant_chats`, sticky Skill reuse directly selects Skill retrieval, periodic background rechecks can keep or clear the active Skill on topic drift, and high-signal grounded requests still force a blocking classifier check. Runtime/API now expose a dedicated Skill routing check path for background refresh, and web activity quietly includes the active Skill name in existing retrieval badges. Focused regressions cover startup/background scheduling, sticky reuse, drift clearing, high-signal blocking, zero enabled Skills, and Skill activity detail.

- **Runtime background tasks and ADR-074 long-idle continuity fix (`apps/runtime`; notification/carry-over reliability 2026-05-01):** fixed idle-reengagement background task evaluation by replacing receipt `requestId`/`idempotencyKey` values that embedded the full scheduler dedupe key with a deterministic short hash key that fits the `runtime_turn_receipts` `VARCHAR(128)` columns. Fixed ADR-074 long-idle cross-session carry-over so the trigger compares against the previous user message timestamp, excluding the current inbound message, instead of trusting `assistant_chats.lastMessageAt` after the API may already have advanced it for the current turn. Verification: runtime suite, runtime lint, runtime typecheck.

- **ADR-079 zero-Skills plan persistence fix (`apps/api`, `apps/web`; founder plan-limit UI follow-up 2026-05-01):** fixed the Admin Plans path so `Max enabled Skills = 0` is a valid saved plan value instead of a validation error or dropped value. Web plan draft validation now allows `0`, API plan parsing/state reconstruction preserves `skillPolicy.maxEnabledSkills=0`, assistant Skill assignment enforcement reads `0` as a real limit, and published materialization treats zero-Skills plans as zero rather than falling back to default limits. Verification: focused Admin Plans, assistant Skills, and Skill selector tests.

- **ADR-079 plan-zero Skills selector state (`apps/web`; founder plan-limit UI follow-up 2026-05-01):** when a plan allows `0` enabled Skills, user-facing Skills selectors now keep the full catalog visible but disable Skill enabling and show a localized plan-upgrade hint under the selector intro. The collapsible selector expands to the full catalog in this state so users can still understand what Skills exist. Verification: focused `AssistantSkillsManager` test and changed-file lints.

- **ADR-079 router classifier default prompt strengthening (`apps/api`, live dev DB; founder routing follow-up 2026-05-01):** strengthened the default `router_classifier` prompt with explicit retrieval-plan rules for semantic Skill selection, user knowledge, Product knowledge, web grounding, multi-source retrieval, and no-retrieval cases. The prompt now tells the router to use Skill names/descriptions/tags/categories/routing examples as meaning hints, not generic words like "document", "knowledge", "PDF", or "search". The live dev DB `router_classifier` prompt was synchronized and global config generation bumped so Admin Presets shows the updated text before a code redeploy/reset.

- **Welcome chat Russian title encoding fix (`apps/web`; Capacitor recreate follow-up 2026-05-01):** replaced a mojibake Russian first-chat title literal in the web welcome-turn payload with `Добро пожаловать`, so assistant recreate/setup no longer creates a broken chat title while the welcome message body remains normal. Added focused `use-chat` coverage for the Russian welcome payload title.

- **ADR-079 semantic Skill routing precheck gap (`apps/runtime`, `docs`; founder GKE validation fix 2026-05-01):** live GKE logs and persisted web turn attempts showed enabled `Диетолог` turns still finalizing in runtime precheck as `simple_turn` / `reasoning_request` with `retrievalPlan.useSkills=false`, so `/internal/runtime/knowledge/orchestrate` was never called even though the assistant had the active Skill, ready Skill PDF chunks, and runtime bundle `routingExamples`. Runtime precheck now defers non-continue turns to the semantic classifier whenever enabled Skills exist, before deterministic reasoning/premium/simple branches can finalize the decision. Added a regression for a short Russian diet/T1D question without explicit "find in docs" wording so Skill routing no longer depends on retrieval keywords.

- **Web/Capacitor text send optimistic UX regression fix (`apps/web`; mobile chat reliability 2026-05-01):** restored immediate local user-bubble rendering for text sends by claiming the optimistic chat turn before the forced fresh Clerk token refresh, while keeping `getToken({ skipCache: true })` for the actual stream request so stale-session protection remains. Empty assistant placeholders no longer show `thinking` while the previous user bubble is still in `sending`/`reconciling`, so the UI only moves from send spinner to assistant thinking after the send is accepted. Verification: focused `use-chat` and `chat-area` tests plus web typecheck.

- **ADR-079 base Skill catalog seed and grouped selector (`apps/api`, `apps/web`, `docs`; founder catalog population 2026-05-01):** added a repeatable `prisma/seed-base-skills.ts` script with 26 active admin-curated base Skills across `personal`, `work`, and `engineering`, including localized names/descriptions, concise instruction cards, guardrails, tags, and routing examples intended for the semantic Skill router. The live GKE dev catalog was populated through the API pod environment (`26` active Skills: `10` personal, `10` work, `6` engineering; existing `Dietitian/Диетолог` updated). User-facing Skill selection now groups cards with `Личное` first, then work/engineering/education, and both setup/recreate and Assistant Settings show the first few cards with an expand/collapse control. API lint now includes the base Skill seed script. Verification: focused web Skill tests, full workspace lint, format check, API/Web typechecks, and live DB group verification.

- **ADR-079 semantic Skill routing correction (`apps/api`, `apps/runtime`, `packages/runtime-bundle`, `docs`; founder live validation fix 2026-05-01):** removed the keyword-only Skill routing hotfix and restored ADR-079's semantic router contract. Enabled Skill summaries in runtime bundles now include up to two admin-authored instruction-card examples as compact routing hints, and the runtime classifier receives those examples without full Skill documents or full instruction cards. When enabled Skills exist, deterministic knowledge precheck no longer auto-selects all Skills; it defers knowledge-intent turns to the semantic classifier so `selectedSkillIds` are chosen by meaning before orchestrated retrieval injects Skill context.

- **ADR-079 setup Skills placement and Skill groups UI (`apps/web`, `docs`; founder UI follow-up 2026-05-01):** moved setup/recreate Skill selection from the final preview step into the previous personalization step, using the compact Professional Skills selector with two visible cards and an explicit expand/collapse control instead of an inner scrollbar. Admin Skills now use a group selector backed by the existing `Skill.category` field (`work`, `engineering`, `personal`, `education`), and user-facing cards render localized group labels. Docs clarify that `Skill.category` is the current Skill group key and that Skill assignment uses the platform catalog.

- **ADR-079 Assistant Settings Skills polish (`apps/web`; founder UI follow-up 2026-05-01):** collapsed the duplicated Skills intro/counter cards into one compact premium header, changed the counter to a simple `enabled / limit` presentation without plan-status copy, shortened the helper text, sorted enabled Skills first, and constrained the Skill card grid to a two-column scroll area with only the first row visible. Verification: web typecheck, format check, changed-file lints.

- **ADR-079 native document processor adapters (`apps/api`, `docs`; founder GKE validation fix 2026-05-01):** corrected Skill/Product/user knowledge indexing to follow the ADR-079 document-processing contract instead of relying on the older chat media PDF fallback. `KnowledgeDocumentProcessorService` now reads the persisted `/admin/tools` document-processing policy and PersAI-managed encrypted provider keys, routes complex documents to Mistral OCR by default, escalates poor/empty extraction to LlamaParse when configured, and keeps local parsing local for explicit/simple local processing. Indexing job claim TTL is now long enough for provider-backed document parsing so another API pod does not reclaim the same long-running OCR job as stale, and terminal empty-extraction failures now preserve provider/quality trace instead of recording `null`. Added focused regressions so provider-backed PDFs do not call the media preprocessor/OpenAI provider-gateway path and failed rows retain provider trace. Verification: focused processor/worker tests, API lint, API typecheck, format check.

- **ADR-079 platform Skills visibility and plan-limit control (`apps/api`, `apps/web`, `packages/contracts`, `docs`; founder validation fix 2026-05-01):** corrected first-class Skills to behave as a platform-wide admin catalog for a multi-user platform. User Skill listing, assignment validation, prompt materialization, and runtime retrieval validation now allow active admin-created Skills across assistant workspaces while still requiring explicit user assignment and active Skill status. Admin Plans now expose `Max enabled Skills` as a first-class plan field backed by `skillPolicy.maxEnabledSkills` / `enabled_skills_limit`, and Assistant Settings Skills cards were made more compact. Docs now state `Skill.workspaceId` is creation/audit provenance rather than selection visibility. Verification: focused assistant Skills and admin plan service tests, changed-file lints, API/web typechecks.

- **ADR-079 deploy-readiness fixes (`apps/api`, `apps/runtime`, `apps/web`, `docs`; audit follow-up 2026-05-01):** closed audit blockers before deploy by registering Clerk middleware for ADR-079 Skills/document-processing/indexing routes, implementing the OpenAPI-declared knowledge indexing job list endpoints, preserving injected `Retrieved Knowledge Context` across runtime durable-compaction message refreshes, preserving classifier-selected Skill id casing, removing active-path legacy global `scope=skill` knowledge assumptions and live UI/type copy tails, and tightening web UX around fresh tokens, setup Skill assignment retention, session-expired loading states, localized fallback activity, and current Skills copy. Verification: focused identity/knowledge/runtime/web tests, runtime package suite, full recursive test suite, full lint, format check, and API/web/runtime typechecks.

- **ADR-079 Step 12 Activity copy and observability (`apps/api`, `apps/runtime`, `apps/web`, `packages/runtime-contract`; knowledge architecture 2026-05-01):** added calm retrieval activity for source-aware orchestrated context and durable source-level observability for retrieval orchestration. Runtime now emits lightweight `retrieval_activity` stream events for retrieved Skill/user/Product/web source classes; API forwards them over existing web SSE, and web renders concise localized activity badges without exposing the internal plan. The API orchestrator records `skill`, `document`, `product`, and `web` plan-source telemetry through `KnowledgeRetrievalObservabilityService` with duration, result counts, empty/error outcomes, and no full prompt/chunk logging. Existing low-level `knowledge_search` / `knowledge_fetch` tools remain unchanged; no public/runtime `skill` source was added. Verification: focused API orchestrator test, runtime turn execution test, web activity badge test, full lint, format check, API/web/runtime typechecks.

- **ADR-079 Step 11 Orchestrated retrieval and source-aware context injection (`apps/api`, `apps/runtime`, `packages/runtime-contract`; knowledge architecture 2026-05-01):** added internal orchestrated retrieval execution for router `retrievalPlan` output and injected a bounded `Retrieved Knowledge Context` block before the current model turn. The orchestrator revalidates selected Skills server-side, searches ready Skill document chunks as `skill_reference`, reuses existing user/Product retrieval services as `user_document` and `product_reference`, and keeps `web_reference` reserved without inventing web content. Runtime excludes the injected block from prompt-cache key material. Verification: focused API orchestrator test, runtime turn execution test, API/runtime/web typechecks.

- **ADR-079 Step 10 Runtime router `retrievalPlan` (`apps/runtime`, `apps/api`, `packages/runtime-bundle`, `packages/runtime-contract`; knowledge architecture 2026-05-01):** extended the existing runtime router with additive semantic `retrievalPlan` output for enabled Skills, user knowledge, Product knowledge, and web grounding. Runtime bundles now carry compact enabled Skill summaries for classifier input, selected Skill ids are validated/capped against enabled Skills, simple-turn precheck stays fast, and the plan is propagated through runtime/API/web routing snapshots without executing retrieval yet. Verification: focused runtime routing/execution tests and runtime/API typechecks.

- **ADR-079 Step 9 Prompt materialization (`apps/api`, `apps/web`, `packages/runtime-bundle`; knowledge architecture 2026-05-01):** added Prompt Constructor-managed `enabled_skills` / `Enabled Skills` prompt materialization. Runtime bundles now include bounded user-enabled Skill instruction cards (title/body/guardrails/examples/category/tags/localized summary) only for active Skills with active assignments, omitting disabled, archived, draft, plan-disabled, and over-plan-limit Skills. Skill assignment changes and assigned Skill updates/archive now dirty affected assistant materialization. Prompt Constructor admin metadata/preview exposes the new block before tool guidance. Verification: focused enabled-Skills materialization and prompt-constructor tests, Skill assignment/admin Skill tests, API/web typechecks.

- **ADR-079 Step 8 User Skills UI and setup/recreate integration (`apps/web`; knowledge architecture 2026-05-01):** added user-facing Skill assignment surfaces without prompt/runtime retrieval materialization. Setup/recreate now loads available active Skills on the final review step, shows plan counters and disabled/archived states, keeps Skills optional and unselected by default, and saves explicit user choices through `PUT /assistant/skills` before publish. Assistant Settings now includes a dedicated Skills section using the same reusable selector, with immediate assignment updates, plan-limit messaging, and archived/over-limit explanations. Added assistant Skill API client wrappers and focused helper/setup tests. Verification: focused Skill manager/setup tests and web typecheck.

- **ADR-079 Step 7 Admin Skills UI (`apps/web`; knowledge architecture 2026-05-01):** added `/admin/skills` for real admin-managed Skills: list/create/edit/archive, localized name/description fields, category/tags/status/order, bounded instruction card editor with counters/validation, and Skill document upload/delete/reindex/status management backed by the Step 6 DB indexing jobs. `/admin/knowledge` is now Product KB only and no longer exposes the old `Skill library` scope. The web API client now treats async knowledge upload `processing` state as a valid queued result instead of an upload error. Verification: focused Admin Skills page helper test and web typecheck.

- **ADR-079 Step 6 DB-backed indexing jobs (`apps/api`; knowledge architecture 2026-05-01):** implemented source-agnostic API worker execution for `assistant_knowledge_source`, `global_knowledge_source`, and `skill_document` jobs. Assistant/Product uploads and reindex now enqueue `KnowledgeIndexingJob` rows and return `processing`; the worker claims due/stale jobs with claim token/epoch/expiry, increments attempts, retries retryable failures with backoff, terminally records clear source/job failures, applies the `needs_review` quality gate without indexing garbage chunks, persists provider/processor/quality/error state, writes legacy chunk rows, and replaces pgvector rows through the `KnowledgeVectorIndex` boundary when embeddings exist. Added source provider/quality columns for assistant/global sources to match Skill document processing truth. Verification: focused indexing worker test, updated assistant/admin knowledge service tests, admin Skill service test, API typecheck.

- **ADR-079 Step 5 Skills and Skill document APIs (`apps/api`; knowledge architecture 2026-05-01):** implemented admin Skill CRUD/archive routes, Skill document upload/delete/reindex routes, and user-controlled assistant Skill assignment routes. Skill document upload/reindex now creates pending `KnowledgeIndexingJob` rows for `sourceType=skill_document` while leaving worker execution/chunking to Step 6. Assignment replacement only accepts active Skills in the assistant workspace, disables removed assignments, marks archived Skill assignments when a Skill is archived, and enforces configured plan limits from `billingProviderHints.skillPolicy.maxEnabledSkills` or compatible `limitsPermissions` keys. Verification: focused admin Skill service test, focused assistant Skill assignment test, API typecheck.

- **ADR-079 Step 4 Document Processing provider settings (`apps/api`, `apps/web`; knowledge architecture 2026-05-01):** implemented `/admin/tools` Document Processing settings with API routes for read/update/test-connection, persisted provider policy in `platform_runtime_provider_settings.document_processing_policy`, encrypted Mistral OCR/LlamaParse keys through the existing PersAI-managed secret store, config-generation bump and admin audit on update, and a focused admin UI block for default provider, high-quality fallback, local/auto fallback, needs-review threshold, keys, and connection tests. Test connection verifies local availability or remote key decryptability; live OCR provider calls remain for the provider-adapter/job steps. Verification: focused API service test, API typecheck, web typecheck.

- **ADR-079 Step 3 processor/vector abstraction boundaries (`apps/api`; knowledge architecture 2026-05-01):** added source-agnostic knowledge processing contracts, local/default/high-quality document-processing provider policy boundaries (`local`, `mistral`, `llamaparse`), the current local `KnowledgeDocumentProcessor` adapter, and a `KnowledgeVectorIndex`/`PostgresPgvectorKnowledgeIndex` pgvector boundary for normalized chunks carrying `sourceType`, `sourceId`, `sourceVersion`, provenance/metadata, provider trace, and extraction quality. Processing statuses remain separate from future ADR-080 lifecycle governance states, and no ADR-080 ingestion/curation workflows were implemented. Verification: focused document-processing policy test, focused vector-index boundary test, existing knowledge/admin/runtime knowledge tests, API/web typechecks, full lint, and format check.

- **ADR-079 future hybrid ingestion boundary clarification (`docs/ADR`; architecture 2026-05-01):** clarified that ADR-079 remains focused on runtime Skills, document processing, vector search, router retrieval planning, and orchestrated retrieval, while web-fed/hybrid knowledge ingestion, curator-LLM maintenance, dedup/merge/cleanup, stale detection, trust governance, and knowledge lifecycle states should move to a future `ADR-080: Hybrid Knowledge Ingestion and Curation`. Step 3 now explicitly requires source-agnostic processor/index abstractions so future web/manual/generated sources can layer on without rewriting ADR-079.

- **ADR-079 Step 2 Skills/document-processing/indexing contracts (`packages/contracts`; knowledge architecture 2026-05-01):** extended `openapi.yaml` and regenerated Orval clients/models for admin Skill CRUD, Skill document upload/delete/reindex, user-controlled Skill assignment, document-processing provider policy/key/test-connection endpoints under `/admin/tools/document-processing`, and indexing job status endpoints for admin/user surfaces. Generated contracts now remove `skill` from `GlobalKnowledgeSourceScope`, include `needs_review` knowledge status, and include future retrieval observability sources for `product`, `skill`, and `web`. Verification: contracts generate/typecheck, API typecheck, web typecheck, full repo lint, format check, changed-file lints.

- **ADR-079 Step 1 Skill/indexing/vector data foundation (`apps/api/prisma`, `apps/api`; knowledge architecture 2026-05-01):** added first-class Prisma models and migration for `Skill`, `SkillDocument`, `SkillDocumentChunk`, `AssistantSkillAssignment`, DB-backed `KnowledgeIndexingJob`, document-processing policy storage on `platform_runtime_provider_settings`, and `pgvector`-backed `knowledge_vector_chunks`. The old admin `GlobalKnowledgeSource.scope=skill` value was removed from active Prisma/API model truth so `/admin/knowledge` remains Product KB only and Skill documents move to the upcoming `/admin/skills` flow. Added `needs_review` indexing status support and future retrieval observability sources for `product`, `skill`, and `web`. Verification: Prisma validate, Prisma generate, API typecheck, changed-file lints; local migration deploy check was blocked because Postgres `localhost:5432` was unavailable.

- **ADR-079 Knowledge, Skills, document processing, and orchestrated retrieval (`docs/ADR`, architecture 2026-05-01):** accepted a detailed target architecture for first-class admin Skills, user-controlled Skill assignment, Skill instruction cards in runtime prompt materialization, provider-backed document processing through `/admin/tools`, DB-backed indexing jobs, `pgvector` vector search behind an abstraction, extension of the existing runtime router with a semantic `retrievalPlan`, and orchestrated source-aware retrieval context. ADR-078 now tracks this as the active knowledge/skills program and explicitly removes the old admin `GlobalKnowledgeSource.scope=skill` concept from active product truth. ADR-079 also carries an execution ledger with per-step status markers for session-to-session implementation continuity.

- **Web chat runtime-session identity cleanup (`apps/api`, `apps/runtime`; context hotfix 2026-05-01):** live GKE/DB audit for the founder's “assistant forgot the last messages” repro showed canonical web chat history was intact, but the current `assistant_chat` row (`createdAt=2026-04-30T23:50:48Z`) was using a `surfaceThreadKey` whose runtime session was older (`createdAt=2026-04-23T17:24:43Z`). That older runtime session carried a stale compaction (`summarizedMessageCount=245`, `preservedRecentMessageCount=8`) over only 85 current hydratable chat messages, so runtime treated the current sequence as already summarized and sent the model only the old synopsis plus the current user message. The API chat lifecycle now deletes web runtime sessions/compactions/turn receipts for the same `surfaceThreadKey` when they predate the current canonical chat before accepting a new web turn, and hard-delete of a web chat deletes its matching runtime state so deleted/recreated draft thread keys cannot inherit stale context. Runtime hydration also keeps the stale-summary invariant as a defensive guard. Regressions cover stale runtime cleanup before turn prepare, hard-delete cleanup, and stale compaction fallback to real chat history.

- **Desktop composer Enter focus restore (`apps/web`; chat UX polish 2026-05-01):** fixed desktop web composer focus not reliably returning after sending with Enter. `ChatInput` now focuses the textarea immediately after send and once more on the next animation frame, preserving the existing mobile guard so touch-only keyboards are not popped. Added a regression that sends with Enter, simulates a post-keydown blur, and verifies focus returns to the composer. Verification: `chat-input.test.tsx` 10/10, format check, `ReadLints` clean.

- **Assistant response list indentation polish (`apps/web`; UI polish 2026-05-01):** adjusted markdown list rendering inside assistant response blocks so bullets, numbered lists, nested lists, and checklist rows have more left breathing room. `MarkdownFragment` list components now use a wider list indent, muted markers, and a small item text offset, making structured answers look less flush to the block edge while leaving code blocks unchanged.

- **Web chat focus-return completed-history terminal cleanup (`apps/web`; stream continuity hotfix 2026-05-01):** founder retested deployed `c96f4483`: A→B→A no longer reproduced, but the focus/app-switch bug remained. Live Chrome + GKE showed the backend was clean (`GET /assistant/chat/web/turns/:clientTurnId` 200, `web_turn_attempt_completed`, `/messages?limit=20` with `activeTurn:null` and one committed server assistant), while the DOM still showed the old `local-assistant-*` streaming bubble with a blinking cursor above the committed server assistant. Root cause: the focus/history terminal path only removed the local active turn when a history refresh introduced a _new_ server assistant relative to the current visible state; in the live repro, a previous refresh had already appended the final assistant, so later cleanup skipped and preserved the stale cursor. `refreshLatestHistory()` now treats authoritative history as terminal whenever it contains the live user followed by a committed server assistant, even if that assistant was already in `prev`; the check is order-scoped so older assistants above the live user do not kill legitimate running reattach. Authoritative no-active-snapshot merges also strip transient `local-*` / `active-assistant-*` placeholders instead of carrying stale streaming UI forward. Added a regression for the exact focus-return sequence: running status first, then completed history already present while the primary local stream hangs; the UI ends with only the committed assistant and `isStreaming=false`. Verification: focused continuity regressions and full `use-chat.test.tsx` 64/64.

- **Web chat A→B→A assistant-tail contamination + focus terminal snapshot cleanup (`apps/web`; stream continuity hotfix 2026-05-01):** live Chrome/GKE debug split the remaining founder repros from backend behavior: the API turns completed normally and `/messages?limit=20` returned clean `activeTurn:null` history, while the DOM showed extra assistant bubbles from a neighboring/older visible window under the current user message. Snapshot debug caught the client source: `activeTurnSnapshotsRef.current[thread].messages` contained non-live assistant ids (`7353...`, `eb1a...`, `642e...`) during `applyThreadMessages`, and swap-back restore admitted any assistant missing from cache as valid carry-over. The restore/merge invariant is now stricter: active snapshots can contribute only the canonical live user/live assistant pair; committed history must come from cache/server history. The legitimate terminal-reattach case is preserved by allowing a single server assistant replacement only after the local live assistant id has been removed from the snapshot. The same slice also prevents a completed primary stream from caching the old `local-assistant-*` streaming bubble beside the committed server assistant. Regressions cover completed history not restoring the old primary local assistant and active-snapshot pollution with both non-live user and non-live assistant messages disappearing from authoritative history. Verification: focused regressions, full `use-chat.test.tsx` 63/63, `ReadLints` clean.

- **Web chat focus-return stream id race + A→B→A diagnostic instrumentation (`apps/web`; stream continuity hotfix 2026-05-01):** live Chrome/GKE audit found the real focus-return freeze path after the backend 401 fix: the backend turn completed normally and `/messages?limit=20` was clean, but a focus resume `GET /assistant/chat/web/turns/:clientTurnId` returned `running` before `completed`, and `applyTurnStatusState("running")` replaced the live assistant id with the status-projected assistant id while the original primary `POST /assistant/chat/web/stream` was still alive. The primary stream handlers had captured the original local assistant id, so subsequent primary `onDelta` / `onCompleted` missed the visible status-swapped bubble, leaving a stale streaming cursor while the final committed assistant appeared separately after history refresh/F5. Running status now preserves the primary-owned assistant id whenever the primary stream still owns the same `clientTurnId`; status may update content/activity, but final id mapping remains owned by primary `onCompleted`. Added a regression that fails on old logic with a stuck `active-assistant-from-status` streaming bubble and passes on the fix. Also added gated diagnostic snapshot instrumentation for the remaining A→B→A phantom-source hunt: enable with `localStorage.setItem("persai.debug.chatSnapshots", "1")` or `?debugChatSnapshots=1`; events are emitted as `[persai-chat-snapshot-debug]` and retained in `window.__persaiChatSnapshotDebug` with callsites including `applyThreadMessages`, `swap-out-cache-sync`, `swap-back-restore`, `applyTurnStatusState:running`, terminal send handlers, and `loadHistory:*`. Verification: focused regression old-logic fail/fixed pass, full `use-chat.test.tsx` 62/62 before instrumentation, focused re-run after instrumentation, `ReadLints` clean.

- **Web chat phantom-bubble swap cleanup (`apps/web`; stream continuity hotfix 2026-05-01):** fixed the remaining A→B→A phantom user-bubble path independently from the backend 401 reconnect issue. Root cause was still in client merge rules: `activeTurnSnapshotsRef.current[thread].messages` can carry full visible state after history/restore merges, but swap-back and `mergeCommittedHistoryWithActiveTurn()` treated any snapshot message whose id was missing from cache/server history as a valid carry-over. That was necessary for a legitimate newly-appended assistant tail, but it also let non-live user messages survive after the next authoritative history refresh and later reappear beside the live assistant. The merge rules now allow snapshot carry-over only for the canonical live pair plus missing assistant messages; non-live user messages and transient optimistic assistants are purged when absent from authoritative history/cache. Added a regression that first pollutes the active snapshot with a non-live user, then returns authoritative history without that user and asserts it is removed while the live user remains. Verification: `use-chat.test.tsx` 61/61; the new test was also run against the old merge logic and failed as expected.

- **Web chat passive reconnect auth allowlist (`apps/api`; stream continuity hotfix 2026-04-30):** GKE logs for the founder's "switch to another Windows app, return, stream stops but server is still running" repro showed a concrete backend failure: `GET /api/v1/assistant/chat/web/turns/:clientTurnId` returned `401 userId=null` while adjacent chat history requests resolved a normal `userId`. The web client uses that turn-status endpoint to reconcile passive disconnects / reattach after focus changes; because the endpoint was missing from `ClerkAuthMiddleware` route registration, the API never resolved the app user and the client treated the live turn as lost, re-enabled the composer, and allowed a second send while the original server turn was still active. Added authenticated middleware registration for both `GET /api/v1/assistant/chat/web/turns/:clientTurnId` and `GET /api/v1/assistant/chat/web/turns/:clientTurnId/stream` next to the existing web chat stream/stop routes. Verification: API lint, API typecheck, format check.

- **Memory Center workspace badges/actions survive deploy/reapply (`apps/api`, `apps/web`; memory UI hotfix 2026-04-30):** fixed disappearing `ЯДРО` / `ФАКТ` / `НЕЗАКРЫТАЯ ПЕТЛЯ` labels and the missing close-loop action on Memory Center workspace rows. The Workspace tab merges registry rows with workspace-memory rows, but `/assistant/memory/workspace/items` was backed by the same registry table while returning only `id/content/createdAt/source`; the UI only rendered badges and the close-loop button for `row.source === "registry"`. When a row survived the merge as a workspace row after reload/deploy/reapply timing, the content remained but its metadata/action layer vanished. `ManageAssistantWorkspaceMemoryService` now includes `memoryClass`, `kind`, and `resolvedAt` in `WorkspaceMemoryItemState`, the web client type accepts those fields, and `AssistantSettings` renders badges from either merged source. Open-loop close now also appears for workspace rows with `kind === "open_loop"` and `resolvedAt === null`, calling the same registry close endpoint because workspace-memory ids are registry item ids; successful close removes the row from both local memory lists. Added regressions for workspace `core/fact` badges and workspace open-loop badge + close action. Verification: `ReadLints`, focused `assistant-settings.test.tsx` (18/18, existing non-fatal background-task fetch stderr), API typecheck, web typecheck.

- **Admin prompt reset hardening + live DB prompt sync (`apps/web`; admin/UX hotfix 2026-04-30):** Admin → "Reset to default" silently re-saved the editor's stale local default whenever the API call rejected. GKE logs showed the chain that broke the new Response UI Contract in production: `POST /api/v1/admin/prompt-templates/system/reset-to-default` returned `401 userId=null` and the editor fell straight into `handleSaveTemplate(id, VISIBLE_PROMPT_TEMPLATE_DEFAULTS[id])`, issuing a `PATCH /system` with status `200` that overwrote the freshly-deployed system prompt with the web bundle's older copy. Fix: `apps/web/app/admin/presets/page.tsx` syncs `VISIBLE_PROMPT_TEMPLATE_DEFAULTS.system` to the API default, and `handleResetTemplate` now throws on `!response.ok` instead of silently PATCHing — the editor surfaces the error via `saveError`. Regression test added in `apps/web/app/admin/presets/page.test.tsx` for the "rejected reset must not PATCH the stale local default" path. To unblock the founder without waiting for a redeploy, the live dev DB was upserted directly via `kubectl exec -n persai-dev deploy/api -- node -e "..."` against the running `0a36d8d9` image: `PromptTemplate.system` now holds `VISIBLE_PROMPT_TEMPLATE_DEFAULTS.system` (length `1189`, `hasContract=true`), so the next assistant turn compiles against the new contract and renders through the structured chat blocks. A speculative Pt 6 stream-continuity attempt (cache-only restore on swap-back, dropping anything outside the canonical live pair from `snapshot.messages`) was tried after founder reported a phantom user-bubble during stream + chat swap, but it broke the legitimate `refreshes terminal reattach history against the originating chat after switching away` test (a server-committed assistant lives in `snapshot.messages` before being written into cache) and was reverted; nothing in `use-chat.ts` shipped. Stream handlers are all `prev.map(updater)` and `applyTurnStatusState` only replaces the live pair, so a theoretical "stray id leak" path could not be confirmed in source. Verification: 76 / 76 focused web tests (`use-chat.test.tsx` 60, `chat-area.test.tsx` 7, `chat-message-blocks.test.tsx` 5, `admin/presets/page.test.tsx` 4), `corepack pnpm run format:check` (clean after a one-shot prettier pass on the two warning files), `corepack pnpm --filter @persai/web run typecheck`, `corepack pnpm --filter @persai/api run typecheck`.

- **Assistant markdown heading polish — remove noisy paragraph cards (`apps/web`, `apps/api`; UI polish 2026-04-30):** fixed the mismatch where headings looked correct while streaming but visually collapsed after commit. `parseAssistantResponseBlocks()` now preserves Markdown heading level (`h1/h2/h3`) for committed section titles, the opening-header detector no longer steals the first paragraph after a pending Markdown heading, and committed body titles now render with level-aware size, line-height, and breathing room. Ordinary body sections no longer render as rounded bordered cards, so normal paragraphs read as one calm premium answer rather than many noisy mini-bubbles; semantic callouts and action chips remain visually distinct. The default Response UI Contract now says opening headers should be plain lines, h2 is for major semantic blocks, h3 for quieter subsections, h1 should be avoided in normal chat, and headings should not be forced before every paragraph. The admin presets page also drops its stale local `VISIBLE_PROMPT_TEMPLATE_DEFAULTS` fallback block because reset now relies on API defaults and the block had become dead code. Verification: focused web markdown tests (19/19), prompt-template API tests, repo lint, format check, API/web typecheck, and `ReadLints`.

- **Web chat performance audit after stream continuity + response blocks (`apps/web`; performance polish 2026-04-30):** audited the current chat path from source and live CDP evidence before optimizing. CDP against the live `persai.dev` chat tab showed a moderate DOM (`~2073` nodes, `34` message containers), no buffered long tasks at capture time, and recent network dominated by expected `/assistant/chat/web/stream`, `/messages?limit=20`, and small `/compaction` calls; API audit confirmed ordinary sends still use one stream POST and status polling is scoped to reattach. The concrete client bottlenecks were render-path churn: `ChatMessageBubble` memoization was defeated by inline callbacks from `chat-area.tsx`, the response-block parser allocated `lines.slice(...)` during its scan and repeatedly joined body lines for emptiness checks, and the high-frequency streaming live tail ran through the full response-block/action-chip parser. `chat-area.tsx` now passes stable assistant-action and do-not-remember callbacks; `chat-message.tsx` now parses response blocks without slice allocations/repeated joins and renders the live streaming tail through a lighter markdown fragment while keeping structured blocks/action chips for stable/committed content. Existing code-block markdown/highlight handling is unchanged. Added regressions for stable callbacks across streaming rerenders and for hiding action chips from the mutable live tail. Verification: focused web chat vitest pack (85/85), full `@persai/web` vitest (217/217), repo lint, format check, API typecheck, and web typecheck.

- **Assistant response blocks + console cleanup (`apps/web`, `apps/api`; founder UI polish 2026-04-30):** assistant text responses now render as structured product blocks instead of one raw markdown wall. `chat-message.tsx` adds a conservative line-based parser and renderer for `header`, `body`, `callout`, `actions`, and `divider`: short first lines become header pills, `###` headings become body section titles, `>` quote blocks become calm callouts, `---` becomes a divider, and final `### Дальше` / `### Actions` bullet lists become up to 4 compact action chips. Chips draft the selected follow-up into the composer through `ChatInputHandle.setDraft()` and never auto-send. Existing fenced code blocks still render through the same `CodeBlock` / `highlight.js` path, so code colors, copy, and collapse behavior are intentionally unchanged. The default system prompt template now includes a `# Response UI Contract` telling assistants to write short header + compact sections + sparse callout + optional final action bullets while preserving fenced code exactly. Console audit via CDP also found and fixed React #418 hydration mismatch from `useNetworkOnline`: Node can expose `navigator` server-side while `navigator.onLine` is `undefined`, causing SSR to render the offline overlay and the client to render nothing; initial state is now always `true` and the real value is only applied post-mount if boolean. `ClerkProvider` now sets `prefetchUI={false}` because PersAI uses Clerk headlessly and does not need the prebuilt `@clerk/ui` bundle, removing the repeated unused-preload warning. Focused verification: chat-message blocks/message/area vitest (23/23), network/sidebar vitest (9/9), full web vitest (212/212 before docs update), prompt-template focused API tests, lint, format, API/web typecheck, and `ReadLints` on touched files.

- **Web chat stream continuity — pt 5: outgoing-sync writes to CACHE not snapshot (`apps/web`; continuity hotfix 2026-04-30):** founder live-validated pt 4 against the running pod via Chrome DevTools (127.0.0.1:9222) and reported a different, still-present symptom — items 19/20/21 of the visible chat were `[user "Напиши длинный спич для теста еще раз", user "когда openai научиться...", asst "Окей, держи ещё один длинный спич..."]`, with item 0 already being the assistant reply to "когда openai..." (the FIRST user message of the chat). The phantom user at index 20 was the same off-screen user from the very top of the chat, paginated off the visible window by `getChatMessages` (latest 20 only) but visible on screen because the founder had earlier loaded older history via `loadOlderMessages`. After a chat-swap it re-appeared right before the live assistant; F5 cleared it (hard reload purges the in-memory snapshot map and rebuilds cache from the server's paginated window only). Diagnosis traced the regression to the pt-3 outgoing-sync block which wrote the FULL visible array into `activeTurnSnapshotsRef.current.get(outgoingThreadKey).messages`. That snapshot therefore carried every visible id including those older than the paginated cache. On swap-back the restore merge `mergeChatMessagesById(cachedBase, liveSnapshot.messages.filter(m => !cachedIds.has(m.id) || liveTurnIds.has(m.id)))` saw the snapshot ids that were NOT in the paginated cache and APPENDED them at the END. Fix: redirect the outgoing-sync to write into `cachedThreadHistorySnapshotsRef` (the cache map) instead of into the snapshot, with optimistic/transient ids stripped, preserving the cache entry's `olderCursor` / `hasOlderMessages` / `chatId` fields, and also updating `cachedThreadKeyByChatIdRef`. Snapshot.messages then stays minimal (live pair + any in-flight committed appends from `refreshLatestHistory`), and the swap-back filter has nothing stale to resurrect. The `mergeCommittedHistoryWithActiveTurn` no-replace branch was kept as `mergeChatMessagesById(sanitizedLoaded, activeSnapshot.messages)` (an over-restrictive `liveTurnIds`-only filter I tried first broke the `refreshes terminal reattach history against the originating chat after switching away` test, where snapshot.messages legitimately carries a newly-appended `server-assistant-A` that is not yet in cache). One regression added: `swap A→B→A does NOT resurrect an older message at the END of the merged thread when cache is paginated and visible included loadOlderMessages results (pt-3 outgoing-sync regression)` — drives the founder repro exactly: paginated `loadHistory` with cursor, `loadOlderMessages` to bring the off-screen user into visible (but NOT into cache, since `loadOlderMessages` only writes to `setMessages`), `send()`, swap A→B→A, then asserts the off-screen user appears EXACTLY ONCE and at a position ABOVE the live user. Verification: 60 / 60 `use-chat.test.tsx` (1 new), `corepack pnpm -r --if-present run lint` (14 packages green), `corepack pnpm run format:check`, `corepack pnpm --filter @persai/web run typecheck`, `corepack pnpm --filter @persai/api run typecheck`. Live-debug evidence (CDP DOM dump showing the founder's exact 19/20/21 sequence) and the contract that any future code path writing into `snapshot.messages` MUST also keep cache in sync (otherwise the swap-back filter would re-append the unsynced ids at the end) are recorded in `docs/SESSION-HANDOFF.md`.

- **Web chat stream continuity — pt 4: synchronous re-entrancy guard for `send()` / `sendWelcome()` (`apps/web`; continuity hotfix 2026-04-30):** founder live-validated the previous pt-3 fix and reported the duplicate-user-bubble symptom STILL reproduced — but now the second bubble's text was _different_ from the first ("Давай еще последний раз" followed by "Еще"), which ruled out the optimistic-vs-server-id leak fixed in pt-3 (those collide on identical content). Founder also exposed the running tab's Chrome DevTools port (127.0.0.1:9222); attached over CDP, dumped DOM + sessionStorage + injected a MutationObserver, and re-read `send()` end to end. Root cause: `send()` (and `sendWelcome()`) check `isStreaming` (closure-stale) and `pendingSendStatusRef` (sync but null in normal idle) at the top, then `await getToken()`, then synchronously `markStreaming(true)` + `setMessages([...prev, user, asst])` + `setThreadPendingSend(... "sending")`. Between the top-of-function guards and that synchronous claim there is at least one microtask. A second `send()` invoked in that window — e.g. the user pressing Enter twice between two key events, or hitting Send right as the previous turn's `markStreaming(false)` flips but React has not re-rendered the composer yet — also passes both guards (closure value of `isStreaming` is still false; the pending-slot ref is still null until the first call's claim block runs) and proceeds. Both calls then push their own optimistic `[user, asst]` pair into `messages`, both `activeTurnSnapshotsRef.set(threadKey, ...)` (per-thread, single-slot → second silently clobbers first), both `streamAssistantWebChatTurn(...)`, both stream in parallel against the API, and the loser's `finally` cleanup runs `cacheThreadHistorySnapshot()` against whatever snapshot survives in the map (the OTHER turn's by then) and `activeTurnSnapshotsRef.delete(threadKey)` removes that snapshot mid-stream. Visible state ends with two user bubbles (different content), one assistant placeholder may go dark, the cache for the next swap is corrupt — exactly the founder's "phantom user bubble below the real one, F5 fixes it" repro. Fix: added per-thread `sendInPreflightByThreadRef = useRef<Set<string>>(new Set())`. `send()` and `sendWelcome()` now check and add to that set BEFORE `await getToken()` and remove from it on every pre-claim early exit (offline, missing token) and on the main path right after the synchronous slot-claim (right after `setThreadPendingSend(... "sending")` for `send()`, right after `setMessages([assistantMsg])` for `sendWelcome()`, since by then any subsequent `send()` is gated by the now-non-null `pendingSendStatusRef`). Two regressions added: `blocks a second send() that races the first one through `await getToken()` (no double user bubble, no double stream)` (controllable `getToken()` promise + microtask-interleaved double `send()` + asserts ONE stream, ONE user bubble) and `blocks a third send() fired in the same microtask as the second (triple-press defence)`. Verification: 59 / 59 `use-chat.test.tsx` (2 new), `corepack pnpm -r --if-present run lint` (14 packages green), `corepack pnpm run format:check`, `corepack pnpm --filter @persai/web run typecheck`, `corepack pnpm --filter @persai/api run typecheck`. Live-debug evidence and constraint that the release point of the preflight gate must move with any future change to the synchronous slot-claim are recorded in `docs/SESSION-HANDOFF.md`.

- **Web chat stream continuity — pt 3: optimistic-id leak into cached history (`apps/web`; continuity hotfix 2026-04-30):** founder live-validated the previous pt-2 fix and reported the stream itself now survived chat A→B→A swaps but a NEW symptom appeared: on swap-back, a second copy of his own user bubble showed up next to the real one (or just above / below it), sometimes with content that looked like it came from a neighbouring chat or older state. F5 fixed it. Root cause: `cacheThreadHistorySnapshot`, the `prevThreadKeyRef` swap-back restore, and `mergeCommittedHistoryWithActiveTurn` (no-replace branch) all merged cached history with the live snapshot's `liveUserMessageId` / `liveAssistantMessageId` without stripping `local-user-*` / `local-assistant-*` / `active-assistant-*` ids from the cached input. When a `loadHistory` ran during the optimistic window of `send()` (between snapshot creation with `local-user-XXX` and the server's `onStarted` event remapping it to `server-user-NEW`), the cache stored the optimistic local-_ id; later `onStarted` remapped the snapshot to the canonical server id, but the cache still carried the optimistic stub, and the next swap-back / cached-merge appended the snapshot's `server-user-_`next to the cached`local-user-_` — two bubbles with the same content but different ids. F5 worked because hard reload rebuilt cache from authoritative server history with no local-_ survivors. All three code paths now filter optimistic / transient ids out of the cached input before merging with the snapshot, and the no-snapshot restore path filters defensively too. Added regression: `swap A→B→A does NOT produce a duplicate user bubble when cached history was written between send() and onStarted (optimistic local-user-* leak)` — gates `onStarted`, runs a `loadHistory` while snapshot is still optimistic, releases `onStarted`, swaps A→B→A, asserts the live user bubble appears exactly once with the canonical server id. Verification: 57 / 57 `use-chat.test.tsx`, 207 / 207 full `@persai/web` vitest, `corepack pnpm -r --if-present run lint`, `corepack pnpm run format:check`, `corepack pnpm --filter @persai/web run typecheck`, `corepack pnpm --filter @persai/api run typecheck`.

- **Web chat stream continuity — pt 2: thread-restore window collapse (`apps/web`; continuity hotfix 2026-04-30):** founder live-repro after the previous live-id-scoping fix: on a chat A→B→A swap the stream itself continued but the user's own bubble (the question that prompted the long answer) disappeared from the chat; on a SECOND A→B→A swap while the same long stream was still in flight, the stream content vanished entirely and a phantom `Думаю...` (empty streaming assistant) appeared. Two more code paths in `apps/web/app/app/_components/use-chat.ts` collapsed the visible thread state down to a 2-message `[liveUserMessage, liveAssistantMessage]` window and dropped the older committed history above the live turn: (1) `applyTurnStatusState` running branch always rebuilt and wrote `[userMessage, liveAssistantMessage]` into both `snapshot.messages` and the visible state, so every focus / `pageshow` / `visibilitychange` resume → `softDetachReconcile` → `startTurnReattach` cycle wiped older history above the live turn; (2) the synchronous `prevThreadKeyRef` thread-restore set `setMessages(restoredSnapshot.messages)` directly from `liveSnapshot`, but during a live stream `liveSnapshot.messages` is just the live pair (the snapshot is created with that pair by `send()` and only grows to include older history AFTER a post-restore `loadHistory` cached merge), so the synchronous restore briefly showed only the 2-message window and any concurrent state mutation in that race window left older history dropped. The running branch of `applyTurnStatusState` now PRESERVES existing `snapshot.messages` / visible state, finds the live user / live assistant slots by `liveUserMessageId` / `liveAssistantMessageId` (and the previous live ids on the snapshot), and replaces them in place — only appending at the tail when not yet present. The thread-restore now pre-merges cached history with the live snapshot's live-turn slice, so the FULL state (older + live pair) is correct synchronously on swap-back, with no 2-message flicker and no race window. Three regression tests added: `switch A → B → A while streaming preserves OLDER committed history above the live turn (no 2-message flash)`, `double swap A→B→A→B→A while streaming preserves older history AND the live assistant content (no 'Думаю...' regression)`, and `soft-detach reattach (running status) PRESERVES older committed history above the live turn`. Verification: 56 / 56 `use-chat.test.tsx`, 206 / 206 full `@persai/web` vitest, `corepack pnpm -r --if-present run lint`, `corepack pnpm run format:check`, `corepack pnpm --filter @persai/web run typecheck`, `corepack pnpm --filter @persai/api run typecheck`.

- **Web chat stream continuity — id-set pollution fix (`apps/web`; continuity hotfix 2026-04-30):** founder reproduced the swap-flow regression (long answer in Chat A → switch to Chat B → switch back → live bubble disappears entirely) plus mid-stream silent disconnects requiring reload, plus a phantom upper `Думаю...` / blinking cursor that survived background completion. Root cause: `ActiveTurnSnapshot.messages` in `apps/web/app/app/_components/use-chat.ts` was overloaded as both visible thread state AND the canonical id-set of the live turn. After a `loadHistory` / cache merge, that field legitimately included OLDER committed user/assistant ids. Every reconciliation predicate (`committedHistoryHasActiveSnapshotResult`, `mergeCommittedHistoryWithActiveTurn`, `refreshLatestHistory`, terminal cleanup in `applyTurnStatusState`) scanned the polluted set, mistook those older committed ids for the live turn already landing, and tore down the live snapshot — abort controller killed, `markStreaming(false)`, snapshot deleted, live bubble gone. `ActiveTurnSnapshot` now carries explicit `liveUserMessageId` / `liveAssistantMessageId`; all reconciliation predicates use only those scoped ids and ignore `local-*` / `active-*` ids in loaded history. Two amplifying bugs were also fixed: `reattachAssistantWebChatTurnStream` in `apps/web/app/app/assistant-api-client.ts` now flushes its trailing SSE buffer (matching `streamAssistantWebChatTurn`) so a `completed` arriving on a connection close without a final `\n\n` is consumed instead of dropped; the entries-assembly in `useChat` defensively hides streaming-empty assistant placeholders that have a NEWER assistant below them, killing the phantom `Думаю...` even when the underlying placeholder cleanup did not fire. Verification: 53 / 53 `use-chat.test.tsx` (4 new live-id-scoping regressions), 34 / 34 `assistant-api-client.test.ts` (2 new reattach trailing-flush regressions), `corepack pnpm --filter @persai/web run typecheck`, `corepack pnpm --filter @persai/api run typecheck`, `corepack pnpm run format:check`, `corepack pnpm -r --if-present run lint`.

- **Android APK download affordance is quieter, centered in Assistant Settings, and hidden on the public landing inside Capacitor (`apps/web`; UI polish 2026-04-30):** restyled the shared APK link as a small premium pill with a subdued phone icon, moved the Assistant Settings instance into a centered lower block, and added native-shell detection so the settings copy reads `Update` / `Обновить` when opened from the Capacitor app. The landing page no longer places APK download beside the primary CTA; it now renders a quiet footer-adjacent client-only link and suppresses it entirely when the native bridge / Capacitor shell is present. Focused verification: landing and Assistant Settings tests, web typecheck, `ReadLints` on touched web files.

- **Soft-detached web-chat turns are recoverable after passive post-header disconnects, including silent/pre-start drops and long stale-history waits (`apps/web`; continuity hotfix 2026-04-30):** re-audited the stream lifecycle from a fresh baseline after the founder reported that switching away/back still stopped streams, streams sometimes vanished in-place until reload, and stale upper `Думаю...` cursors remained after background completion. Fresh `persai-dev` logs showed the relevant turns completing server-side, including one long `web_stream_timing totalRuntimeMs=153061` with `firstDeltaMs=151013`, while the client was also seeing occasional unauthenticated turn-status probes (`userId=null`, `401`) and many successful `/messages?limit=20` refreshes. Root cause: the client still had two destructive passive-disconnect exits even though the API contract says passive disconnects keep runtime turns alive until terminal history/status/event or explicit Stop: it could clear `activeTurnSnapshotsRef`, abort-controller state, and `markStreaming(false)` at the old soft-detach polling cap, and it could skip recovery entirely if the stream closed after 2xx headers but before `onStarted` supplied a `chatId`. `useChat` now keeps local active turns alive past the old 60 x 2s polling cap, backs off to a long interval instead of deleting the live snapshot, starts client-turn reattach recovery even when no `chatId` is known yet, and only treats reattach terminal callbacks as terminal after history actually reconciles. Added regressions for both classes: stale/older history beyond the former cap and post-header/pre-`onStarted` disconnect recovery by `clientTurnId`. Verification: fresh GKE API/runtime log correlation, `corepack pnpm --filter @persai/web exec vitest run app/app/_components/use-chat.test.tsx`, `ReadLints` on touched files.

- **Attachment/file turns now fail early on missing source objects and preserve produced artifacts on degraded terminal paths (`apps/api`, `apps/runtime`, `packages/runtime-contract`; systemic file pipeline fix 2026-04-30):** API now checks Telegram inbound and web staged/chat attachments against media object storage before handing refs to runtime, so a missing `storagePath` becomes deterministic `attachment_object_unavailable` instead of a late tool-side `No such object`. Runtime `failed` / `interrupted` stream events can carry already-produced `artifacts` / `fileRefs`, failed receipts persist that terminal payload, and Telegram/web native stream adapters return a degraded result with generic text when artifacts exist after follow-up failure. Added busy/in-flight and failed/interrupted lease-release observability. Focused verification: attachment availability test, Telegram degraded media adapter test, web-stream degraded media adapter test, `@persai/api` typecheck, `@persai/runtime` typecheck.

- **Live chat streams no longer disappear after switching away/back while history refresh returns `activeTurn: null` (`apps/web`; continuity hotfix 2026-04-30):** checked recent `persai-dev` API/runtime logs for the founder repro and confirmed turns were still accepted/running/completed server-side (`web_turn_attempt_completed`, `web_stream_timing`) while repeated `/messages?limit=20` refreshes returned `200`, so the regression was client reconciliation. `useChat` no longer treats `activeTurn: null` plus any older committed assistant message as permission to clear the current live turn. Cleanup now requires committed history to contain the result for the current active snapshot, and the optimistic committed-tail heuristic only applies while the active snapshot still has a local optimistic user id. This prevents older user+assistant history from being mistaken for the current turn after `onStarted` has already supplied the server user id. Added a regression for `activeTurn: null` with older assistant history while a stream remains live. The Android APK download surface was also reduced to a single quiet phone-icon link on the landing page and assistant settings, removing title/body/version text and the download icon. Verification: GKE API/runtime log check, `corepack pnpm --filter @persai/web test -- app/app/_components/use-chat.test.tsx app/page.test.tsx app/app/_components/assistant-settings.test.tsx`, `corepack pnpm -r --if-present run lint`, `corepack pnpm run format:check`, `corepack pnpm --filter @persai/web run typecheck`, `corepack pnpm --filter @persai/api run typecheck`, `ReadLints` on touched web files.

- **Background-completed turns now clear stale `Думаю...` active placeholders from committed history (`apps/web`; continuity hotfix 2026-04-30):** checked recent `persai-dev` logs for the founder repro; API/runtime showed the turn completing server-side (`web_turn_attempt_completed`, `web_stream_timing`, with one long turn around 95s) rather than a backend stream failure, and a background turn-status probe returned 401, so cleanup cannot depend only on reattach/status. `useChat` now treats authoritative history with `activeTurn: null` or a stale activeTurn whose result is already committed as sufficient to clear local active state even if the browser still has `activeThreads`/AbortController state after backgrounding. Transient streaming cleanup now covers both `local-assistant-*` and server-projected `active-assistant-*` placeholders, preventing committed final history from coexisting with an upper empty `Думаю...` bubble. - **Live reattached long streams keep rendering after switching back before completion (`apps/web`; continuity hotfix 2026-04-30):** fixed the remaining founder repro where a long answer in Chat A could briefly resume after switching away/back, then disappear until final completion. The client bug was in `useChat`'s running reattach status path: a server `assistantMessage` from turn status was converted through the committed-message mapper, so later live `onDelta` callbacks skipped it because they only append to `status === "streaming"` assistant bubbles. Reattached running assistant bubbles now stay `streaming`, keep the longest currently known content, and continue accepting deltas after status refresh. Focused regression restores `persai.active-web-turn.v1.thread-A`, applies a running reattach status with an assistant message, and verifies the next delta appends to the same still-streaming bubble. - **Android app download banners now point at an auto-exported release manifest (`apps/web`, `persai-mobile`; mobile release surface 2026-04-30):** the landing page and assistant settings now show a subdued PersAI Android APK banner with visible version/build metadata. - **Image generate/edit now use bounded flexible worker timeouts instead of the shared 90s gateway default (`apps/runtime`, `apps/provider-gateway`, `packages/runtime-contract`; timeout hotfix 2026-04-30):** runtime image tools now resolve `timeoutMs` from the published bundle worker-tool config with a `180000ms` default, send it through the provider-gateway request body, and use it for the runtime fetch abort window. Provider-gateway normalizes the value and OpenAI image generate/edit now use a bounded image abort window: at least the shared gateway timeout, default `180000ms`, capped at `240000ms`. Video remains on its existing `300000ms` path. Focused verification: `corepack pnpm --filter @persai/runtime test -- --runTestsByPath apps/runtime/test/provider-gateway.client.service.test.ts apps/runtime/test/turn-execution.service.test.ts`, `corepack pnpm --filter @persai/provider-gateway test -- --runTestsByPath apps/provider-gateway/test/provider-image-generation.service.test.ts apps/provider-gateway/test/openai-provider.client.test.ts`, `corepack pnpm --filter @persai/runtime run typecheck`, `corepack pnpm --filter @persai/provider-gateway run typecheck`.

- **Failed/interrupted image/tool turns no longer leave a duplicate empty `Думаю...` bubble above the real failed reply (`apps/web`; continuity/UI hotfix 2026-04-30):** founder showed the concrete screenshot case where the lower assistant message already contained text (`Попытка не прошла...`), but a separate empty local streaming placeholder remained above it. The fix is not based on “no text”; failed/interrupted handlers in `useChat` now remove any other empty optimistic local assistant placeholders in the same thread when applying the terminal failed/partial assistant message. A textless interrupted result is also forced out of `streaming` as a guardrail. Focused verification: `corepack pnpm --filter @persai/web exec vitest run app/app/_components/use-chat.test.tsx`, `corepack pnpm --filter @persai/web run typecheck`.

- **Switched-away long streams now refresh reattach completion against the correct chat (`apps/web`; continuity hotfix 2026-04-30):** founder clarified that the remaining regression was not only post-completion cleanup, but the older “long stream stops after switching chats” path. API logs still showed `web_turn_attempt_completed` / `web_stream_timing`, so the server was not killing the turn. The client bug was in `useChat`'s reattach path: terminal callbacks inside `startTurnReattach()` called `refreshLatestHistory(targetThreadKey)` even though that function expects a `chatId`, so a switched-away thread could finish reattach without fetching its own authoritative chat history. Reattach terminal callbacks now resolve the originating thread's known `chatId` first and refresh history against that chat while preserving the thread key. Focused verification: `corepack pnpm --filter @persai/web exec vitest run app/app/_components/use-chat.test.tsx`, `corepack pnpm --filter @persai/web run typecheck`.

- **Background-completed turns no longer leave a stale `Думаю...` cursor above the final answer (`apps/web`; continuity hotfix 2026-04-29):** fixed the remaining resume bug where a turn could finish while the browser/app was backgrounded, then return with both the committed assistant reply and a stale local thinking placeholder still visible until reload. The root cause was an in-memory reconcile gap in `useChat`: if passive disconnect happened before `onStarted` remapped the optimistic user id, history merge/reconcile could keep the orphan local placeholder even after the committed server user+assistant pair was already present. `mergeCommittedHistoryWithActiveTurn()` and `refreshLatestHistory()` now treat an exact new committed tail (`1 new user + 1 new assistant`, ending in assistant) as authoritative enough to replace the optimistic local snapshot and let the detached-turn finalizer clear `isStreaming`. Focused verification: `corepack pnpm --filter @persai/web exec vitest run app/app/_components/use-chat.test.tsx`, `corepack pnpm --filter @persai/web run typecheck`.

- **Chat switch no longer reconciles a detached stream against the wrong chat (`apps/web`; continuity hotfix 2026-04-29):** founder reported that switching away from an in-flight chat could make the earlier stream look interrupted again. Live `persai-dev` API logs showed the turns were still reaching `web_turn_attempt_completed` / `web_stream_timing` without `client-aborted`, so the regression was client-side. `useChat`'s passive-disconnect path had been starting soft-detach reconciliation for `thread-A` with the global `activeChatIdRef.current`, which already pointed at the newly opened `chat-B`; the follow-up history refresh therefore targeted the wrong chat after a thread switch. `apps/web/app/app/_components/use-chat.ts` now resolves the originating thread's own known `chatId` from its active/cached snapshot before starting reconciliation (and reuses the same resolver for off-thread post-completion compaction refresh). Focused verification: `corepack pnpm --filter @persai/web exec vitest run app/app/_components/use-chat.test.tsx`, `corepack pnpm --filter @persai/web run typecheck`.

- **Native mobile media share for image lightbox (`apps/web`, `persai-mobile`; mobile shell reliability 2026-04-29):** the chat image lightbox no longer relies on `navigator.share(...)` inside the Capacitor WebView when the shell can do better. `apps/web` now prefers `window.PersaiNative.shareMedia(...)` for lightbox share actions, passing the authenticated media URL plus filename/user-agent metadata. Android extends the existing `PersaiNative` JS interface so the shell downloads the file with the WebView cookie into cache and launches the system `ACTION_SEND` chooser via the existing `FileProvider`; iOS injects the same bridge from `AppDelegate.swift`, reuses the WKWebView cookie store, writes the file into temporary cache, and presents `UIActivityViewController`. Browser web keeps the previous Web Share/download fallback. Focused verification: `image-lightbox` regression test, web typecheck, workspace lint, API typecheck, Android debug APK build with Android Studio JBR.

- **ADR consolidation 2026-04-29 (`docs/ADR/072`..`077`, `docs/ADR/078-consolidated-follow-through-program.md`, source-of-truth docs):** ADR-072 through ADR-077 are now archived historical ADRs rather than active execution programs. `Step 15a` was cancelled instead of being left deferred. The only active continuation backlog now lives in `docs/ADR/078-consolidated-follow-through-program.md`, which keeps only genuinely open follow-through grouped into mobile shell reliability/rollout, remaining runtime/tool efficiency work (`R2 -> R3`), background-task verification/test cleanup, and long-tail deferred research. Source-of-truth repo docs were repointed so new sessions no longer treat ADR-073 as the live program.

- **Final chat continuity now has server-owned active-turn projection and SSE reattach (`apps/api`, `apps/web`, contracts; final chat 2026-04-29):** web chat list/bootstrap rows now carry a compact `activeTurn`, message history responses return full `activeTurn` beside committed messages, and the web client renders committed history plus the server-projected active turn instead of treating local cache/session storage as primary truth. A new `GET /api/v1/assistant/chat/web/turns/:clientTurnId/stream` reattach SSE route lets resume/switch flows reconnect to running turns without adding a blocking request to the normal first-send stream path. Focused verification: regenerated contracts, `use-chat`/chat continuity regression suite, API/web typechecks.

- **Chat switch cache now validates against server history instead of hiding new messages (`apps/web`; chat switch cache correction 2026-04-29):** fixed the ordinary chat-switch path where returning to a cached thread could skip `loadHistory()` because the hook already held the same `chatId`, or `loadHistory()` could stop at the local per-thread cache. The cache is now only an instant preview: `ChatPage` still asks `useChat.loadHistory()` for existing chats, and `loadHistory()` displays cached messages while continuing to fetch and merge latest server history. New messages no longer stay hidden until F5. Focused verification: `use-chat` regression suite, `chat/page` regression test, web typecheck, format check.

- **History load no longer wipes restored active tool UI after reload (`apps/web`; active history merge correction 2026-04-29):** fixed the later-reload race where turn status correctly restored a running tool placeholder/cursor, but the normal chat history load for the same thread arrived afterward and replaced visible messages with committed history that did not yet include the in-flight assistant placeholder. `loadHistory()` now merges committed history with any active turn snapshot and keeps the active snapshot/cache aligned, so cursor/tool status stays visible until the tool finishes. Focused verification: `use-chat` regression suite and web typecheck.

- **Active turn reload restore now retries before focus changes (`apps/web`; reload continuity correction 2026-04-29):** fixed the early-reload race where the first `/assistant/chat/web/turns/{clientTurnId}` lookup could return `unknown` or `accepted` before the API had marked the web turn `running`, causing the cursor/tool status to stay gone until a later focus event retriggered reconciliation. Stored active turn restore now performs a bounded retry loop after reload until the server exposes a running/terminal turn, then restores the live cursor/tool status or committed result. Focused verification: `use-chat` regression suite and web typecheck.

- **Completed active-turn results now refresh the per-thread chat cache (`apps/web`; cache correction 2026-04-29):** fixed the post-reload/resume path where a completed turn-status result could appear in the visible chat but not update `cachedThreadHistorySnapshotsRef`, so switching to another chat and back restored a stale cached thread without the newest assistant result. Terminal turn-status reconciliation now writes the committed user+assistant messages into the per-thread cache before clearing active state. Focused verification: `use-chat` regression suite and web typecheck.

- **Active web-chat tool status now survives reload/resume without historical badges (`apps/api`, `apps/web`; current-turn activity 2026-04-29):** `assistant_web_chat_turn_attempts` now carries a bounded `currentActivity` projection for active turns only, updated from native runtime tool lifecycle events and cleared on completed/failed/interrupted terminal states. The existing `/assistant/chat/web/turns/{clientTurnId}` status response exposes that live activity so desktop web and Capacitor can restore the current turn's working/tool badge after focus changes or full reload using the stored active `clientTurnId`, while committed chat history still renders without fabricated tool badges. Focused verification: `use-chat` regression suite, `web-chat-turn-attempt` service test, API/web typechecks.

- **Chat history no longer fabricates media tool badges from attachments (`apps/web`; tool activity correction 2026-04-29):** removed the attachment-derived `Image ready` / `Video ready` / `Voice ready` reconstruction that made completed historical media messages look like they still carried tool status. Tool activity remains a current-turn/live UI state only; loaded chat history now renders committed messages and attachments without manufacturing historical tool badges. Focused verification: `use-chat` regression test and web typecheck.

- **Offline fallback now covers Capacitor cold-start assets and guarded mid-session navigation (`persai-mobile`, `apps/web`; offline fallback 2026-04-29):** Capacitor Android assets were regenerated so the generated `capacitor.config.json` contains `server.errorPath: "offline.html"` plus the WebView background color, and `www/offline.html` is bundled into `android/app/src/main/assets/public/offline.html`. The static retry action now explicitly navigates back to `https://persai.dev` instead of risking a reload loop on the local error page. Web mid-session offline checks now share `/api/health` verification across hook instances, and sidebar-owned app navigations are guarded so stale `navigator.onLine=true` keeps the current screen mounted and opens `OfflineGate` instead of routing into a blank/error WebView. Focused verification: Capacitor sync/asset inspection, Android debug APK build with Android Studio JBR, sidebar offline navigation regression test, web typecheck, targeted prettier/lints.

- **Web chat resume keeps an in-flight tool turn visibly active after passive window/app aborts (`apps/web`; tool UI continuity 2026-04-29):** post-headers passive disconnects are no longer treated as ordinary stream completion when the user did not press Stop, so the blinking cursor/working state stays active while the bounded history reconciliation loop polls for the committed tool result. Tool status remains live/current-turn UI state rather than historical message state. Focused verification: `use-chat` regression test, web typecheck, targeted prettier, lints.

- **Tool-turn resume reconciliation now polls past the first stale history read (`apps/web`; desktop/mobile image-tool resume race 2026-04-29):** when a browser tab or Capacitor app returns while an image/tool turn is still running, `useChat` no longer relies on a single resume `getChatMessages` call. If committed assistant history is not visible yet but the thread still has an active stream/snapshot/controller, it starts the existing bounded soft-detach reconciliation loop and keeps polling until the committed assistant message and attachment replace the local placeholders. Successful reconciliation now uses the shared detached-turn finalizer, aborting only the stale local controller without calling the server hard-stop endpoint. Focused verification: `use-chat` regression test, web typecheck, targeted prettier, lints.

- **Runtime Admin OpenAI key now wins over static provider-gateway env keys (`apps/provider-gateway`; GKE runtime-admin key path 2026-04-29):** live `persai-dev` checks showed Runtime Admin saves were persisting correctly to encrypted DB storage and both `openai/api-key` / `anthropic/api-key` resolved through the internal secret resolver, but `provider-gateway` skipped managed resolution for OpenAI whenever `PROVIDER_GATEWAY_OPENAI_API_KEY` existed in Kubernetes env. Provider warmup now resolves PersAI-managed provider keys whenever the internal API is configured and uses that value as the SDK warmup key, leaving static env keys only as bootstrap fallback when no managed secret is configured. Focused verification: provider-gateway warmup regression test, provider-gateway typecheck, lints.

- **Web attachment staging no longer blocks the follow-up stream (`apps/api`; GKE regression 2026-04-27):** live `persai-dev` logs showed image/file sends reaching `POST /api/v1/assistant/chat/web/stage-attachment` with `201`, but staging also created `web_turn_attempt_accepted`; the subsequent `POST /api/v1/assistant/chat/web/stream` with the same `clientTurnId` was treated as `web_turn_attempt_duplicate_inflight status=accepted` and returned `409`. Staged uploads now keep `clientTurnId` / `clientAttachmentId` ownership on the attachment only; the logical turn attempt is claimed by the actual send/stream request, so attachments can be merged into the user message without blocking the turn. Focused verification: API media staging test, stream web-turn test, API typecheck.

- **Web chat send reliability (`apps/web`, `apps/api`, contracts, Prisma):** web/Capacitor sends now reuse a stable `clientTurnId` on retry, stage uploads with durable `clientAttachmentId`s, merge staged attachments by `clientTurnId` ownership, and persist logical web-turn attempts in `assistant_web_chat_turn_attempts`. A new `GET /api/v1/assistant/chat/web/turns/:clientTurnId` status endpoint lets the client reconcile ambiguous network outcomes before retrying, preventing duplicate turns/uploads when the server already accepted or completed the send. Focused verification: web `use-chat`/`chat-message` tests, API staging/merge/send/stream tests, API/web typecheck, Prisma and contract generation.

- **Mobile unlock image-turn stale streaming cleanup (`apps/web`; focused regression/typecheck green):** resume history reconciliation now clears a per-thread streaming flag when the server history already contains a committed assistant message for the optimistic turn, covering mobile WebView/screen-lock cases where the generated image appears after unlock but the local SSE/fetch transport remains pending forever and leaves the composer showing `Stop`. The cleanup aborts only the stale local controller and does not call the hard-stop endpoint, so completed soft-detached turns are not killed. Focused verification: `corepack pnpm --filter @persai/web exec vitest run app/app/_components/use-chat.test.tsx`, `corepack pnpm --filter @persai/web run typecheck`, targeted prettier check.

- **One-screen gateway + human activity labels (founder UI polish 2026-04-25: reduce noise on the public entry screen and replace raw tool labels like `knowledge_search_finished`; `apps/web`):** the public unauthenticated home page is now a compact one-screen product gateway rather than a scrollable sales landing: clearer context-memory positioning, quieter capability pills, primary free-start CTA, secondary plans CTA, sign-in link, and footer links for plans, terms, privacy, contacts, and company details. Chat activity badges now humanize and localize known tool/runtime lifecycle labels in RU/EN (`Ищу в интернете`, `Поиск в знаниях завершён`, `Ответ готов`, etc.) and defensively fall back to neutral user-facing labels for unknown tool events instead of leaking snake_case.
