Focused verification green: activity-badge vitest coverage, web typecheck, lints, and prettier check on touched files.
  - Follow-up: added explicit `files` tool lifecycle labels (`Работаю с файлами`, `Файл готов`, `Файл создан`, etc.) so file-tool activity does not fall through to generic labels.

- **Desktop chat surface polish (founder UI polish 2026-04-25: desktop attachment menu should only show File, chat title was too heavy, and desktop voice recording should match mobile calm style; `apps/web`):** desktop web attachment popover now renders only the `File` tile, while touch/mobile keeps Camera / Gallery / File with the live camera preview. The chat header title is now quieter single-line context (`text-sm`, medium weight, muted tone) instead of competing with the conversation. Desktop voice recording keeps the same click-to-record logic and `Cancel` / `Send` actions, but now uses the calmer mobile-like recording card with a mic pulse, monospaced timer, and rounded action pills. Focused verification green: chat-input + chat-area vitest coverage, web typecheck, lints, and prettier check on touched files.

- **Chat voice retry guidance + scroll-to-latest button (founder UI polish 2026-04-25: empty voice recognition should ask to repeat, and chat needs a calm button down when reading older messages; `apps/web`):** empty/undetected voice transcription now maps to a dedicated `voice_transcription_empty` UX issue and renders localized RU/EN copy asking the user to repeat the voice message instead of showing the generic/raw failure. The chat view now shows a quiet floating “Back to latest” / “К последним” button once the user scrolls away from the bottom; it works on mobile and desktop and keeps streaming auto-follow unchanged while the user stays near the latest message. Product guidance remains: Android chat history should load older messages at the top rather than using pull-to-refresh, because pull gestures conflict with reading history and WebView refresh. Focused verification green: chat-area + API-client vitest coverage, web typecheck, lints, and prettier check on touched files.

- **Mobile voice short-tap race fix (founder live repro 2026-04-25: short tap on the mobile mic left the recording banner/timer stuck and later attempts produced transcription errors; `apps/web`):** mobile hold-to-record now invalidates any pending `getUserMedia` start when the user releases/cancels before the recorder is ready. Late audio streams from a short tap are stopped immediately, `MediaRecorder` is not created, and no corrupted/unsupported short audio blob is uploaded. GKE logs around the repro showed failed `/api/v1/assistant/voice/transcribe` requests with provider-gateway `400 Audio file might be corrupted or unsupported`, matching the client-side race. Focused verification green: `chat-input` regression coverage for short-tap cancellation, web typecheck, lints, and prettier check on touched files.

- **Mobile camera attachment preview (founder mobile polish 2026-04-25: paperclip menu should show a Telegram-style live camera preview in the first tile; `apps/web`):** the chat attachment popover now starts a mobile/touch-only rear-camera `getUserMedia` preview while the menu is open and renders it inside the Camera tile. The stream is stopped as soon as the menu closes/unmounts, and denied/unavailable camera access falls back to the existing icon tile. The camera tile still opens the existing capture picker on tap, so attachment semantics are unchanged. Focused verification green: `chat-input` vitest coverage, web typecheck, lints, and prettier check on touched files.

- **Avatar center crop + image lightbox actions (founder live polish 2026-04-25: tall avatar saved top-heavy, image lightbox needed save/share; `apps/api` + `apps/web`):** assistant avatar normalization now uses stable center crop instead of `sharp` attention crop, so tall portraits keep the middle of the frame rather than biasing upward. The chat image lightbox now has a compact glass action bar with “save to gallery”, “share”, and close actions; share prefers Web Share file sharing, falls back to URL sharing, then falls back to download. Image attachments now pass download URL + filename into the lightbox, and RU/EN labels were added. Focused verification green: avatar center-crop test, lightbox/chat-message tests, API typecheck, and web typecheck.

- **Soft-detach passive stream disconnect polish (founder live repro 2026-04-25: phone screen lock during image generation / long answer briefly showed an error, but manual refresh revealed the image had committed; `apps/web`):** fresh GKE logs showed runtime kept processing after the phone slept and API later served the committed history/attachment with `200`, so server-side Slice 1.2 soft-detach was working. The remaining bug was client-side: after stream headers were accepted, a passive WebView/SSE/fetch disconnect without terminal event was still treated as a real stream failure and surfaced `issue`. `useChat` now classifies post-headers passive disconnects as soft-detach when the local controller was not explicitly aborted by `stop()`, keeps the UI quiet, leaves the originating thread marked streaming, and polls latest history until committed server messages replace the optimistic local bubbles. Once reconciled, it clears the active snapshot and releases the per-turn abort entry. Focused verification green: `use-chat` regression now covers quiet post-headers disconnect + history reconciliation with generated attachment, and web typecheck passes.

- **Live turn return-state polish (founder UX repro 2026-04-25: long stream/tool/image generation continues in background after switching chats, but returning before completion showed no typing cursor/tool banner and often required reload; `apps/web`):** `useChat` now keeps a per-`threadKey` in-memory live turn snapshot for active streams, not just the old `threadKey -> isStreaming` flag. When the user returns to a still-streaming thread, the local user bubble, assistant streaming placeholder, live tool/compaction/runtime activity, chat id, and streaming text/thought state are restored immediately instead of rendering an empty pane. Snapshots are cleared once the turn leaves the active streaming set, so completed turns fall back to normal persisted history. Focused verification green: `use-chat` regression suite now covers switching away during `image_generate` and returning to see the `Generating image` activity without reload, plus web typecheck and ESLint on touched files.

- **Clerk avatar same-origin proxy (founder follow-up 2026-04-25: “аватарка clerk так и не работает”; `apps/web`):** the previous cache-busting/retry hook still rendered Clerk's remote `user.imageUrl` directly, so Capacitor WebView / remote CDN failures could still drop the sidebar/profile avatar to initials. `apps/web` now exposes authenticated `GET /api/clerk-avatar`, resolves the current Clerk user server-side, fetches the Clerk image server-side, validates that the upstream response is an image, and streams it back as a same-origin private response. `useClerkAvatar()` now returns `/api/clerk-avatar?v=...` and bumps the version after `user.reload()` resolves, so a refreshed Clerk profile can repaint immediately without relying on direct `img.clerk.com` rendering. Focused verification green: hook + route vitest coverage, web typecheck, and ESLint on touched files.

- **Telegram owner-claim live fix (founder live repro 2026-04-25: connected bot showed `claim_required`, but sending the code did not complete binding; `apps/api` + `apps/web`):** GKE showed healthy `persai-dev` API/web pods and ingress, but no `/telegram-webhook` traffic around the failed attempt. Root cause: `ConnectTelegramIntegrationService` verified the bot token with `getMe` and persisted the binding, but never called Telegram `setWebhook`, so new bots had no delivery route into PersAI. Connect now registers `setWebhook` to `TELEGRAM_WEBHOOK_BASE_URL/telegram-webhook/<assistantId>` with the HMAC-derived `secret_token` already enforced by the webhook controller and `allowed_updates: ["message"]`. The webhook owner-claim parser now accepts manually typed codes with spaces/hyphens. The Telegram settings UI opens BotFather and the bot via top-level `t.me` navigation for the Capacitor WebView, removes duplicate/resend wording from the "How it works" help, tightens code display, and keeps the claim card calmer. Focused verification green: Telegram integration connect test, Telegram webhook proxy test, API/web typechecks, and ESLint on touched files.

- **Limits & Plan display polish (founder ask 2026-04-25: show only real numeric limits, not every unlimited tool; RU/EN human-readable labels; `apps/web`):** Assistant Settings → Limits & Plan now filters quota buckets and tool daily limits to capped entries only (`limit !== null` / `dailyCallLimit !== null`), so unlimited `∞` tools no longer fill the panel. Known tool codes now render localized product labels instead of raw API display names: browser, code execution, files, image/video generation, knowledge read/search, scheduled actions, shell, TTS, web fetch, and web search. No API/data-model/policy change. Focused verification green: Assistant Settings vitest suite, web typecheck, web lint, and prettier check on touched files.

- **Telegram / Knowledge settings polish (founder ask 2026-04-25: Telegram and Knowledge panels were wider than Assistant Settings; Channels row should open TG settings; owner-claim flow should be clear and premium on mobile; `apps/web`):** Telegram and Knowledge document slide-overs now use the same `narrow` panel width as the main Assistant Settings surface. Assistant Settings → Channels now treats the Telegram row as an interactive settings link with a chevron, while WhatsApp/MAX remain coming-soon rows. The Telegram owner-claim card was simplified into a calmer two-step mobile-friendly flow: open the bot, send the displayed code, with a larger claim code, full-width copy action on mobile, and a primary "Find bot" action. No backend/API/data-model change. Focused verification green: Assistant Settings vitest suite, web typecheck, web lint, and prettier check on touched files.

- **Soft-detach browser resume reconciliation (founder live repro 2026-04-25: after phone lock / tab background the UI showed an error, but refresh revealed generated images had committed; `apps/web`):** `useChat` now runs a debounced latest-history reconciliation on `focus`, `pageshow`, and `visibilitychange` back to visible. The refresh bypasses the existing one-shot `loadHistory` guard, replaces optimistic `local-*` user/assistant bubbles with committed server messages, merges server attachments, clears stale issue state after a successful reconciliation, and keeps `activeChatIdRef` current as soon as stream `onStarted` returns a chat id. This closes the practical UX gap where soft-detached image/tool turns completed server-side but required a manual page reload to appear. It is not a full in-flight SSE reattach; live deltas during the detached window remain a future enhancement.

- **Admin-managed media model catalog (founder ask 2026-04-25: image generate/edit were hardcoded while video had a selector; `apps/api` + `apps/web` + `apps/runtime` + `apps/provider-gateway` + contracts):** runtime provider settings now store a capability-aware model catalog in `platform_runtime_provider_settings.available_model_catalog_by_provider` (`CHAT / IMAGE / VIDEO` per provider) while preserving the existing `availableModelsByProvider` chat alias for text routing/provider warmup. `Admin > Runtime` now renders three textarea sections per provider. `Admin > Plans` now exposes plan-level selectors for `imageGenerateModelKey`, `imageEditModelKey`, and catalog-driven `videoGenerateModelKey` instead of the old hardcoded Sora enum. Materialization writes those selections into runtime `toolCredentialRefs.modelKey`; runtime sends the selected image/video model to provider-gateway; OpenAI image generate/edit now use the selected model instead of the hardcoded `gpt-image-1`. OpenAPI + generated contracts and Prisma client were regenerated. Full commit gate green: lint, format, API/web/runtime/provider-gateway typecheck, recursive workspace tests, and focused media-model tests.

- **Provider-gateway managed text-provider keys (founder live GKE repro 2026-04-25: Anthropic selected in admin settings but chat returned `runtime_unreachable`; `apps/provider-gateway`):** text-generation warmup now bridges the admin runtime-provider secret store and provider-gateway. `ProviderWarmupService` still uses static `PROVIDER_GATEWAY_OPENAI_API_KEY` / `PROVIDER_GATEWAY_ANTHROPIC_API_KEY` env vars when present, but if an env key is absent it resolves `openai/api-key` or `anthropic/api-key` through the existing PersAI internal secret resolver before marking the provider `unconfigured`. `OpenAIProviderClient.warm(...)` and `AnthropicProviderClient.warm(...)` now accept the resolved key override, so an Anthropic key saved through the admin surface can warm the SDK client without also creating a Kubernetes env var. Focused coverage in `apps/provider-gateway/test/provider-warmup.service.test.ts` pins the exact failure shape: no Anthropic env key, internal API configured, `anthropic/api-key` resolves from PersAI, and `ensureReadyForRequest` returns ready for `claude-opus-4-7`.

- **Chat image attachment normalization (founder ask 2026-04-25 «при отправке фото и картинок в чат их можно оптимизировать»; `apps/api` only; verification gate green: workspace lint clean, prettier clean, api+web typecheck clean, all workspace tests green incl. 5 new image cases in `apps/api/test/media-preprocessor.service.test.ts`):** `MediaPreprocessorService.processImage` in `apps/api/src/modules/workspace-management/application/media/media-preprocessor.service.ts` was rewritten on top of the existing sharp pipeline so every chat image attachment that flows through `InboundMediaService.resolve` (web chat, Telegram, WhatsApp, VK) lands in storage already vision-friendly: `.rotate()` first applies the EXIF orientation tag (iPhone portrait photos previously stored sideways because the orientation header was respected by phone galleries but not by `<img>` in the browser nor by OpenAI vision), then `.resize(2048, 2048, { fit: "inside", withoutEnlargement: true })` always runs (was: only on >2048 inputs), then JPEG/HEIC/HEIF outputs go through `.jpeg({ quality: 85, mozjpeg: true })` (was: 90 on HEIC, pass-through on JPEG) — same trade-off the avatar pipeline uses, indistinguishable from the source for vision/edit tools at ~30% smaller bytes. PNG and WEBP keep their format so transparency / lossless guarantees survive but still flow through rotation+resize. GIF is now an explicit short-circuit (returns the original buffer untouched) so animated GIFs do not collapse to a first-frame still — sharp's default behavior without `{ animated: true }` would have lost animation. Output dimensions now come from the post-rotation `info.width/height` returned by `pipeline.toBuffer({ resolveWithObject: true })`, fixing a latent bug where pre-rotation metadata was persisted for orientation-6/7 photos. The 2048 cap matches OpenAI vision's internal tile pipeline (anything larger is rescaled at their cost) and stays above `gpt-image-1`'s 1536×1024 edit ceiling so a single normalized asset serves both vision-analyze and image-edit code paths without further downscaling. New tests cover: oversized 4000×3000 JPEG → 2048×1536 JPEG with smaller bytes; portrait JPEG with EXIF orientation 6 → output dimensions swapped (100→200) + orientation tag stripped from output; 320×240 PNG with alpha → format preserved + 4-channel alpha intact; minimal single-frame GIF → buffer reference-equal pass-through; 800×600 high-quality JPEG → re-encoded smaller at q85 (proves rotation+quality always lands even when no resize is needed). Risks/residuals: re-encoding a small JPEG that had no quality issue costs ~30–80ms CPU per image on Node; acceptable trade-off in exchange for guaranteed orientation correctness. Animated WEBP collapses to a still (sharp limitation; very rare in chat — accept). Storage rewrite of pre-existing oversized images is out-of-scope (only forward uploads); historical attachments stay as-is. Next recommended slice: admin-managed image/video model catalog (three textareas per provider for CHAT / IMAGE / VIDEO + plan-level `imageGenerateModelKey` / `imageEditModelKey` selectors mirroring the existing `videoGenerateModelKey`).

- **Post-ADR-076 hotfix wave (avatar pipeline hardening + Clerk default-avatar resilience; founder asks 2026-04-25 «Аватарка ломается часто» / «иногда загружается но не отображается» / «в TG-бот имя меняется при смене а аватарка нет» / «проблема с аватаркой Clerk не работает или работает через раз»; `apps/api` + `apps/web`; verification gate green: lint clean, format clean, api+web+runtime+provider-gateway typecheck clean, all workspace tests green):** four founder-reported regressions on the avatar surface fixed in one bundle. (1) `validateAvatarUrl` in `apps/api/src/modules/workspace-management/application/update-assistant-draft.service.ts` now matches `^/api/avatar/[a-f0-9]{8,64}(?:\.[a-z0-9]{2,8})?$` first and falls through to the existing `https://` branch — Slice 076 writes content-addressed `/api/avatar/<hash>.<ext>` paths and the validator was rejecting its own output with «`avatarUrl must use the https:// scheme.`». Insecure schemes (`javascript:`, `http:`) still rejected. (2) `apps/api/src/modules/workspace-management/interface/http/assistant.controller.ts` raises the avatar `FileInterceptor` cap from 2 MB to 12 MB and `apps/api/src/modules/workspace-management/application/manage-assistant-avatar.service.ts` adds `normalizeAvatarBuffer(buffer, mimeType)` that lazy-loads `sharp` and pipes through `.rotate()` (EXIF) → `.resize(1024, 1024, { fit: "cover", position: "attention", withoutEnlargement: false })` → `.jpeg({ quality: 85, mozjpeg: true })`. The normalised buffer is what we hash, persist, and hand to Telegram, so HEIC/HEIF iPhone uploads now display in browsers and the Telegram bot photo path always has a JPEG it can accept. `buildAssistantAvatarUrl(buffer)` is now a single-argument helper because the output extension is fixed at `.jpg`. `apps/api/package.json` pins `sharp: "^0.34.5"` explicitly (no longer transitive). (3) `apps/api/src/modules/workspace-management/application/telegram-bot.client.service.ts` — `setBotProfilePhoto` rebuilds the multipart envelope to match Telegram Bot API 9.x: `photo` is JSON-encoded `InputProfilePhotoStatic` (`{"type":"static","photo":"attach://profile_photo_file"}`) and the actual JPEG bytes attach as a separate multipart field named `profile_photo_file`. Bot avatar now updates when the assistant draft updates, matching name-update behavior. (4) `apps/api/src/modules/identity-access/identity-access.module.ts` — `IdentityAccessModule.configure(...)` adds `{ path: "api/v1/assistant/avatar/:hash", method: RequestMethod.GET }` to the `ClerkAuthMiddleware` allowlist; previously the parameterised route hit Nest's auth-less default branch and `userId` resolved to `null` (visible in GKE logs as 401s on `GET /api/v1/assistant/avatar/<hash>.jpg`). (5) New web-side resilience hook `apps/web/app/app/_components/use-clerk-avatar.ts` — fires one `user.reload()` per browser session (gated by `sessionStorage["persai-clerk-user-reloaded"]`, `Promise.resolve(user.reload?.())`-wrapped so vi.fn() returning `undefined` in unit tests doesn't throw), produces an `<img src>` URL with cache-buster `?v=<updatedAt>-<YYYY-MM-DD>-<attempt>` (the day-bucket compresses the «dashboard avatar customisation visibility» window from per-device-24h to ≤1 day on every device), and exposes an `onError` handler that retries once with the bumped `attempt` before surfacing `broken=true` and falling back to initials (stops the «работает через раз» flicker on transient `img.clerk.com` errors). `apps/web/app/app/_components/sidebar.tsx` and `apps/web/app/app/profile/page.tsx` switched to the hook; both `<img>` tags now carry `referrerPolicy="no-referrer"` so the CDN sees no domain in the Referer header. The profile page keeps its local-blob preview path (`avatarPreviewUrl`) and only delegates to the hook when `user.hasImage === true`; the obsolete `avatarRefreshKey` counter is removed because `user.updatedAt` changes naturally on `user.reload()` after `user.setProfileImage()`. Tests: 4 new/updated unit suites (`apps/api/test/identity-access.module.test.ts`, `apps/api/test/manage-assistant-avatar.service.test.ts`, new `apps/api/test/telegram-bot-client.set-profile-photo.test.ts`, new `apps/api/test/update-assistant-draft.service.test.ts`) plus new vitest suite `apps/web/app/app/_components/use-clerk-avatar.test.tsx` (6 tests covering null user, day-bucketed buster, query-string preservation, single-retry-then-fallback, once-per-session reload, undefined-returning reload). Risks/residuals: `sharp` cold-start adds a one-time WASM init cost on first avatar upload after pod restart (lazy-loaded; no boot blocker); per-device 24h CDN cache cannot be bypassed without paying a fresh fetch on every render — day-bucket is the agreed trade-off, documented inline in `use-clerk-avatar.ts`; `sessionStorage` reload flag is per-tab, so multiple tabs of the same session each fire one (cheap, idempotent) `user.reload()`. Next recommended slices (founder-confirmed in same conversation, scoped separately): generalise the `sharp` pipeline into chat-attachment normalisation (2048 px long side, JPEG q85, EXIF rotate, HEIC→JPEG) so OpenAI vision (2048×2048 ceiling) and `gpt-image-1` edits (≤1536×1024 output) aren't wasted by oversized iPhone uploads; promote the Sora video registry pattern into an admin-managed catalog with three textareas per provider (CHAT / IMAGE / VIDEO) and plan-level `imageGenerateModelKey` / `imageEditModelKey` selectors mirroring `videoGenerateModelKey`.

- **Pre-prod polish 2026 — FIX 1 / Slice 1.2 (server-side soft-detach of the web-chat SSE turn; founder ask 2026-04-25 «План огонь — стартуй»; `apps/api` + `apps/web`; new architectural contract change to ADR-073 § 4a + `docs/API-BOUNDARY.md`; verification gate green: lint clean, format clean, api typecheck clean, web typecheck clean, registry tests 6/6, use-chat tests 20/20, assistant-api-client tests 31/31):** before this slice, the SSE controller in `apps/api/src/modules/workspace-management/interface/http/assistant.controller.ts` aborted the runtime turn on _any_ client disconnect — both `req.on("aborted")` and `res.on("close")` fed the same `clientAbortController.abort()`, and that controller was the runtime fetch's abort signal. So a phone screen lock mid-`image_generate`, a backgrounded tab, or a brief WiFi drop killed the turn server-side, the side-channel media tools dropped their results, and the persisted assistant message was a stub. On reopening the app the user saw a half-message with no image — the same class of bug Telegram never had because Telegram has no SSE socket coupled to runtime liveness. Slice 1.2 splits "explicit Stop" (hard abort) from "passive disconnect" (soft-detach): SSE socket close on the stream route now only flips a local `clientClosed` flag (suppresses further SSE writes) and never touches the runtime abort signal; explicit Stop is dispatched through a brand-new `POST /api/v1/assistant/chat/web/stop` endpoint that walks an in-memory `WebChatTurnHardStopRegistry` (process-local `Map<clientTurnId, {controller, userId, registeredAt}>`) to find the matching turn and call `controller.abort()`. The registry enforces userId match as defense-in-depth on top of the controller's normal auth, returns `false` (and the endpoint returns 204) on cross-user attempts and on misses so existence is not leaked. The web client now has `stopAssistantWebChatTurn(token, clientTurnId)` in `apps/web/app/app/assistant-api-client.ts` and `useChat.stop()` in `apps/web/app/app/_components/use-chat.ts` fires it as a fire-and-forget IIFE before locally aborting the controller — local abort is synchronous so the UI flips out of streaming immediately, and the POST is best-effort (errors swallowed; runtime falls through to the soft-detach path on failure, which is strictly safer than the pre-Slice-1.2 default). The per-thread abort map's value shape changed from `AbortController` to `{controller, clientTurnId}` so `stop()` can name the turn it's stopping; both registration sites (the normal `send` flow and the welcome-turn branch) updated. `streamToCompletion` is now passed `isClientAborted: () => clientAbortController.signal.aborted` instead of `() => clientClosed`, so the existing `client-aborted → persistInterruptedOutcome` path triggers on hard-stop only and a soft-detached turn walks through the regular full-message persistence path. The cooperation contract is now: `req.aborted` / `res.close` → soft-detach, runtime runs to completion, full message persisted, recoverable on next history fetch; `POST .../stop` with a registered `clientTurnId` → hard abort, partial message via existing path; `POST .../stop` with no match → idempotent 204, no-op. Files touched: new `web-chat-turn-hard-stop-registry.service.ts` (in-memory dispatcher with register/release/signalHardStop/hasForTesting); `assistant.controller.ts` (SSE handler refactor + new `stopWebChatTurn` route at `assistant/chat/web/stop`); `workspace-management.module.ts` (provider registration); `assistant-api-client.ts` (new `stopAssistantWebChatTurn` export with `ContractsApiError` mapping for non-2xx); `use-chat.ts` (abort-map shape change + `stop()` POST wiring + cleanup helpers updated to compare `entry.controller`); new tests `apps/api/test/web-chat-turn-hard-stop-registry.test.ts` (6 unit tests covering register/release/signalHardStop happy path, cross-user refusal, miss handling, rapid-retry replace semantics, and the soft-detach-decoupling invariant); 3 new tests in `apps/web/app/app/_components/use-chat.test.tsx` under "server-side soft-detach (slice 1.2)" pinning down "stop POSTs the in-flight clientTurnId before aborting the local controller", "does not POST stop when the user simply navigates away (soft-detach)", and "stop still aborts locally even if the hard-stop POST rejects"; 3 new tests in `apps/web/app/app/assistant-api-client.test.ts` covering the new client function's URL/headers/body, 204 success path, and ContractsApiError on non-2xx; `docs/API-BOUNDARY.md` web-chat section adds the hard-stop route and pins the soft-detach contract on the stream route; `docs/ADR/073-post-adr072-residue-and-polish-program.md` gains a new § 4a "Pre-prod polish 2026 — chat-turn lifecycle correctness wave" section that documents all four pre-prod fixes (1.1, 1.2, 2, 3) and records two known residuals (multi-replica registry routing; live-resume of in-flight stream after soft-detach) as deferred. Telegram parity is preserved (Telegram channel never had SSE-coupled liveness so no behavioral change there). Pre-prod polish 2026 wave is now complete (FIX 1.1 + 1.2 + 2 + 3 + 4); next bounded slice should re-enter the ADR-073 economics program (item 3 — provider-native cached-input-first prompt assembly is the highest-value remaining track).

- **Pre-prod polish 2026 — FIX 4 (sidebar SSR/CSR hydration mismatch crashed React in Capacitor WebView; founder ask 2026-04-25 «на мобилке так же ничего не изменилось — голос не работает»; debugging session via `adb logcat -s chromium`/`Capacitor/Console`; root-caused on production deploy `81afe34cba30791fab5874ecb4bdb40c1a1a9ad8`; web-only frontend fix; verification gate green: lint clean, format clean, web typecheck clean, web tests 125/125 passing):** before this slice, `apps/web/app/app/_components/sidebar.tsx` (a `"use client"` component that Next.js still SSR-renders for the initial HTML) called `groupChatsByDate(...)` and `formatChatRowTimestamp(iso, locale)` at render time. Both functions instantiate `new Date()` and use `Intl.DateTimeFormat` against the device's local timezone — so the GKE pod (UTC) and the user's device (Europe/Moscow, UTC+3) produced different timestamp strings («10:23» vs «13:23») and, on day boundaries, different group buckets (a chat at 23:30 МСК = 20:30 UTC lands in `today` on the device but in `yesterday` on the server). The mismatch threw a minified `Error #418` («Text content does not match server-rendered HTML») on every cold load — confirmed in logcat: `04-25 19:23:08.938 E Capacitor/Console: Uncaught Error: Minified React error #418; visit https://react.dev/errors/418` originating from a Next.js production chunk. In a desktop browser React swallows #418 with a single warning and silently re-renders the subtree client-only; in Capacitor's older WebView the recovery is brittle — freshly-mounted pointer event handlers (mic hold-to-record `pointerdown` / `pointermove` / `pointerup`, attachment menu `onClick`) routinely fail to attach to the post-recovery DOM nodes, so the user observed «hold microphone does literally nothing» despite the code being correctly deployed. **Fix.** Gate every date-aware render in `Sidebar` on a `mounted` flag (state already existed at line 137 for `AccountFooter`'s popup wiring, now also applied to the chat list). The SSR pass and the first client render both produce `<ChatListSkeleton />`, identical bytes; `useEffect(() => setMounted(true), [])` flips to `true` after hydration and the second client render produces the grouped list with timestamps — at that point timezone disagreement no longer matters because the server's render is already discarded and only the client's render is in the DOM. Specifically: (1) `chatGroups` becomes `mounted ? groupChatsByDate(...) : []` so `new Date()` doesn't run during SSR; (2) the chat-list render branch becomes `!mounted || data.isLoading || (data.isReloadingChats && chatGroups.length === 0) ? <ChatListSkeleton /> : ...` so neither group headers nor timestamps appear until after mount. `ChatListItem`'s `formatChatRowTimestamp(iso, locale)` call at line ~775 is reached only after mount because the entire `chatGroups.map(...)` subtree is gated. **Architecture decision.** A `mounted` gate is the standard React fix for client-only render branches that touch `Date`, `navigator`, `window`, `localStorage`, etc. Alternatives considered and rejected: (a) `Intl.DateTimeFormat(locale, { ..., timeZone: "UTC" })` — would unify the strings but display the wrong wall-clock time on the device; (b) `<span suppressHydrationWarning>` on the `<time>` element — fixes the warning but doesn't fix the structural mismatch from `groupChatsByDate` (different number of `<section>` headers when the day boundary is crossed); (c) `dynamic(() => import("./sidebar"), { ssr: false })` — would eliminate SSR for the entire sidebar including avatar / assistant card / footer, producing visible FOUC during navigation. The `mounted` gate gives a one-frame skeleton flash (~16ms) only on cold load and zero flash on subsequent navigations within the SPA. **Why this also unblocks hold-to-record voice messages and attachment-menu touches on Capacitor.** Without #418 firing on every load, React's effect/handler attachment runs once cleanly against the SSR DOM rather than running again against the post-recovery DOM with stale handler closures; the `pointerdown` listener on the mic button registers on the first try, the `useTouchDevice()` hook's `useEffect`-driven media query subscribes correctly, and the floating-overlay `<AnimatePresence>` renders without losing its mounted-vs-pre-mount race. **Files touched.** `apps/web/app/app/_components/sidebar.tsx` (only — two surgical edits: `chatGroups` ternary on `mounted`, chat-list render-branch ternary leads with `!mounted ||`). **Verification gate.** `corepack pnpm --filter @persai/web run typecheck` clean; `corepack pnpm --filter @persai/web run lint` clean (0 warnings, max-warnings=0); `corepack pnpm exec prettier --write apps/web/app/app/_components/sidebar.tsx` reports `unchanged`; `corepack pnpm --filter @persai/web run test` 125/125 passing across 24 web test files including the existing `sidebar.test.tsx` (5 tests) which already exercise the chat-list render branches. **Out of scope (deliberate).** No backend / API / contracts / data-model change. No new ADR — `mounted` gating is a well-established React idiom, not system-truth. No `persai-mobile` change — the WebView picks up the new web bundle on next reload. No deploy command run — caller must `pnpm --filter @persai/web run build && docker build && kubectl rollout` per the existing GitOps flow before the device sees the fix. **Risks / residuals.** A one-frame skeleton flash appears on cold load of the sidebar; visually indistinguishable from the existing `data.isLoading` skeleton because the same `<ChatListSkeleton />` component is reused. If a future refactor re-introduces a date-dependent client component without a `mounted` gate, #418 returns and Capacitor handlers regress — the `formatChatRowTimestamp` JSDoc block at line 70 calls this out, and `groupChatsByDate` should be similarly annotated in a follow-up. **Streaming turn lifecycle Slice 1.2 still pending** (server-side soft-detach + per-thread message buffer); FIX 1 is not closed until that lands. **Next recommended step.** Slice 1.2 (server-side soft-detach for streaming turns) — see the FIX 1 changelog entry below for scope.

- **Pre-prod polish 2026 — FIX 2 (tool-result filename hygiene; founder ask 2026-04-25 «3 правки: жизненный цикл стриминга, гигиена tool-result имён файлов, сообщение только с вложениями»; pre-prod polish batch order `1.1 → 3 → 2 → 1.2`; runtime-only sanitizer applied to the LLM-visible tool-result JSON only; verification gate green: 6/6 lint clean, format clean, api+web typecheck clean, runtime + api tests passing; awaiting Slice 1.2 server-side soft-detach to close FIX 1):** before this slice, `apps/runtime/src/modules/turns/turn-execution.service.ts:1963` serialized the entire tool-result `payload` to JSON via `JSON.stringify(payload)` and fed it back into the model's tool-history channel as the next provider call's `toolResult.content`. Worker tools that produce `RuntimeOutputArtifact` records — `image_generate`, `image_edit`, `video_generate`, `tts`, files / sandbox — included full presentation metadata (`artifactId`, `objectKey`, `filename`, `sizeBytes`) in that JSON. Frontier models that saw `"filename": "interesting_scene.png"` empirically liked to quote the value back into their assistant text — producing user-facing bubbles like `Готово, держи interesting_scene.png` while the actual image was _also_ attached to the same message via the parallel `outcome.artifacts` path. The filename appeared twice (once as inline text, once as the attachment label) and the user-facing fix is the founder ask "remove the filename from the text bubble". **Fix.** Sanitize only the model-visible JSON; leave the runtime-side artifact records and the outer `outcome.artifacts` array (which the API attachment pipeline reads through `runtimeOutputArtifactsToMediaArtifacts` in `assistant-runtime.facade.ts`) untouched. New `apps/runtime/src/modules/turns/sanitize-tool-result-for-model.ts` exports `stringifyToolResultPayloadForModel(payload): string` — internally a `JSON.stringify` replacer that detects `RuntimeOutputArtifact`-shaped objects (signature: string `artifactId` + string `kind`, which uniquely distinguishes them from `RuntimeAttachmentRef` whose key field is `attachmentId`) and strips four presentation-only fields: `artifactId`, `objectKey`, `filename`, `sizeBytes`. Keeps `kind`, `mimeType`, `voiceNote`, `caption` so the model retains every semantically meaningful signal it needs (artifact type, MIME for format-aware reasoning, voice-note flag for audio routing, runtime-synthesized caption for follow-up reasoning). `apps/runtime/src/modules/turns/turn-execution.service.ts:createToolExecutionOutcome` swaps `JSON.stringify(payload)` for `stringifyToolResultPayloadForModel(payload)` with an inline FIX 2 comment marking the line as the enforcement point. **Two-surface invariant.** The model-visible JSON gets the redaction; the runtime-side `payload` (used by observability) and the parallel `outcome.artifacts: RuntimeOutputArtifact[]` field (used by `applyToolExecutionOutcome` to surface artifacts to the API and persist `filename` to the chat-attachment DB row so download URLs stay meaningful) are completely untouched. `RuntimeAttachmentRef`-shaped objects (user-uploaded inputs the model already saw filename context for in the user's message) pass through verbatim. Top-level `sourceFilename` / `referenceFilename` on `image_edit` / `video_generate` results pass through verbatim — these are user-supplied input filenames, same justification. Non-artifact-bearing tool results (`web_search`, `knowledge_search`, `memory_write`, `quota_status`, `compact_context`, etc.) get byte-equivalent output to `JSON.stringify(payload)` — the replacer is a no-op when the payload contains nothing that matches the artifact shape signature. **Tests.** New `apps/runtime/test/sanitize-tool-result-for-model.test.ts` exports `runSanitizeToolResultForModelTest()` (single-function pattern matching the runtime suite's custom runner in `run-suite.ts`, NOT node:test's describe/it which the runtime suite does not use) covering seven scenarios: (1) plural `artifacts: RuntimeOutputArtifact[]` (image*generate shape) — strips all four fields, keeps `kind`/`mimeType`/`voiceNote`; (2) singular `artifact` field (video_generate / tts shape) — same redaction; (3) artifact with a model-relevant `caption` — `caption` is preserved alongside `kind`/`mimeType`; (4) `RuntimeAttachmentRef`-shaped object (uses `attachmentId`) — passes through verbatim with `filename`/`objectKey`/`sizeBytes` intact; (5) non-artifact-bearing payload (web_search) — `stringifyToolResultPayloadForModel` is byte-equivalent to `JSON.stringify`; (6) `sourceFilename` / `referenceFilename` at top level alongside an output artifact — top-level filenames preserved, artifact filename stripped; (7) `artifact: null` on a skipped tool result — replacer doesn't crash. `apps/runtime/test/run-suite.ts` registers `runSanitizeToolResultForModelTest` alongside the other 28 runtime tests. `apps/runtime/test/turn-execution.service.test.ts` updates the existing `image_generate` / `image_edit` / `video_generate` end-to-end happy-path tests: the model-visible JSON assertions now require `filename` / `objectKey` / `artifactId` / `sizeBytes` to be `undefined` (regression pin for FIX 2 — if a future refactor accidentally drops the sanitizer or restores `JSON.stringify(payload)`, these assertions catch it), and the runtime-side `*Completed.artifacts[0].filename` assertions are added/kept (`poster.png`, `sunrise-clip.mp4`, `living-room-edit.png`) so the storage surface continues to receive the full filename. **Files touched.** `apps/runtime/src/modules/turns/sanitize-tool-result-for-model.ts`(new — ~70 lines incl. doc header explaining the bug, the two-surface invariant, the`RuntimeOutputArtifact`vs`RuntimeAttachmentRef`distinction, and the field allow-list rationale),`apps/runtime/src/modules/turns/turn-execution.service.ts`(import the helper + swap the JSON serializer + inline FIX 2 comment),`apps/runtime/test/sanitize-tool-result-for-model.test.ts`(new),`apps/runtime/test/run-suite.ts`(register the new test),`apps/runtime/test/turn-execution.service.test.ts`(regression-pin assertions for the redaction, plus storage-side filename assertions on`_Completed.artifacts[0]`), `docs/SESSION-HANDOFF.md`(full entry),`docs/CHANGELOG.md`(this entry). **Architecture decision.** Sanitizing only the LLM-visible JSON (vs deleting`filename`from`RuntimeOutputArtifact` entirely) keeps the existing storage / attachment / DB pipeline untouched and avoids a runtime contract change. Detection by shape signature (`artifactId`+`kind`) means a future tool author who introduces a new artifact-like return shape that doesn't carry both fields will pass through verbatim — explicit opt-in to the hygiene by using the `RuntimeOutputArtifact`shape. Other content-filtering approaches considered and rejected: (a) post-process the assistant text to strip filenames — fragile because the model paraphrases ("the poster", "the image I generated") so a literal-match strip leaves false-positives and misses paraphrases; (b) extend the system prompt with "do not mention filenames" — also unreliable across model versions; (c) suppress the filename at render time on the web client — doesn't fix Telegram / mobile shells, and still embeds the noisy text in the persisted assistant message and in subsequent turns' history. **Verification gate.**`corepack pnpm --filter @persai/runtime run test`passes the full custom suite including the new`runSanitizeToolResultForModelTest`and the updated`turn-execution.service.test.ts`filename-redaction assertions;`corepack pnpm --filter @persai/api run test`45/45 across the relevant suites (sanity check since runtime-contract changes can echo into API consumers — they don't here, but verified);`corepack pnpm -r --if-present run lint`clean across all 6 lint scopes (0 warnings);`corepack pnpm run format:check`clean (one prettier auto-write on the two new runtime files to match project style);`corepack pnpm --filter @persai/api run typecheck`clean (Prisma generate +`tsc --noEmit`); `corepack pnpm --filter @persai/web run typecheck` clean (`tsc --noEmit`). **Out of scope (deliberate).** No web change — FIX 2 is a runtime-only structural fix (the leak source is the LLM context, not the renderer). No new ADR — this is enforcement of the existing runtime contract surface, not a contract change. No telemetry / observability surface change — the runtime-side `payload`field still carries everything for trace inspection. No mobile-side change in`persai-mobile`(runtime is server-side; the web/mobile shells receive the cleaned-up assistant text automatically). **Risks / residuals.** Models that previously relied on seeing the artifact filename in the JSON to phrase a textual handoff ("here is`poster.png`") now have to phrase the response without that token; in practice frontier models handle this fine because the artifact still appears in their next-turn input via the attachment pipeline and they reference it as "the image" / "the result". If a regression surfaces where a model becomes confused about whether an attachment landed, the right correction is to add a richer `caption`field (already preserved through the redaction) or re-introduce a synthesized`description`field — but do **not** re-add`filename`. Future tool authors adding a new tool whose result includes a custom artifact-like shape that is \_not_ `RuntimeOutputArtifact` (i.e., doesn't carry both `artifactId` and `kind` strings) will pass through verbatim — that's the intended escape hatch; if they want the same hygiene, use the `RuntimeOutputArtifact` shape. The DB attachment metadata still receives `poster.png` / `sunrise-clip.mp4` / `living-room-edit.png` so download URLs stay meaningful, voice-note routing is preserved through the kept `voiceNote` field, and the side-channel image binding to chat messages is unaffected. **Streaming turn lifecycle Slice 1.2 still pending** (server-side soft-detach + per-thread message buffer); FIX 1 is not closed until that lands. **Next recommended step.** **FIX 1, slice 1.2** — server-side soft-detach for the streaming turn lifecycle: differentiate "user pressed Stop" (hard abort, propagate `AbortController`) from "client tab/screen went background" (soft disconnect, let the runtime finish writing to durable session state, allow the next reconnect to resume from the persisted partial). Touches `apps/api/src/modules/workspace-management/application/stream-web-chat-turn.service.ts` and the runtime turn finalization path; protocol-level change requires an ADR amendment under ADR-073.

- **Pre-prod polish 2026 — FIX 3 (attachments-only user message no longer renders «(attached files)»; founder ask 2026-04-25 «3 правки: жизненный цикл стриминга, гигиена tool-result имён файлов, сообщение только с вложениями»; pre-prod polish batch order `1.1 → 3 → 2 → 1.2`; web-only renderer-side suppression with shared sentinel; verification gate green: 5/5 lint clean, format clean, api+web typecheck clean, web tests 119/119 passing; awaiting FIX 2 (tool-result filename hygiene) next, then Slice 1.2 server-side soft-detach to close FIX 1):** before this slice, `apps/web/app/app/_components/chat-input.tsx:180` filled the user message's text with a hard-coded `"(attached files)"` whenever the user pressed Send with at least one staged attachment but no typed text. That string was a workaround for `SendWebChatTurnService.parseInput` (`apps/api/src/modules/workspace-management/application/send-web-chat-turn.service.ts:166`) rejecting empty `message` payloads with `400 BadRequest`, but it leaked into the user bubble verbatim — every attachments-only message displayed a literal «(attached files)» line above the actual attachments, both during the optimistic `sending` phase and forever afterwards in persisted history. **Fix.** Renderer-side suppression with a shared sentinel — the placeholder still reaches the API (so the contract stays intact), but the user bubble recognizes it at render time and hides the `<p>` for any user-role message whose only content is the placeholder (or, defensively, whitespace-only content). New `apps/web/app/app/_components/attachments-only-placeholder.ts` exports `ATTACHMENTS_ONLY_PLACEHOLDER = "(attached files)"` and `isAttachmentsOnlyPlaceholderText(content)` — both producer (`chat-input.tsx`) and renderer (`chat-message.tsx`) read from this single module so they cannot drift. `chat-input.tsx` imports the constant and uses it in place of the hard-coded string (no behavior change at the network layer; same exact bytes go to the API). `chat-message.tsx` imports the predicate, computes `hideUserTextForAttachmentsOnly = isUser && (message.attachments?.length ?? 0) > 0 && isAttachmentsOnlyPlaceholderText(message.content)` next to the existing `hideUserVoiceTranscript` flag, and gates the user-side `<p>` on `!hideUserVoiceTranscript && !hideUserTextForAttachmentsOnly`. The `AttachmentStrip`'s `mt-0` className override (already used for the voice-only path) now also fires when `hideUserTextForAttachmentsOnly` is true so the bubble's accent background doesn't carry an awkward empty top gap where the missing text used to live. **The suppression is deliberately gated on `attachments.length > 0`**: if a future composer regression were to write the placeholder text without staging any attachment, the bubble would render it verbatim instead of silently swallowing user-visible content — there is a regression test for that case (placeholder content alone with empty attachments → renders verbatim). **Architecture decision.** A contract change to allow empty `message` would touch `packages/contracts/openapi.yaml` + the Nest service + the runtime prompt (LLM would now see an empty user turn) + tests in api + contracts, and is system-truth territory needing an ADR. For pre-prod polish the renderer-side suppression is sufficient; the placeholder remains the canonical sentinel because keeping the human-readable string also means any historical row that already has it persisted is suppressed by the same predicate (no migration required). **Tests.** New `describe("ChatMessageBubble — attachments-only user message (FIX 3)")` block in `apps/web/app/app/_components/chat-message.test.tsx` adds four cases: placeholder + image attachment → no `<p>` containing the placeholder text; whitespace-only content + image attachment → no `p.whitespace-pre-wrap` element rendered at all (queried via `container.querySelector`); real text + image attachment → text still renders verbatim; placeholder text alone (no attachments) → renders verbatim, defensive against composer regressions. Web suite goes from 115/115 (Slice 1.1 baseline) to **119/119 passing**. **Files touched.** `apps/web/app/app/_components/attachments-only-placeholder.ts` (new), `apps/web/app/app/_components/chat-input.tsx` (import + use constant), `apps/web/app/app/_components/chat-message.tsx` (import + flag + gate `<p>` + conditional `mt-0`), `apps/web/app/app/_components/chat-message.test.tsx` (new describe block + image-attachment factory), `docs/SESSION-HANDOFF.md` (full entry), `docs/CHANGELOG.md` (this entry). **Verification gate.** `corepack pnpm -r --if-present run lint` clean (5 of 5 lint-bearing workspace projects), `corepack pnpm run format:check` clean (one prettier write on the new module to match the project's import-block style), `corepack pnpm --filter @persai/api run typecheck` clean (Prisma generate + `tsc --noEmit`), `corepack pnpm --filter @persai/web run typecheck` clean (`tsc --noEmit`), `corepack pnpm --filter @persai/web run test` 119/119 passing across 23 web test files. **Out of scope (deliberate).** No backend changes. No contract changes. No new ADR — this is a UI polish, not a system-truth change. No telemetry add — the user already has visual confirmation through the absent placeholder. No mobile-side change in `persai-mobile` (this is purely client-side rendering that lives in the web shell loaded into Capacitor; the WebView gets the new behavior automatically). **Risks / residuals.** The user message's `content` field still equals «(attached files)» in the database and the runtime prompt sent to the LLM still contains that string as the user turn's text — empirically the model handles this gracefully because the staged attachments are also delivered to the model in the same turn, but if we ever observe LLM responses that fixate on the literal phrase, the right correction is the contract change described above (allow empty `message`), not a different sentinel. A bubble that contains only the attachment strip is shorter than a bubble with text — visual review confirms the bubble's accent background, padding, and bottom-corner radius still look correct thanks to the `mt-0` override; if a future refactor strips that override, the test that checks for absence of `p.whitespace-pre-wrap` will still pass, so add a visual-regression check before that refactor lands. **Streaming turn lifecycle Slice 1.2 still pending** (server-side soft-detach + per-thread message buffer); FIX 1 is not closed until that lands. **Next recommended step.** Per founder's stack-rank, **FIX 2** (tool-result filename hygiene) — when an assistant tool emits an image (e.g., `image_generate` returning `interesting_scene.png` plus the binary), the filename leaks into the assistant text bubble while the image is also rendered as an attachment; the fix path likely lives in the tool-result formatter on the runtime side or in the assistant message normalization on the API side and needs a diagnostic walk to identify the exact emission point before scoping. After FIX 2, FIX 1 closes with Slice 1.2 (server-side soft-detach + stream resume).

- **Pre-prod polish 2026 — Slice 1.1 of FIX 1 (streaming turn lifecycle): per-thread `isStreaming` + per-thread AbortController + sidebar live-streaming dot (founder ask 2026-04-25 «3 правки: жизненный цикл стриминга, гигиена tool-result имён файлов, сообщение только с вложениями»; pre-prod polish batch order `1.1 → 3 → 2 → 1.2`; web-only frontend refactor; verification gate green: 5/5 lint clean, format clean, api+web typecheck clean, web tests 115/115 passing; awaiting Slice 1.2 server-side soft-detach to close FIX 1):** before this slice, `apps/web/app/app/_components/use-chat.ts` held `isStreaming` in a single `useState(false)` local to the hook. The thread-switch reset block (lines 374–396 — clears `messages` / `activities` / `compaction` / `pendingSendStatus` when `prevThreadKeyRef.current !== threadKey`) deliberately does **not** clear `isStreaming` because the in-flight stream from the previous thread is still alive; effect: switching from Chat A (mid-stream) to Chat B leaves `isStreaming === true` for the same hook instance, `chat-input.tsx`'s `inputDisabled || isStreaming` rule disables the textarea in Chat B, and the user cannot type until A finishes. Same single-ref shape applied to `abortRef` (single `useRef<AbortController | null>(null)`), making `stop()` racy on top of the UX lock — A's `finally { abortRef.current = null }` would clobber a controller B installed afterwards, so a Stop button click for B could become a no-op. **Fix.** Lift "which threads are currently streaming?" out of the per-call hook into a tree-shared registry. New `apps/web/app/app/_components/streaming-threads.tsx` exposes `<StreamingThreadsProvider>`, `useStreamingThreadsRegistry() → { activeThreads: ReadonlySet<string>; markStreaming(threadKey, active) }`, and a narrow `useIsThreadStreaming(threadKey)` consumer; `markStreaming` is idempotent (returns the same `Set` reference when value matches existing membership, so subscribers don't churn). Registry shape is a `ReadonlySet<string>` keyed by `surfaceThreadKey` and updated through `useState` so React schedules re-renders for subscribers when a thread enters/leaves the active set. Production wiring: `<StreamingThreadsProvider>` mounted in both branches of `apps/web/app/app/_components/app-shell.tsx` (the setup-page short-circuit AND the main shell), so every authenticated surface that mounts `useChat` sees one shared registry instance. Refactor in `useChat`: replace the local `isStreaming` boolean with `const { activeThreads, markStreaming } = useStreamingThreadsRegistry(); const isStreaming = activeThreads.has(threadKey)`; replace the single `abortRef` with `abortControllersByThreadRef = useRef<Map<string, AbortController>>(new Map())`; `send()` and `sendWelcome()` capture `const sendThreadKey = threadKey` at call time so every subsequent `markStreaming` / abort-map mutation in that turn targets the _originating_ thread (not whichever thread the user navigated to before the `finally` block runs); per-turn `releaseAbortController()` helper only deletes the map entry if it still equals _this_ turn's controller (so a fast retry that overwrites the entry doesn't get nuked by the older turn's cleanup); `stop()` aborts only `abortControllersByThreadRef.current.get(threadKey)` — the stream attached to the thread the user is _currently_ viewing — so streams in other threads keep generating in the background and the new sidebar dot lights up for them. **Tests-without-provider compatibility.** `useStreamingThreadsRegistry()` falls back to a hook-local registry (its own `useRegistryState()` instance) when no provider is mounted in the context tree, so the existing 14 `useChat` tests + the 5 `sidebar` tests + everything else keep working _without_ any per-test wrapper boilerplate. New `streaming-threads.test.tsx` covers the registry directly (3 tests: independent thread tracking, idempotent no-op repeated marks return the same `Set` reference, no-provider fallback works). New `describe("per-thread streaming (slice 1.1)")` block in `use-chat.test.tsx` adds two tests: thread B's view never observes thread A's `isStreaming === true`, and `stop()` aborts only the _current_ thread's controller while the other thread's controller stays untouched (verified by reading `signal.aborted` per-stream). **Sidebar live indicator.** `ChatListItem` in `apps/web/app/app/_components/sidebar.tsx` reads `useIsThreadStreaming(item.chat.surfaceThreadKey)` and renders a small `h-1.5 w-1.5 animate-pulse rounded-full bg-accent` dot next to the chat title when the thread is in flight, with `title` / `aria-label` from the new `sidebar.streamingIndicator` translation (`"Generating reply"` en, `"Генерирует ответ"` ru). **What's NOT in this slice (deliberate).** The thread-switch reset block in `useChat` is left as-is — an in-flight stream from Chat A continues calling `setMessages((prev) => prev.map(... assistantMsgId ...))` against the cleared messages array, so deltas accumulated AFTER the user switched away are dropped from Chat A's UI even after switching back; recovering "the text I missed while I was elsewhere" is a server-side soft-detach + resume problem owned by Slice 1.2 and would conflate two fixes if shoehorned here; `chat-input.tsx`'s `inputDisabled || isStreaming` rule is unchanged and now gets per-thread `isStreaming` for free, so no change in `chat-input.tsx` was needed. No backend / API / data-model change; no new ADR (this is frontend state-shape refactor, not system-truth change). **Files touched.** `apps/web/app/app/_components/streaming-threads.tsx` (new), `apps/web/app/app/_components/streaming-threads.test.tsx` (new), `apps/web/app/app/_components/app-shell.tsx` (provider in both branches), `apps/web/app/app/_components/use-chat.ts` (registry + per-thread map + per-turn `sendThreadKey` capture + `releaseAbortController` + per-thread `stop`), `apps/web/app/app/_components/use-chat.test.tsx` (new describe block), `apps/web/app/app/_components/sidebar.tsx` (live indicator dot), `apps/web/messages/en.json` + `apps/web/messages/ru.json` (`sidebar.streamingIndicator`), `docs/SESSION-HANDOFF.md` (full entry), `docs/CHANGELOG.md` (this entry). **Risks / residuals.** The classic "double-send in the same render frame" race against `useState`-backed `isStreaming` is unchanged from before — original code had it too, and the user-facing Stop UI only allows one click per render. Sidebar indicator depends on `surfaceThreadKey` matching the chat's URL key (which is true today: `ChatListItem.onNavigate` pushes `?thread=${item.chat.surfaceThreadKey}`, exactly what `useChat(threadKey)` consumes); flagged here so a future refactor that splits the URL thread param from the registry key catches this assumption. **Slice 1.2 still required to close FIX 1** — closing the phone screen mid-image-generation still truncates the assistant text because the server aborts the runtime turn on SSE close (`assistant.controller.ts` calls `clientAbortController.abort()` on disconnect); slice 1.2 will distinguish hard-abort (Stop button) from soft-disconnect (tab/screen backgrounded) so the runtime keeps the turn alive and the next reconnect can resume it. **Next recommended step.** Per founder's stack-rank, **FIX 3** (attachments-only message must not display the «(attached files)» placeholder) — change lives in `chat-message.tsx` rendering when `message.content.trim().length === 0 && message.attachments.length > 0`; then **FIX 2** (tool-result filename hygiene); FIX 1 closes with Slice 1.2 (server-side soft-detach + resume).

- **ADR-076 hotfix — Slice 3 cold-start bootstrap was returning 401 for every authenticated user (founder live `persai-dev` gate 2026-04-25 «после slice 076 не загружаются асистенты», screenshot showed sidebar header reading `Не создан` indefinitely; same regression class as ADR-074 «Session expired»; `apps/api` middleware allowlist + `apps/web` defense-in-depth fallback; verification gate green; awaiting redeploy of new `apps/api` + `apps/web` images and a re-run of the ADR-076 founder live `persai-dev` gate):** the production-baseline ADR-076 deploy was already live at api+web image tag `1a2207d0` on `persai-dev`, but every authenticated user saw the assistant card stuck on `Не создан` and an empty chat list — even though the backing data exists in the database and the legacy per-endpoint routes still work for the same Clerk session. Root cause is a two-layer bug: the **primary cause** is in `apps/api` — the `ClerkAuthMiddleware` is wired through `IdentityAccessModule.configure(MiddlewareConsumer)` to a hardcoded list of routes via `.forRoutes(...)`, and Slice 3's new `GET /api/v1/app/bootstrap` endpoint (the single SSR-bootstrap surface that replaces the six-call client fan-out) was added to `AppBootstrapController` without a matching entry in that allowlist — so requests reached the controller with `req.resolvedAppUser === undefined`, the controller correctly threw `UnauthorizedException("Authenticated user context is missing.")`, and the route returned 401 in ~1 ms with no Clerk `verifyToken` call ever happening. GKE log audit confirmed: every `POST/GET /api/v1/app/bootstrap` request from the production session returned 401, while every `/api/v1/admin/...` and `/api/v1/assistant` request from the same Clerk session returned 200 — auth itself was healthy, only this one route was missing from the allowlist. This is the **exact same regression class** that ADR-074 Memory Center hit when `POST /api/v1/assistant/memory/items/:itemId/close-open-loop` was added without the matching middleware registration; the existing test in `apps/api/test/identity-access.module.test.ts` even calls the failure mode out by name. The **secondary cause** is in `apps/web` — `useAppData(initialData)` in `apps/web/app/app/_components/use-app-data.ts` only triggered the legacy client fan-out when `initialData === null` (the documented degraded-SSR path), but when the SSR bootstrap returned an envelope with all sections set to `{ ok: false, error: { ... } }` (which is exactly what Slice 3's `fetch-app-bootstrap.ts` emits on a 401 from the API) the hook treated that as a successful seed and the client fan-out never fired. The user was left staring at "Не создан" with no recovery path short of a full session reset. **Fix.** Two-line surgical fix on the API side: `apps/api/src/modules/identity-access/identity-access.module.ts` adds `{ path: "api/v1/app/bootstrap", method: RequestMethod.GET }` to the `forRoutes` list. Defense-in-depth on the web side: `apps/web/app/app/_components/use-app-data.ts` adds a new `needsClientFallback: boolean` flag inside `SeededState` (`true` whenever the seeded `assistant` section is `ok: false`), and the cold-start `useEffect(loadAll, [initialData])` now also fires `loadAll()` when `seed.current.needsClientFallback === true` — so any future bootstrap regression (auth, network, parse error, partial section failure) gracefully falls back to the legacy six-call fan-out instead of leaving the UI in a permanently empty state. The `isLoading` flag stays `true` while `needsClientFallback` is true so the sidebar shows the proper cold-start skeleton during the fallback fan-out, instead of a misleading "empty list" affordance. **Regression test pinned.** `apps/api/test/identity-access.module.test.ts` gains a third explicit assertion in the same shape as the ADR-074 entry, with a long-form comment documenting the failure mode and how the screenshot looked, so any future `forRoutes` rewrite that drops the route immediately fails CI before reaching production. **Files touched.** `apps/api/src/modules/identity-access/identity-access.module.ts` (one new entry in the `forRoutes` allowlist for `GET /api/v1/app/bootstrap`), `apps/api/test/identity-access.module.test.ts` (regression assertion + ADR-076-shaped comment), `apps/web/app/app/_components/use-app-data.ts` (`SeededState.needsClientFallback`, `seedFromInitialData` sets it on errored assistant section, `useEffect` triggers `loadAll()` when set, `isLoading` left true during the fallback so the cold-start skeleton renders correctly), `docs/CHANGELOG.md` (this entry), `docs/SESSION-HANDOFF.md` (matching session entry). **Verification gate green** — `corepack pnpm -r --if-present run lint` clean (5 of 5 lint-bearing workspace projects), `corepack pnpm run format:check` clean, `corepack pnpm --filter @persai/api run typecheck` clean (Prisma generate + `tsc --noEmit`), `corepack pnpm --filter @persai/web run typecheck` clean (`tsc --noEmit`), `corepack pnpm --filter @persai/web run test` 110/110 passing, `corepack pnpm --filter @persai/api run test` 0 failed including the new regression assertion. **Out of scope (deliberate).** No architecture / API contract / data-model change — the bootstrap envelope shape, the bootstrap controller, the `fetchAppBootstrap` server helper, the avatar pipeline, the skeleton contracts, and the `next/dynamic` slide-over deferral all stay exactly as they landed in Batch A + Batch B. The Slice 3 envelope shape (`{ ok, data | error }` per section) is the right shape — the bug was the auth middleware not running on this one route. No transitional dual-mode where the client side ALSO calls the legacy six routes when bootstrap returns `ok: true` — that would just bring back the very pop-in that Slice 3 was designed to remove; the fallback is gated strictly on `needsClientFallback`, which only goes high when bootstrap itself failed. No retroactive change to `auth-verify.controller.ts` or any other already-allowlisted route. **Diagnostic methodology recorded.** GKE audit followed the standard runbook (`infra/dev/gke/RUNBOOK.md`): `kubectl get pods -n persai-dev` confirmed both `api` replicas at image `1a2207d0`, `kubectl logs -n persai-dev api-... -c api --since=15m` filtered for `/app/bootstrap` returned only 401 entries (zero 200), `kubectl logs ... | rg '"status":200'` filtered for non-health paths confirmed the same Clerk user `4d3d176a-866d-4087-a66e-2b2f372512e5` was making authenticated requests to `/api/v1/admin/*` successfully — pinpointing the bug to a route-specific middleware miss, not a global auth outage. An in-cluster `curl` probe via `kubectl run probe-curl --image=curlimages/curl -n persai-dev` confirmed the route returns 401 unauth (so the route IS registered with NestJS — only the middleware is absent), ruling out a missing-controller-registration hypothesis. **Awaiting** redeploy of new `apps/api` + `apps/web` images on `persai-dev` (CI will pick up the next push) and a founder live `persai-dev` re-gate covering: (a) cold load of `/app` populates sidebar / footer / chat header in the first paint with no spinner / skeleton flash and the actual assistant name in the assistant card (NOT `Не создан`); (b) GKE `kubectl logs -n persai-dev -l app.kubernetes.io/name=api -c api` shows `/api/v1/app/bootstrap` returning 200 with the Clerk userId populated; (c) the legacy six-call fallback path can be triggered manually by force-emptying the bootstrap response and confirming the sidebar still populates from the client fan-out (defense-in-depth proven). **Next recommended step after this commit lands** — confirm the GKE deploy goes green, founder re-runs the four ADR-076 live `persai-dev` gates that were originally green-lit when ADR-076 closed, then continue with the ADR-075 follow-up offline-pipeline-hardening slice as planned.

- **ADR-076 closed at Slices 1–6 + Section M; Slice 7 deferred (founder decision 2026-04-25 «делай все без слайс7» following the «по-хорошему его нужно делать?» exchange; verification gate green; this commit is the end-of-ADR-076 batch commit covering both repos):** ADR-076 (PersAI cold-start visual continuity & bootstrap pipeline) closes after Slice 1 (cookie-as-truth theme + SSR-baked `<html class>` + Section M sending-indicator micro-fix), Slice 2a + 2b (Capacitor system-bars bridge + cold-start visual continuity), Batch A = Slice 3 + Slice 4 (RSC bootstrap + content-addressed avatar pipeline), and Batch B = Slice 5 + Slice 6 (skeleton contracts where data is genuinely pending + slide-over `next/dynamic` code-splitting + bundle audit) all landed and verified green over the 2026-04-25 wave. **Slice 7 (Service-Worker PWA shell) is explicitly deferred**, not landed and not silently dropped. Reasoning recorded in ADR-076 ledger and Status block: (a) the cold-start artifacts that originally motivated ADR-076 — theme flash, empty-shell pop-in, avatar pop-in — are fully resolved by Slices 1, 3, 4 and the `next/dynamic` slide-over deferral in Slice 6 already removes 78,726 B (~76.9 KiB) of JS from the initial `/app` route bundle. The original Slice 7 acceptance criteria were always conditional on a measured production baseline (« decision after Batch B lands and a measured Slice 6 baseline is captured») — that baseline does not yet exist, so we cannot honestly say a Service Worker layer is justified. (b) Founder live test on Z Fold 6 with airplane mode (both before launch and mid-session) surfaced two real bugs in ADR-075's offline pipeline that a Service Worker would not fix: `<OfflineGate />` is mounted only inside `AppShell` (so it never appears on `/`, `/sign-in`, `/sign-up`, pre-auth setup, or any cold-start failure that prevents hydration), and Capacitor 8's `server.errorPath: "offline.html"` does not reliably swap to `www/offline.html` on `ERR_INTERNET_DISCONNECTED` main-frame errors when `server.url` points at a remote origin. SW only helps for the second cold-start of an already-installed page and cannot run if the WebView never reaches the page in the first place — so the right next step is an ADR-075 follow-up slice, not Slice 7. The follow-up scope is recorded in the ADR ledger entry for Slice 7: mount `<OfflineGate />` at root layout, harden `useNetworkOnline` with active health probing, add a custom Android `WebViewClient.onReceivedError` shim in `MainActivity.java` that explicitly loads `file:///android_asset/public/offline.html`, refresh `www/offline.html` to the warm `--chrome` palette from Slice 1. Once that ADR-075 follow-up lands AND a production baseline is captured on real devices, Slice 7 gets re-evaluated — flipped to `landed` if SW measurably helps, or to `decided not to ship` if the gain is below the SW lifecycle/iOS-quirk cost. The PWA-installable manifest portion of Slice 7 (Add-to-Home-Screen on RU desktops where Play Store is unreliable, Chrome desktop standalone-window install) stays bundled with Slice 7 rather than shipping standalone. **Verification gate (closing run)** — `corepack pnpm -r --if-present run lint` clean (5 of 5 lint-bearing workspace projects), `corepack pnpm run format:check` clean, `corepack pnpm --filter @persai/api run typecheck` clean (Prisma generate + `tsc --noEmit`), `corepack pnpm --filter @persai/web run typecheck` clean (`tsc --noEmit`), `corepack pnpm --filter @persai/web run test` 110/110 passing, `corepack pnpm --filter @persai/api run test` 130/130 passing across 19 node test suites. **Files touched in this closing slice (docs only, no code change).** `docs/ADR/076-cold-start-visual-continuity-and-bootstrap-pipeline.md` (Status block flipped to "Accepted and closed at Slices 1, 2, Batch A (3+4), Batch B (5+6) + Section M"; `Updated:` line carries the deferral decision and ADR-075 follow-up scope; Slice 7 ledger row flipped from `proposed` to `deferred` with the full reasoning), `docs/CHANGELOG.md` (this entry), `docs/SESSION-HANDOFF.md` (matching session entry + end-of-program summary). **End-of-program file footprint (queued in working tree until this commit).** `apps/api`: new `app-bootstrap.controller.ts`, new `get-assistant-app-bootstrap.service.ts`, modified `manage-assistant-avatar.service.ts` (content-addressed URLs + `downloadByHash`), modified `assistant-lifecycle.mapper.ts` (`sanitizeAvatarUrl`), modified `assistant.controller.ts` (legacy `GET /avatar` removed, new bearer-protected `GET /avatar/:hash`), `workspace-management.module.ts` wired; new tests for bootstrap, avatar URL helpers, lifecycle sanitiser. `apps/web`: new `app/api/avatar/[hash]/route.ts` (cookie-auth BFF), new `app/app/_server/fetch-app-bootstrap.ts`, new `app/app/_components/sidebar.test.tsx`, new `app/app/_components/chat-message.test.tsx`; modified `app/layout.tsx` (SSR-baked theme + `<meta theme-color>` + `themeFallbackScript`), `app/app/layout.tsx` (async RSC + bootstrap fetch), `next.config.ts` (`Accept-CH`/`Critical-CH`/`Vary` headers), `app/app/_components/{app-shell,sidebar,chat-area,chat-input,chat-message,assistant-avatar,assistant-settings,offline-gate,use-app-data,use-theme}.tsx/.ts`, `app/app/setup/page.tsx`, `app/app/chat/page.tsx`, `app/page.tsx` (landing), `messages/{en,ru}.json`. `packages/contracts`: `openapi.yaml` (new `/app/bootstrap` path + per-section schemas + `BootstrapSectionError` envelope + `AssistantNotificationPreferenceState` + content-addressed avatar URL doc), regenerated orval clients under `src/generated/**`. `persai-mobile`: new `SystemBarsBridge.java`, new `colors.xml`, new `drawable/splash_logo.xml`, modified `MainActivity.java` (Java bridge registration + pre-WebView system-bars colouring from SharedPreferences), modified `values/styles.xml` (`AppTheme.NoActionBarLaunch` modernised to `Theme.SplashScreen` API attributes), modified `capacitor.config.ts` (`android.backgroundColor` + `ios.backgroundColor` = `#161513`), rewritten `ios/App/App/Base.lproj/LaunchScreen.storyboard` (chrome bg + centred PersAI UILabel in chrome_light), emptied `ios/App/App/Assets.xcassets/Splash.imageset/Contents.json`. **Pre-launch UI polish 2026 residue.** Several scoped UX slices that landed in the same 2026-04-25 wave but outside ADR-076 — Telegram-style attachment menu, hold-to-record floating mic overlay, assistant-card cog affordance, chat-row kebab portal escape, header-title-on-new-chat fix, premium send-failed indicator, warm tonal palette / bento desktop frame / Geist Sans+Mono — also queued for this same end-of-batch commit per the founder rule «комит только в конце ADR». Each has its own dedicated CHANGELOG entry below; this closing entry only covers the ADR-076 program, the residue is itemised individually in their own entries. **Awaiting** `persai-dev` deploy + founder live `persai-dev` gate covering all four ADR-076 user-visible deltas at once: (a) cold load of `/app` populates sidebar / footer / chat header in the first paint with no spinner / skeleton flash; (b) deleting the last chat shows a brief 2–3 row shimmer in place of the empty state during in-flight `reloadChats`; (c) DevTools Network shows `assistant-settings` and `telegram-connect` chunks fetched only on first open of their respective slide-overs; (d) cold reload reuses the HTTP cache for the avatar (no JS-driven round-trip in DevTools Network) and a fresh upload produces a new content hash → new `/api/avatar/<hash>.<ext>` URL → fresh fetch on next paint. **Next recommended step after this commit lands** — ADR-075 follow-up slice (offline pipeline hardening) per the scope recorded in ADR-076 Slice 7 ledger row.

- **Pre-launch UI polish 2026 (continued) — Telegram-style hold-to-record on touch with floating mic overlay (founder ask 2026-04-25 «и еще правка для записи голосового в мобилке запись нужно начинать при удержании можно показать по центру и чуть выше поля ввода какую то анимацию микрофона чтобы понятно было что идёт запись + секунды при отпускании отправка как в TG в обычном web всё и так норм»; presentational + UX slice on `apps/web` only, no architecture / API / data-model change; verification gate green; awaiting founder live mobile gate on Z Fold 6):** the chat composer's mic button used the same `onClick → toggle` model on both desktop and touch, which on mobile felt foreign after years of Telegram press-and-hold UX — tap to start, do something else, tap again to send, with a desktop-shaped «Cancel / Send» banner sitting above the composer. The fix branches the gesture model on `useTouchDevice()` so touch users get press-and-hold while desktop users keep their existing toggle exactly as-is (the founder explicitly asked us not to disturb the web flow). **Pointer-event lifecycle (touch only).** New refs `holdActiveRef` / `holdStartTimeRef` / `holdStartYRef` / `cancelArmedRef` (+ `cancelArmed` state) drive a small state machine on the mic `<button>`: `onPointerDown` (gated on `e.pointerType === "touch"`) calls `e.preventDefault()` (suppresses the synthetic `click` follow-up + steals focus from the textarea), `setPointerCapture(pointerId)` so move/up keep firing on the mic button even when the thumb drifts off, fires a 15 ms `navigator.vibrate` haptic burst (best-effort `try/catch`; iOS lacks the API), and starts the recorder. `onPointerMove` tracks `dy = startY - currentY` and flips `cancelArmedRef.current` once `dy > 80 px`, with each transition into the armed state firing a 10 ms vibrate. `onPointerUp` releases capture and routes the gesture: if `cancelArmedRef.current === true` (swipe-up cancel) **OR** the press lasted less than `HOLD_MIN_MS = 250 ms` (treated as an accidental tap) → `cancelRecording()`. Otherwise → `stopRecording()` (the existing path that finalises the blob, dispatches `onTranscribeVoice`, and ultimately sends — same as the founder's existing voice flow on web). `onPointerCancel` (browser-initiated cancel: pull-to-refresh, OS interruption, parent gets a `touchcancel`) routes unconditionally to `cancelRecording()`. **Floating mic overlay (touch only).** Mounted under the same `relative` composer parent as the attachment popover, anchored `absolute bottom-full left-1/2 -translate-x-1/2 mb-3` so it sits centred a hair above the input row — exactly where the founder asked. The overlay itself is `pointer-events-none`; the mic button keeps the captured pointer, so the user's thumb continues to drive the gesture even though the overlay is layered on top of it. Visual contents: a `relative h-14 w-14` container with two stacked layers — an `absolute inset-0 animate-ping rounded-full bg-accent/30` ring (warm sage in resting state, `bg-destructive/30` once cancel is armed) and on top of it a `bg-accent/15 text-accent` filled disc with the `Mic` icon. Below: a monospace `tabular-nums` timer (`formatDuration(recordingSeconds)`) and a single-line caption that crossfades between «Отпустите, чтобы отправить · Свайп вверх — отмена» and «Отпустите, чтобы отменить» based on `cancelArmed`. All colour tokens swap to destructive when cancel-armed. `AnimatePresence` + `motion.div` with `initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 12, scale: 0.96 }}` → `animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0, scale: 1 }}` → matching exit, `duration: 0.18, ease: [0.22, 1, 0.36, 1]` — same warm 180 ms curve as the attachment menu and AccountFooter popup. **Mic button styling on touch.** The button itself gains `bg-accent/15 text-accent` while `isRecording && !cancelArmed`, swapping to `bg-destructive/15 text-destructive` once `cancelArmed` engages — so the user simultaneously sees the overlay change tone AND feels the button under their thumb light up, two confirmation surfaces for the same gesture. `select-none` suppresses the long-press text-selection blue glow on Android Chromium WebView; `onContextMenu={preventDefault}` suppresses the long-press image/save menu on iOS WKWebView; `aria-label` and `title` use `voiceHoldToRecord` on touch and the existing `voiceMessage` on desktop. **Desktop banner gated.** The original «Запись 0:12 [Cancel] [Send]» banner above the composer (`isRecording && (...border-destructive/30 bg-destructive/5...)`) was a desktop-shaped two-button affordance, useless under press-and-hold. Now gated to `isRecording && !isTouchDevice` so desktop keeps it and touch falls back to the floating overlay. **i18n.** Four new `chat.voice*` keys in `messages/{ru,en}.json` — `voiceHoldToRecord` (mic button's `title`/`aria-label` on touch), `voiceHoldRelease` (primary overlay caption), `voiceSwipeUpToCancel` (secondary half of the resting-state caption), `voiceCancelArmed` (caption shown once the swipe threshold is crossed). **Files touched.** `apps/web/app/app/_components/chat-input.tsx` (pointer handlers, hold/cancel-armed state machine, floating overlay JSX, mic button styling on touch, top-banner gating, `safeVibrate` helper), `apps/web/messages/ru.json` (four new chat keys), `apps/web/messages/en.json` (four new chat keys), `docs/SESSION-HANDOFF.md` (matching session entry), `docs/CHANGELOG.md` (this entry). **Verification gate.** `corepack pnpm -r --if-present run lint` clean (5 of 5 lint-bearing workspace projects), `corepack pnpm run format:check` clean, `corepack pnpm --filter @persai/web run typecheck` clean.
