No new tests — pure presentation slice with no contract / state-machine / wire-format change; existing component tests re-render through the unchanged props because `startRecording` / `stopRecording` / `cancelRecording` retain their signatures. **Out of scope (deliberate).** No architecture / API / data-model change; ADR-072 / ADR-073 / ADR-074 / ADR-075 / ADR-076 are unaffected. The recorder still uses `MediaRecorder` (web `getUserMedia`), which works inside Capacitor Android Chromium WebView (already verified live on Z Fold 6) and inside iOS WKWebView (the existing `NSMicrophoneUsageDescription` from ADR-075 covers it); no `cap sync` needed because the change is purely web-side and ships to mobile via the existing `server.url` contract on next page load. No swipe-left-to-show-cancel-zone (Telegram's other cancel gesture) — single upward-swipe cancel zone is enough for this slice. No haptic feedback on iOS (the `navigator.vibrate` API simply isn't there; safely no-ops). No `@capacitor/haptics` adoption — the JS-glue model from ADR-075 keeps the recorder web-side, and adding a native plugin just for vibration on iOS isn't worth the cap-sync round-trip. **Commit posture.** Changes left uncommitted in the working tree, alongside the prior pre-launch UI polish residue (Telegram-style attachment menu, assistant-card cog, chat-row kebab portal escape, header-title-on-new-chat fix, premium send-failed indicator) and the still-uncommitted ADR-076 Batch A + Batch B residue, all queued for the next batched commit. **Awaiting** founder live mobile gate on Z Fold 6: hold the mic → see the floating overlay with timer pulsing in warm sage; release on the mic → message routes through the existing transcribe → send pipeline; swipe up past the cancel threshold and release → recording cancels with no send (overlay fades out, no message in the chat); quick tap (< 250 ms) → no recording is sent (treated as an accidental press, no transient bubble appears).

- **Pre-launch UI polish 2026 (continued) — live header title for newly created chats + premium send-failed indicator (founder asks 2026-04-25 «1 при создании нового чата он появляется в списке слева при моем первом сообщении с заголовком первые несколько слов моего сообщения а заголовок сверху при это не обновляется до обновления страницы», «2 смотри фото, мне не нравится как это оформлено: не доставлено, повторить, отменить, не красиво всё смешано внутри бабла - нужно обыграть по проф и дорого»; presentational + UX slice on `apps/web` only, no architecture / API / data-model change; verification gate green):** two scoped UX defects spotted right after the Telegram-style attachment menu landed are fixed in one slice. **(1) Header title race on new-chat first send.** `apps/web/app/app/chat/page.tsx` previously matched its `existingChat` lookup against `threadFromUrl` (`appData.chats.find(c => c.chat.surfaceThreadKey === threadFromUrl)`) and then bailed when `threadFromUrl` was `null` — which is exactly the case for a brand-new chat the user is composing into. The first send hit the server, the server created a row whose `surfaceThreadKey` matched the locally-generated `web-${Date.now()}` key, `reloadChats()` landed the row in the sidebar (so its auto-derived title — first words of the message — appeared in the list immediately), but the `<header>` of the chat was still bound to `existingChat?.chat.title ?? undefined ?? t("newChat")` and so kept showing «Новый чат» / «New chat» until a hard refresh. Fix: lookup is now `appData.chats.find(c => c.chat.surfaceThreadKey === threadKey)`, where `threadKey = useMemo(() => threadFromUrl ?? \`web-\${Date.now()}\`)`is the same value`useChat()`was initialized with — so the moment`reloadChats()`lands the row,`existingChat`resolves and`displayTitle`follows it, no refresh required. Added`router.replace(\`/app/chat?thread=\${threadKey}\` as Route)`inside the existing «new chat created» effect (the one that already calls`appData.reloadChats()`once`chat.chatId`shows up); the URL now mirrors the durable`threadKey`so a hard refresh / copied URL keeps the user on the same conversation, and`prevChatIdRef`keeps the replace from running more than once per session. The`loadHistory` effect (`useEffect(() => { if (existingChat?.chat.id) chat.loadHistory(...) }, [existingChat?.chat.id])`) was hardened with `if (existingChat.chat.id === chat.chatId) return;`— the chat we just created in this session already has its messages in memory and a live stream feeding it, so reloading history would race the stream and clobber it. Switching threads still triggers history load because`useChat(threadKey)`resets`chat.chatId`to`null`on threadKey change, so the equality breaks and`loadHistory`runs as before. **(2) Premium`send*failed`indicator.** The previous failed-send UI in`apps/web/app/app/\_components/chat-message.tsx` rendered \_inside* the user bubble: the message text on top, then a row with `AlertCircle` + «Не доставлено» in red, then a second row with chip-style buttons (`<RefreshCw>` Retry + `<X>` Cancel, each with `rounded-md px-1.5 py-0.5` chrome and `hover:bg-surface-hover`), all stacked inside the same `bg-accent/15 rounded-2xl` capsule. Founder called it «не дорого, всё смешано внутри бабла». The bubble was also accompanied by a redundant «Сообщение не ушло. Повтори или отмени, чтобы отправить новое.» banner directly above the composer (`apps/web/app/app/_components/chat-input.tsx:sendBlockedByFailedSlot && <div className="mb-2 ... border-destructive/20 bg-destructive/5">`), which doubled the noise. Fix: split the user-bubble layout into `wrapper (flex flex-col items-end gap-1) → bubble (bg-accent/15 rounded-2xl ...) + meta-row` so the failed indicator becomes a sibling of the bubble, not a child. The new meta-row is a single muted line under the bubble: `[1.5 px destructive dot] Не доставлено · Повторить · Отменить` — 11 px text, `text-text-subtle` for the middle-dot separators, `text-destructive/85` only on the dot + label, text-only buttons (`<button type="button" className="cursor-pointer font-medium text-text-muted underline-offset-4 transition-colors hover:text-text hover:underline">`) that surface an underline on hover. No icons, no rectangles, no `bg-`/`border-` chrome at all — reads as «just metadata», matches the same warm, quiet, premium language as the chat header's deep-mode subtitle, the assistant-card cog hint, and the Sparkles premium-mode badge. The bubble itself now dims to `opacity-80` when the message is in `send_failed` (the dim is on the bubble, not on its content paragraph — the previous `whitespace-pre-wrap ... break-words opacity-80` lived inside `<p>`, which combined badly with the inner buttons; pushing the dim up one level removes the «opacity inside opacity» feel and keeps text legible). The redundant `failedHelper` banner above the composer is deleted entirely; the new under-bubble meta-row already says «Не доставлено · Повторить · Отменить» right next to the offending message, so a second helper banner was pure noise. The `sendBlockedByFailedSlot` _logic_ (blocking sends until the failed slot is resolved, dimming the composer at `opacity-90`, gating Enter-to-send) stays exactly as it was — only the visible banner is gone. Removed unused `AlertCircle` and `X` icon imports from `chat-message.tsx`, and the now-unused `AlertCircle` import + `tSend = useTranslations("send")` binding from `chat-input.tsx` (its only call site was the deleted banner). The `send.failedHelper` translation key is intentionally left in place in `messages/{ru,en}.json` — harmless and cheaper to keep than to remove + re-add later if a banner-style helper turns out to be useful elsewhere. **Files touched.** `apps/web/app/app/chat/page.tsx` (existingChat lookup by `threadKey`, `router.replace` URL mirror, loadHistory race guard), `apps/web/app/app/_components/chat-message.tsx` (bubble/meta split, new under-bubble failed row, icon imports trimmed), `apps/web/app/app/_components/chat-input.tsx` (removed `failedHelper` banner, trimmed `AlertCircle` + `tSend` imports), `docs/SESSION-HANDOFF.md` (matching session entry), `docs/CHANGELOG.md` (this entry). **Verification gate.** `corepack pnpm -r --if-present run lint` clean, `corepack pnpm run format:check` clean, `corepack pnpm --filter @persai/web run typecheck` clean. No new tests — pure presentation slice with no contract / state-machine / wire-format change; existing component tests re-render through the unchanged props. **Out of scope (deliberate).** No architecture / API / data-model change; ADR-072 / ADR-073 / ADR-074 / ADR-075 / ADR-076 are unaffected. The mobile shell does not need a `cap sync` — all changes live in the web origin loaded over the existing `server.url` contract. **Commit posture.** Changes left uncommitted in the working tree, alongside the prior pre-launch UI polish residue (Telegram-style attachment menu, assistant-card cog, chat-row kebab portal escape) and the still-uncommitted ADR-076 Batch A + Batch B residue, all queued for the next batched commit.

- **Pre-launch UI polish 2026 (continued) — Telegram-style attachment tiles popover above the composer (founder ask 2026-04-25 «Смотри есть скрепка в чате и для mob версии нужно сделать так при клике появляется над полем ввода карточка в нашем стиле внутри 3 квадрата красивые скруг как у нас первый это фото второй это галерея а третий это файл - вложение»; presentational slice on `apps/web` only, no architecture / API / data-model change; verification gate green):** the paperclip in the chat composer no longer opens the OS file picker directly — tapping it now opens a small Telegram-style three-tile popover sitting right above the input row, matching the rest of the new "quiet but premium" UI language and giving the user one tap to choose between Camera / Photos / File instead of having to navigate inside a single context-less file dialog. **Trigger button.** `apps/web/app/app/_components/chat-input.tsx` paperclip got `aria-haspopup="menu"` + `aria-expanded={attachMenuOpen}`, a new `attachTriggerRef` so click-outside can exclude the trigger itself, and a "pressed" visual state when the menu is open (`bg-surface-hover text-text-muted`). The button no longer calls `fileInputRef.current?.click()` directly; it toggles the new `attachMenuOpen` state. **Popover anchored to the composer.** The composer row (the `<div>` with `flex items-end gap-2 rounded-2xl border bg-surface-raised`) got `relative` positioning so a new `motion.div` with `absolute bottom-full left-0 mb-2 w-full max-w-[18rem] rounded-2xl border border-border bg-surface-raised p-2 shadow-xl backdrop-blur-sm` can sit just above it. Anchoring inside the input row (rather than via `createPortal` to `document.body` like the chat-row kebab) is intentional: the chat input lives at the bottom of the viewport against the safe-area inset, so on mobile the on-screen keyboard never interacts with the popover, and the popover never has to be re-positioned on virtual-keyboard show/hide. **Three tiles, three input refs, one handler.** Inside the popover, a `grid grid-cols-3 gap-2` lays out three tiles via a new local `AttachTile` component (`aspect-square rounded-xl bg-surface ring-1 ring-border/40` in rest, `hover:bg-surface-hover hover:ring-accent/40` on interaction, with the icon warming to `text-accent` on `group-hover` — same warm easing language as the `AccountFooter` popup, the `Settings` cog affordance on the assistant card, and the `Sparkles` premium signal). The Camera tile triggers a new hidden `<input type="file" accept="image/*" capture="environment">` (so iOS / Android open the camera directly, no in-picker tab navigation; on desktop with no camera the OS file picker appears, which is the right fallback). The Photos tile triggers a new hidden `<input type="file" accept="image/*" multiple>` so the OS opens its native multi-select photo sheet. The File tile triggers the existing `<input type="file" multiple accept={CHAT_ATTACHMENT_ACCEPT}>`. All three inputs share the existing `handleFileChange` callback unchanged, so per-file validation (`isAcceptedChatFile` from `chat-file-policy.ts`), the `MAX_FILES = 5` cap, the pending-file pill row, the knowledge-base toggle for documents, the drag-drop and paste paths, and the voice-recording integration all continue to work — three new entry points all converge on the same `pendingFiles` state with no new state machine. **Animation + close behaviour.** `AnimatePresence` + `motion.div` with `initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 8, scale: 0.98 }}` → `animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0, scale: 1 }}` → matching exit, `duration: 0.18, ease: [0.22, 1, 0.36, 1]` (the warm 180 ms curve used elsewhere in the polish). Close fires on outside-click (both `mousedown` and `touchstart` listeners — needed because mobile Safari and Capacitor WebView don't synthesize `mousedown` for tap-on-document reliably), with the trigger button explicitly excluded so the second paperclip tap toggles cleanly without `mousedown` closing before `click` can re-open. Escape on document also closes. After tile-tap, the popover collapses and the actual OS picker is opened on `requestAnimationFrame` so the user perceives `tile press → menu collapse → picker raise` as one chained motion instead of two competing surfaces fighting for the same screen space. **Camera plugin not wired (deliberate).** `@capacitor/camera` is pre-installed (per ADR-075) but not adopted in this slice; `<input capture="environment">` already gives the right UX on both Android Chromium WebView and iOS WKWebView (one tap → camera, take shot → file lands in `pendingFiles`). The plugin will become attractive only when we want richer return shapes (e.g. controlled image editing before confirm), at which point the camera tile branch can be flipped behind `Capacitor.isNativePlatform()`. Live preview inside the camera tile is also explicitly out of scope today — adding it requires `getUserMedia` + permission prompts on web (with the prompt firing on menu-open, which is shouty), or `@capacitor-community/camera-preview` (a separate plugin from `@capacitor/camera`) plus iOS `WKWebViewConfiguration.allowsInlineMediaPlayback`, plus new `Info.plist` / `AndroidManifest.xml` permission strings, plus a `cap sync` + APK rebuild, plus a per-platform founder gate. Founder confirmed the staged plan: tile UI + native pickers now, live preview as a separate slice if it turns out to be needed. **i18n.** New `chat.attachMenuCamera` (ru `"Камера"` / en `"Camera"`), `chat.attachMenuPhotos` (ru `"Галерея"` / en `"Photos"`), `chat.attachMenuFile` (ru `"Файл"` / en `"File"`) for the tile labels. `chat.attachFile` is preserved as the paperclip button's `title=` and the popover's `aria-label`, so screen readers still hear "Прикрепить файл" / "Attach file" when the menu opens. **Type fix.** `KeyboardEvent` was already imported as a React type at the top of `chat-input.tsx` (for the textarea `handleKeyDown`), so the new document-level `keydown` listener inside the popover effect had to use `globalThis.KeyboardEvent` to disambiguate the DOM type — otherwise `tsc --noEmit` rejected the listener as `KeyboardEvent<Element>` instead of the global one. **Files touched.** `apps/web/app/app/_components/chat-input.tsx` (new `attachMenuOpen` state, `cameraInputRef` / `photosInputRef` / `attachMenuRef` / `attachTriggerRef` refs, outside-click + Escape effect, `pickFromTile` helper, three hidden `<input>`s, popover JSX, new local `AttachTile` component), `apps/web/messages/ru.json` (three new chat keys), `apps/web/messages/en.json` (three new chat keys), `docs/SESSION-HANDOFF.md` (matching session entry), `docs/CHANGELOG.md` (this entry). **Verification gate.** `corepack pnpm -r --if-present run lint` clean (5 of 5 lint-bearing workspace projects), `corepack pnpm run format:check` clean, `corepack pnpm --filter @persai/web run typecheck` clean (after the `globalThis.KeyboardEvent` fix), `corepack pnpm --filter @persai/api run typecheck` clean. No new tests — pure presentation slice with no contract / state-machine / wire-format change; existing component tests re-render through the unchanged `pendingFiles` API. **Out of scope (deliberate).** No architecture / API / data-model change; ADR-072 / ADR-073 / ADR-074 / ADR-075 / ADR-076 are unaffected. No `cap sync` — pure web change loaded over the existing `server.url` contract; the mobile shell sees it on next page load. No `@capacitor/camera` adoption (see "Camera plugin not wired" above). No live camera preview (see same). No multi-shot capture in the camera tile (single photo per tap, by `<input capture>` semantics; multi-photo flows go through the Photos tile). **Commit posture.** Changes left uncommitted in the working tree, alongside the prior pre-launch UI polish residue (assistant-card cog + chat-row kebab portal escape) and the still-uncommitted ADR-076 Batch A + Batch B residue, all queued for the next batched commit.

- **ADR-076 Batch B — Slice 5 (skeleton contracts) + Slice 6 (slide-over code-splitting + bundle audit) (founder ask 2026-04-25 «далее» on top of the standing batched-slice authorisation; `apps/web` only; verification gate green; awaiting founder live `persai-dev` gate):** Batch B finalises the program by replacing the surviving global loading state with targeted shimmers and lazy-loading the two heaviest slide-overs out of the initial route bundle, in one coherent slice with one founder gate. **Slice 5 — `useAppData` flag split.** `apps/web/app/app/_components/use-app-data.ts:AppData` now distinguishes three orthogonal pending states: `isLoading` is reserved exclusively for the cold-start fan-out (`loadAll()` started without a resolved assistant, i.e. SSR seeding failed), `isReloading` is true only during explicit `reload()` after the initial cold start has resolved (the path used by assistant-mutation onUpdated callbacks), and `isReloadingChats` is true only while `reloadChats()` is in flight. The implementation gate inside `loadAll()` is `if (!assistantResolved) setIsLoading(true); else setIsReloading(true);` — so a settings save triggering `appData.reload()` no longer flashes `isLoading=true` and never flips the sidebar into a global-skeleton state. The cold-start `useEffect(loadAll, [initialData])` only fires when `initialData === null` (degraded SSR path), keeping the seeded path silent. **Slice 5 — sidebar shimmer.** `apps/web/app/app/_components/sidebar.tsx` deletes the previous `<Loader2 className="h-5 w-5 animate-spin">` global spinner and introduces a new internal `ChatListSkeleton` component (3 ghost rows with widths `[72, 60, 80]%`, descending opacity `1.00 / 0.82 / 0.64`, `aria-hidden="true"`, `data-testid="chat-list-skeleton"`, the row body using `animate-pulse rounded bg-surface-raised`). The skeleton fires on a strict two-pronged condition: `data.isLoading || (data.isReloadingChats && chatGroups.length === 0)`. So in normal SSR-seeded flow the skeleton never appears at all; it only surfaces if cold-start fan-out actually had to run, or if the user just emptied their chat list (e.g. deleted their last chat) and `reloadChats` is still in flight. Non-empty lists keep all rows visible during reloads — no flash, no flicker. **Slice 6 — `next/dynamic` for slide-overs.** `apps/web/app/app/_components/app-shell.tsx` switches from `import { AssistantSettings } from "./assistant-settings"` and `import { TelegramConnect } from "./telegram-connect"` to two `next/dynamic(() => import("..."), { ssr: false })` factories at module scope (each calls `.then((m) => ({ default: m.<Named> }))` because the source modules use named exports). The actual chunk fetch is gated by two new sticky `useState` flags `hasOpenedSettings` / `hasOpenedTelegram`, set to `true` via `useEffect` the first time `settingsOpen` / `telegramOpen` becomes `true` and never reset thereafter. Inside each `<SlideOver>`, the dynamic-loaded child is rendered as `{hasOpenedSettings && <AssistantSettings ... />}` (and the same for Telegram) — so the chunk is fetched on first open, the component stays mounted across subsequent close/reopen cycles (preserving form state and letting `<SlideOver>`'s framer-motion exit animation play out cleanly), and on the very first paint of `/app` the heavy bodies are simply not in the DOM. **Slice 6 — measured impact.** Production build via Next.js 16.2.1 + Turbopack: the per-route `apps/web/.next/server/app/app/page/react-loadable-manifest.json` now points at 3 lazy chunks for `/app` totalling **78,726 bytes (~76.9 KiB)** (`0eaa625blo6u..js` 5,876 B + `05.y3y~dhm00p.js` 49,141 B + `0.2xbfdltn0v4.js` 23,709 B); these chunks previously lived in the initial-route main bundle. Total `apps/web/.next/static/chunks` count went 49 → 53 (+4 chunks at +8,767 bytes due to the next/dynamic loader scaffolding) but per-route initial JS dropped by ~76.9 KiB. The lazy chunks are fetched only when the user actually opens Settings or Telegram. **Slice 6 — bundle audit recorded.** `lucide-react` usage was audited across all 32 call sites (`apps/web/app/app/_components/*.tsx`, `apps/web/app/admin/*.tsx`, `apps/web/app/{sign-in,sign-up,sso-callback,page}.tsx`) — every site uses named imports (`import { X } from "lucide-react"`); zero namespace imports (`import * as`) anywhere in the tree. Tree-shaking remains intact, no action needed. `framer-motion` is used in 7 files: `app-shell.tsx` (mobile sidebar overlay with spring physics — kept; CSS replacement loses `damping/stiffness` feel), `sidebar.tsx` (account popup `<AnimatePresence>` enter/exit — kept; CSS would need a state-machine to time the unmount), `slide-over.tsx` (panel slide + dim with `<AnimatePresence>` — kept; same lifecycle reason), `chat-message.tsx` (sending indicator delayed entry — kept), `setup/page.tsx` (wizard transitions — kept). Per-site decision: **keep all `framer-motion` use**, because each site relies on either spring physics or `<AnimatePresence>` enter/exit lifecycle which CSS-only replacements can't cleanly replicate, and the bundle gain from removing them is small compared to the 76.9 KiB recovered by lazy-loading the slide-over bodies. **Tests.** New `apps/web/app/app/_components/sidebar.test.tsx` covers the five shimmer paths: cold-start `isLoading=true` shows skeleton, `isReloadingChats=true && chats=[]` shows skeleton, `isReloadingChats=true && chats.length>0` keeps existing rows (no skeleton), idle empty list shows the `startFirst` empty-state copy (no skeleton), `isReloading=true && isReloadingChats=false` does not flash the skeleton even with chats present. Test mocks updated to thread the new flags through: `apps/web/app/app/_components/assistant-settings.test.tsx:makeAppData` adds `isReloading: false, isReloadingChats: false`; `apps/web/app/app/chat/page.test.tsx:appDataMocks` adds the same. **Verification gate green** — `corepack pnpm -r --if-present run lint` clean (5 of 5 lint-bearing workspace projects), `corepack pnpm run format:check` clean (the new `sidebar.test.tsx` was prettier-fixed during the slice and re-checked), `corepack pnpm --filter @persai/web run typecheck` clean, `corepack pnpm --filter @persai/api run typecheck` clean (Prisma generate + `tsc --noEmit`), `corepack pnpm --filter @persai/web run test` 110/110 (was 105/105; the new sidebar suite contributes 5 of those tests), `corepack pnpm --filter @persai/api run test` 0 failed (Batch B touched only `apps/web` so api-side passes unchanged). **Files touched.** `apps/web/app/app/_components/use-app-data.ts` (AppData interface gains `isReloading`/`isReloadingChats`; `loadAll()` gates on `assistantResolved`; `reloadChats` toggles its flag in a try/finally), `apps/web/app/app/_components/sidebar.tsx` (skeleton swap-in + new `ChatListSkeleton` internal component), `apps/web/app/app/_components/app-shell.tsx` (dynamic imports + sticky open flags + `useEffect`-driven first-open latch + conditional child mount), `apps/web/app/app/_components/sidebar.test.tsx` (new), `apps/web/app/app/_components/assistant-settings.test.tsx` (mock fields), `apps/web/app/app/chat/page.test.tsx` (mock fields), `docs/ADR/076-cold-start-visual-continuity-and-bootstrap-pipeline.md` (Status block flipped to "Slices 1, 2, Batch A (3+4) and Batch B (5+6) landed; Slice 7 pending"; ledger rows 5 + 6 flipped from `proposed` to `landed` with full descriptions; `Updated:` line carries the new state), `docs/CHANGELOG.md` (this entry), `docs/SESSION-HANDOFF.md` (matching session entry). **Out of scope (deliberate, ADR-076 §"Out of scope across the whole program").** No SSR caching of authenticated app routes, no transitional dual-mode keeping the old `<Loader2>` spinner alive alongside the skeleton, no `<ImageLightbox>` or `<VoiceMessagePlayer>` lazy-loading (deeper-nested components that already render `null` when closed; their bytes are smaller and the gain is marginal — flagged as a follow-up if a Slice 7 audit reveals it as a bottleneck), no `framer-motion`-to-CSS rewrite of any individual call site (per the audit decision above), no Prisma migration (Slice 5/6 are presentational + bundle-only). **Commit posture.** Per founder rule «комит только в конце ADR» — the working tree stays uncommitted and now carries Slice 1 + Section M + Slice 2a + Slice 2b + Batch A + Batch B residue, all queued for the end-of-ADR-076 batch commit. Slice 7 (Service-Worker PWA shell) remains conditional and will be evaluated against a measured production baseline before any decision to ship. **Awaiting** founder live `persai-dev` gate covering: (a) cold load of `/app` shows sidebar populated in the first paint with no spinner / skeleton flash; (b) deleting the last chat in the sidebar shows a brief 2–3 row shimmer in place of the empty state during the in-flight `reloadChats`, then resolves to the `startFirst` copy; (c) DevTools Network shows `assistant-settings` and `telegram-connect` chunks fetched only on first open of their respective slide-overs (not on initial `/app` paint); (d) opening Settings, closing it, and re-opening it reuses the cached chunk (no second download) and preserves any unsaved input.

- **Pre-launch UI polish 2026 (continued) — assistant-card cog affordance + chat-row kebab portal escape (founder asks 2026-04-25: «карточка асистента не понятно что можно нажать может как то обыграть либо ... либо премиальная щестеренка», «когда много чатов и появляется скролл при клике на .. у чата выпадает меню с действиями оно внутри и скрывается в поле - нужно показать поверх»; presentational slice on `apps/web` only, no architecture / API / data-model change; verification gate green):** two scoped defects in the redesigned sidebar that surfaced after the bento polish landed are fixed in a single slice. **(1) Assistant card click affordance.** The card at the top of the sidebar (avatar + assistant name + status pill in `apps/web/app/app/_components/sidebar.tsx:Sidebar`) opens the assistant-settings slide-over on click, but in the new "quiet UI" warm tonal palette there was nothing visible signalling that the whole row is a button — founder offered «... либо премиальная шестерёнка», and the cog wins because it reads as "settings", which is exactly what the click does. The card's `<button>` is now a `group` with `aria-label={t("assistantSettingsHint")}` and a matching native `title=` (so screen readers and desktop hover tooltips both name the action). A new trailing `<span>` renders a `lucide-react` `Settings` cog (`h-3.5 w-3.5`) with `text-text-subtle/40` in the resting state and `group-hover:text-accent-premium group-hover:bg-surface` on hover — the default tone keeps the card visually calm (the cog reads as a faint hint, not a competing CTA against the active chat row directly below it), and on hover it warms up to the same premium gold tone the chat list (`Sparkles` deep-mode badge) and chat header (deep-mode subtitle) already use, tying the premium signal language together. The inner name/status block is now `flex-1` so the cog rides on `ml-1 shrink-0` at the right edge without forcing the assistant name to truncate prematurely. New i18n string `sidebar.assistantSettingsHint`: ru `"Настройки ассистента"` / en `"Assistant settings"`. **(2) Chat-row kebab dropdown portal escape.** The kebab dropdown (rename / archive / delete) in `ChatListItem` was positioned `absolute right-1 top-full` relative to the chat row. The chat list sits inside `flex-1 overflow-y-auto` (the sidebar's only scrollable region), which clips any descendant that paints outside its content box — so once the chat list scrolled and the kebab was opened on a row near the bottom of the visible viewport, the dropdown was visually cut off **inside** the scroll container instead of floating above it. Fix: `createPortal` is now imported from `react-dom` at the module top; `ChatListItem` got a new `kebabRef: useRef<HTMLSpanElement>` attached to the kebab span plus a `menuPos: { top: number; right: number } | null` state holding the dropdown's viewport-anchored fixed coordinates. Two named callbacks replace the old inline toggle: `openMenu()` reads `kebabRef.current.getBoundingClientRect()`, computes `spaceBelow = window.innerHeight - rect.bottom`, flips the menu **above** the row when `spaceBelow < MENU_H_EST + 16` (with `MENU_H_EST = 132` covering rename + archive + divider + delete + padding), and writes `top` / `right` such that the menu's right edge aligns with the kebab's right edge (`right: window.innerWidth - rect.right`). Both axes get a min-clamp of `8` px so the menu never glues to the viewport edge. `closeMenu()` resets `menuOpen` and `confirmDelete` together so a re-open never reveals the stale "Confirm delete" affirmative state. The mousedown click-outside handler now checks both `menuRef.current.contains(target)` **and** `kebabRef.current.contains(target)` — without the second check, mousedown would close the menu before the kebab's click-toggle could re-open it on the same gesture, producing a confused "stays open by accident" state. While the menu is open, capture-phase scroll (`window.addEventListener("scroll", closeMenu, true)`) and `resize` listeners auto-close it the moment the user scrolls under it; capture is mandatory because the chat list's own `overflow-y-auto` does not bubble scroll. The dropdown JSX is wrapped in `typeof document !== "undefined" && createPortal(<div … style={{ position: "fixed", top: menuPos.top, right: menuPos.right }} … />, document.body)` so it always paints above all sidebar chrome regardless of which row was the anchor. The kebab `<span>` got `aria-haspopup="menu"` + `aria-expanded={menuOpen}` and a keyboard handler that responds to `Enter` and `Space` (with `preventDefault` on Space so the page doesn't scroll). **Files touched.** `apps/web/app/app/_components/sidebar.tsx` (the `Sidebar` assistant card cog + group-hover wiring; `ChatListItem` portal dropdown, fixed positioning, auto-flip, scroll/resize close, kebab keyboard a11y), `apps/web/messages/ru.json` (added `sidebar.assistantSettingsHint`), `apps/web/messages/en.json` (added `sidebar.assistantSettingsHint`), `docs/SESSION-HANDOFF.md` (matching session entry), `docs/CHANGELOG.md` (this entry). **Verification gate.** `corepack pnpm -r --if-present run lint` clean (5 of 5 lint-bearing workspace projects), `corepack pnpm run format:check` clean, `corepack pnpm --filter @persai/web run typecheck` clean, `corepack pnpm --filter @persai/api run typecheck` clean. No new tests — pure presentation slice with no contract / state-machine / wire-format change; existing component tests re-render through the unchanged props. **Out of scope (deliberate).** No architecture / API / data-model change; ADR-072 / ADR-073 / ADR-074 / ADR-075 / ADR-076 are unaffected. The mobile shell does not need a `cap sync` — all changes live in the web origin loaded over the existing `server.url` contract. **Commit posture.** Changes left uncommitted in the working tree, alongside the prior pre-launch UI polish residue and the still-uncommitted ADR-076 Batch A residue, all queued for the next batched commit.

- **ADR-076 Batch A — Slice 3 (RSC bootstrap) + Slice 4 (cookie-auth versioned avatar pipeline) (founder ask 2026-04-25 «Далее» on top of the standing batched-slice authorisation; `apps/api` + `apps/web`; verification gate green; awaiting founder live `persai-dev` gate):** the cold-start client fan-out and the bearer-fetched-blob avatar pipeline are both replaced in a single coherent slice — the lifecycle envelope from Slice 4 ships through the bootstrap envelope from Slice 3 so they share one orval-regenerate cycle and one founder gate, no transitional dual-mode shape on either surface. **Slice 3 — single-batch web bootstrap.** `apps/api` adds `GET /api/v1/app/bootstrap` (bearer-protected via the existing Clerk middleware): new `apps/api/src/modules/workspace-management/application/get-assistant-app-bootstrap.service.ts:GetAssistantAppBootstrapService` injects the six already-existing application services (`GetAssistantByUserIdService`, `ManageWebChatListService`, `ResolveTelegramIntegrationStateService`, `ResolveAssistantNotificationPreferenceService`, `ResolvePlanVisibilityService.{getUserVisibility,getAdminVisibility}`) and runs them in parallel via `Promise.allSettled`, returning `{ requestId, sections: { assistant, chats, telegram, notificationPreference, plan, admin } }` where each section is a tagged union `{ ok: true, data } | { ok: false, error: { code, category, message } }`. `classifyError` maps `UnauthorizedException → category:"auth"`, `ForbiddenException → "forbidden"`, `NotFoundException → "validation"`, `Error → "infra"`, anything else → `"unknown"`, so a non-admin's `getAdminVisibility` rejection (which throws `UnauthorizedException` by design) renders as `admin: { ok: false, error: { category: "auth" } }` and the rest of the response stays usable. New `apps/api/src/modules/workspace-management/interface/http/app-bootstrap.controller.ts:AppBootstrapController` exposes the endpoint at `@Controller("api/v1/app")` + `@Get("bootstrap")` and delegates to the service after resolving `req.resolvedAppUser.id`. Module wiring lives in `apps/api/src/modules/workspace-management/workspace-management.module.ts` (controller in the `controllers` array, service in `providers`). **Slice 3 — `apps/web` RSC layout.** `apps/web/app/app/layout.tsx` is now `async function AppLayout({ children })` that calls a new server-only helper `apps/web/app/app/_server/fetch-app-bootstrap.ts:fetchAppBootstrap()` (marked `import "server-only"` to keep it out of client bundles). The helper resolves the Clerk session via `auth()` from `@clerk/nextjs/server`, obtains a server-side bearer token via `session.getToken()`, and `fetch`es the upstream `apps/api` bootstrap endpoint directly (not through the local `/api/v1/[[...path]]` proxy) with `cache: "no-store"`; failures (no session, `getToken()` throw, network error, non-200, JSON parse error) are mapped into a structured `AppBootstrapInitialData` with appropriate per-section error states so the UI never crashes on bootstrap failure. The resolved data flows into `<AppShell initialData={...}>`. **Slice 3 — `useAppData` seeded from SSR.** `apps/web/app/app/_components/use-app-data.ts:useAppData(initialData)` now seeds its state synchronously from the bootstrap envelope when present (`isLoading: false`, all sections populated, `assistantResolved: true`) and only fires the six per-endpoint client calls in a `useEffect` when `initialData === null` (degraded SSR path). `app-shell.tsx` accepts `initialData` and forwards it. The per-endpoint client wrappers in `assistant-api-client.ts` are intentionally preserved as the inputs for `reload()` / `reloadChats()` after mutations — the new bootstrap endpoint is for cold start only, not for refresh paths. **Slice 4 — content-addressed avatar URL.** `apps/api/src/modules/workspace-management/application/manage-assistant-avatar.service.ts` introduces `buildAssistantAvatarUrl(buffer, mimeType): "/api/avatar/<hash>.<ext>"` (16-char SHA-256 prefix + extension from `MIME_TO_EXT` table for `image/{png,jpeg,jpg,webp,gif,avif}`, falling back to `"bin"`) and `extractAvatarHashFromUrl(url): string | null` (returns the hash component when the URL matches the new prefix and `[a-f0-9]{8,64}` shape, else `null`). `ManageAssistantAvatarService.upload` now stamps `draftAvatarUrl` with the content-addressed URL instead of the legacy absolute URL. New `ManageAssistantAvatarService.downloadByHash(userId, hash)` resolves the assistant's current `draftAvatarUrl`, extracts its hash via `extractAvatarHashFromUrl`, and returns `null` when the request hash doesn't match — so a stale CDN entry / out-of-date BFF call never leaks bytes. **Slice 4 — internal hash-validated read endpoint.** `apps/api/src/modules/workspace-management/interface/http/assistant.controller.ts` removes the legacy public `GET /assistant/avatar` and adds bearer-protected `GET /assistant/avatar/:hash` that calls `downloadByHash` and returns 404 on mismatch / 200 with `Cache-Control: private, max-age=31536000, immutable` + `ETag: "<hash>"` + `Content-Type` headers on success. The `buildAbsoluteAssistantAvatarUrl` helper is deleted (no consumers left after the lifecycle flip). **Slice 4 — lifecycle envelope sanitisation.** `apps/api/src/modules/workspace-management/application/assistant-lifecycle.mapper.ts` introduces `sanitizeAvatarUrl(rawAvatarUrl)` that returns `null` for any URL that doesn't start with `/api/avatar/` — applied to both `draft.avatarUrl` and `latestPublishedVersion.snapshot.avatarUrl`. Legacy absolute URLs persisted in dev databases are returned as `null` so the UI shows the emoji avatar until re-uploaded; no transitional dual-mode shape, no Prisma backfill needed. **Slice 4 — `apps/web` BFF route + thin avatar component.** New `apps/web/app/api/avatar/[hash]/route.ts` is a Next.js Route Handler under the App Router with `runtime: "nodejs"` + `dynamic: "force-dynamic"`: validates the `:hash` param shape (`^([a-f0-9]{8,64})(?:\.[a-z0-9]+)?$`), authenticates via `auth()` + `session.getToken()` (cookie session → bearer token), fetches `/assistant/avatar/:hash` from `apps/api` server-side, propagates 404 / non-200 statuses, and on success streams `upstreamResponse.body` back with `Cache-Control: private, max-age=31536000, immutable` + `ETag: "<hash>"` + `Content-Type` from upstream. Browsers/CDNs cache by URL, so a fresh upload (new hash → new URL) is automatically cache-busted. `apps/web/app/app/_components/assistant-avatar.tsx` collapses from ~100 lines (with `useAuth().getToken()`, `fetch + blob + URL.createObjectURL`, `useEffect`, and `AVATAR_BLOB_CACHE`) to a thin presentational component: `<img src={avatarUrl} loading="lazy">` when `avatarUrl` is non-null, emoji fallback span when only `avatarEmoji` is present, `Sparkles` icon otherwise. **OpenAPI + orval regen.** `packages/contracts/openapi.yaml` adds the `GET /app/bootstrap` path entry, the `GetAppBootstrapResponse` schema, the per-section `AppBootstrap{Assistant,Chats,Telegram,NotificationPreference,Plan,Admin}Section` schemas, the shared `BootstrapSectionError` schema (with `category: "auth" | "forbidden" | "validation" | "infra" | "unknown"`), the `AppBootstrapSectionsState` envelope, and a new `AssistantNotificationPreferenceState` schema (modelled from the existing TS type since the per-endpoint route was previously a bare fetch). `assistantDraftState.avatarUrl` and `assistantPublishedVersionSnapshotState.avatarUrl` descriptions now document the content-addressed URL format and the legacy-URL → `null` sanitisation. Orval clients regenerated via `corepack pnpm --filter @persai/contracts run generate`; `packages/contracts/src/generated/**` is checked in and prettier-formatted. **Tests.** New `apps/api/test/get-assistant-app-bootstrap.service.test.ts` covers three paths against in-process service fakes: happy path (all six sections `ok: true`), partial-failure path (`NotFoundException` on assistant ⇒ `category:"validation",code:"not_found"`; `UnauthorizedException` on admin ⇒ `category:"auth",code:"auth_required"`; remaining sections succeed), and infra-class errors (raw `Error("...")` ⇒ `category:"infra"` with the error's message; non-Error rejection like `throw "string-error"` ⇒ `category:"unknown"`). New `apps/api/test/manage-assistant-avatar.service.test.ts` covers `buildAssistantAvatarUrl` for png / jpeg / mixed-case mime / unknown mime fallback to `bin` and `extractAvatarHashFromUrl` for null / legacy absolute URL / new format with extension / new format without extension / non-hex hash that should be rejected. New `apps/api/test/assistant-lifecycle-avatar-sanitizer.test.ts` covers the mapper's `sanitizeAvatarUrl` flow through both `toAssistantLifecycleState` (draft path) and `toAssistantPublishedVersionState` (published-snapshot path) for legacy-URL → `null` and content-addressed URL → passthrough. **Verification gate green** — `corepack pnpm -r --if-present run lint` clean (5 of 5 lint-bearing workspace projects), `corepack pnpm run format:check` clean (initially flagged the regenerated orval output + the new files; `prettier --write` brought them in line, second `format:check` returns clean), `corepack pnpm --filter @persai/api run typecheck` clean (Prisma generate + `tsc --noEmit`), `corepack pnpm --filter @persai/web run typecheck` clean (`tsc --noEmit`), `corepack pnpm --filter @persai/api run test` 0 failed (every node test suite exits with `# fail 0` including the three new files), `corepack pnpm --filter @persai/web run test` 105/105 passed (existing AssistantAvatar / AppShell / chat-area / chat-message tests transparently re-render through the simplified component thanks to the unchanged prop interface). **Files touched** (this slice): `apps/api/src/modules/workspace-management/application/get-assistant-app-bootstrap.service.ts` (new), `apps/api/src/modules/workspace-management/interface/http/app-bootstrap.controller.ts` (new), `apps/api/src/modules/workspace-management/workspace-management.module.ts` (controller + provider wiring), `apps/api/src/modules/workspace-management/application/manage-assistant-avatar.service.ts` (content-addressed URL helpers + `downloadByHash`), `apps/api/src/modules/workspace-management/application/assistant-lifecycle.mapper.ts` (`sanitizeAvatarUrl`), `apps/api/src/modules/workspace-management/interface/http/assistant.controller.ts` (legacy `GET /avatar` removed, new bearer-protected `GET /avatar/:hash`), `apps/api/test/get-assistant-app-bootstrap.service.test.ts` (new), `apps/api/test/manage-assistant-avatar.service.test.ts` (new), `apps/api/test/assistant-lifecycle-avatar-sanitizer.test.ts` (new), `apps/web/app/app/layout.tsx` (async RSC), `apps/web/app/app/_server/fetch-app-bootstrap.ts` (new server-only helper), `apps/web/app/app/_components/app-shell.tsx` (`initialData` prop), `apps/web/app/app/_components/use-app-data.ts` (seed-from-initialData path), `apps/web/app/app/_components/assistant-avatar.tsx` (collapsed to `<img>`), `apps/web/app/api/avatar/[hash]/route.ts` (new BFF route), `packages/contracts/openapi.yaml` (new `/app/bootstrap` path + schemas + avatar URL doc updates), `packages/contracts/src/generated/**` (orval regen), `docs/ADR/076-cold-start-visual-continuity-and-bootstrap-pipeline.md` (Status block updated, Slice 3 + Slice 4 ledger rows flipped from `proposed` to `landed`, `Updated:` line carries the new state), scope (deliberate, ADR-076 §"Out of scope across the whole program").** No SSR caching of authenticated app routes (the bootstrap response is `cache: "no-store"`). No transitional dual-mode that supports both the old and new avatar URL shape simultaneously — legacy absolute URLs sanitise to `null`, period. No transitional dual-mode that supports both the old client fan-out and the new bootstrap simultaneously. No Prisma migration (all changes ride existing columns; legacy `draft_avatar_url` rows remain untouched and degrade gracefully through `sanitizeAvatarUrl`). No change to the upload route (`POST /api/v1/assistant/avatar`); the bytes still land in the same object-storage path, only the recorded URL format changed. **Commit posture.** Per founder rule «комит только в конце ADR» — both repos' working trees stay uncommitted; the Batch A changes accumulate alongside the prior Slice 1 + Section M + Slice 2a + Slice 2b residue, all queued for the end-of-ADR-076 batch commit. **Awaiting** founder live `persai-dev` gate covering both targets at once: (a) cold load of `/app` shows sidebar + account footer + chat header populated in the first paint with no `isLoading=true → loaded` transition; (b) cold reload reuses the HTTP cache for the avatar (no JS-driven round-trip in DevTools Network), and a fresh upload produces a new content hash → new `/api/avatar/<hash>.<ext>` URL → fresh fetch on next paint; (c) a non-admin user's bootstrap still returns 200 with `admin.ok = false, admin.error.category = "auth"` and the rest of the surfaces populated.

- **ADR-076 Slice 2 (residual 2b) — Capacitor cold-start visual continuity (founder ask 2026-04-25 «делай»; `persai-mobile` only; PersAI repo verification gate green; awaiting `cap sync` + APK rebuild on `persai-mobile` + Z Fold 6 live cap-install gate; iOS rebuild gate deferred until founder runs an iOS build):** the residual half of ADR-076 Slice 2 lands so the entire native shell now hands a chrome-dark, system-bar-correct frame to the SSR-baked `apps/web` paint with no white frame, no missing-drawable fallback, and no out-of-tone iOS storyboard. **Android resource set.** New `persai-mobile/android/app/src/main/res/values/colors.xml` defines `chrome` (`#FF161513`) and `chrome_light` (`#FFE0D8C8`), anchored in code comments to the `--chrome` token in `apps/web/app/globals.css` and the `CHROME_DARK` / `CHROME_LIGHT` constants in `com/persai/app/SystemBarsBridge.java` so all three move together on any future palette change. New `persai-mobile/android/app/src/main/res/drawable/splash_logo.xml` is a four-pointed PersAI sparkle vector (24-unit viewport scaled to 192dp, `fillColor=@color/chrome_light`) — replaces the missing `@drawable/splash` placeholder previously referenced by `AppTheme.NoActionBarLaunch`. Geometry mirrors the in-app `Sparkles` glyph used by `AssistantAvatar` fallback / premium callouts / the landing page hero, so the cold-start frame is visually continuous with the first React paint. **Android launch theme modernised.** `persai-mobile/android/app/src/main/res/values/styles.xml:AppTheme.NoActionBarLaunch` drops `<item name="android:background">@drawable/splash</item>` and now uses the `androidx.core.splashscreen` (already in `app/build.gradle` as `implementation "androidx.core:core-splashscreen:..."`) attribute set: `windowSplashScreenBackground=@color/chrome`, `windowSplashScreenAnimatedIcon=@drawable/splash_logo`, `postSplashScreenTheme=@style/AppTheme.NoActionBar` (so the moment the system splash dismisses the activity flips to the transparent post-theme that the WebView paints onto), plus `android:windowBackground=@color/chrome` as the pre-API-31 fallback (the project's `minSdk` is 24; Z Fold 6 itself is API 34 so the SplashScreen path is the hot one). The runtime system-bars bridge from Slice 2a (already landed) keeps pre-coloring the status / nav bars from `SharedPreferences` during the same window, so there is no visible discontinuity between the splash, the bars, and the WebView's first paint. **Capacitor container background.** `persai-mobile/capacitor.config.ts` adds `android.backgroundColor: "#161513"` and `ios.backgroundColor: "#161513"` (both `string`-typed in `@capacitor/cli@^8.3.1`'s `CapacitorConfig` declarations), so the WebView container itself starts in chrome dark and the moment between the launch theme and the first HTML byte is also chrome — no white frame anywhere on the cold-start path. The existing `server.url`, `allowNavigation`, `errorPath`, and `android.allowMixedContent` settings are unchanged. **iOS LaunchScreen rewrite.** `persai-mobile/ios/App/App/Base.lproj/LaunchScreen.storyboard` is rewritten from a single `imageView` referencing the `Splash` imageset (whose backing PNGs are not present in the working tree — `splash-2732x2732{,-1,-2}.png`) to a chrome-dark `UIView` containing a centered `UILabel` with text `PersAI`, system semibold 48pt, color `#E0D8C8` (chrome_light). Layout uses `centerX` / `centerY` constraints against the safe area; the label needs no asset catalog so the storyboard is fully self-contained and Xcode no longer chases the missing PNGs. The unused `persai-mobile/ios/App/App/Assets.xcassets/Splash.imageset/Contents.json` is rewritten to an empty info-only stub (`{ "info": { "version": 1, "author": "xcode" } }`) so the asset catalog compiler never tries to resolve the missing PNG references; the dormant imageset directory is left in place to avoid touching `project.pbxproj`. **Files touched.** `persai-mobile/android/app/src/main/res/values/colors.xml` (new), `persai-mobile/android/app/src/main/res/drawable/splash_logo.xml` (new), `persai-mobile/android/app/src/main/res/values/styles.xml` (modified — `AppTheme.NoActionBarLaunch` only; `AppTheme` and `AppTheme.NoActionBar` untouched), `persai-mobile/capacitor.config.ts` (modified — `android.backgroundColor` and `ios.backgroundColor` added), `persai-mobile/ios/App/App/Base.lproj/LaunchScreen.storyboard` (rewritten), `persai-mobile/ios/App/App/Assets.xcassets/Splash.imageset/Contents.json` (emptied), `docs/ADR/076-cold-start-visual-continuity-and-bootstrap-pipeline.md` (Slice 2 ledger row flipped from `partial` to `landed`; `Updated:` line and Status block carry the new state), `docs/CHANGELOG.md` (this entry), `docs/SESSION-HANDOFF.md` (matching session entry). **Verification gate.** PersAI repo gate (`corepack pnpm -r --if-present run lint`, `corepack pnpm run format:check`, `corepack pnpm --filter @persai/api run typecheck`, `corepack pnpm --filter @persai/web run typecheck`) was rerun and stays green; this slice does not touch any `apps/*` source so the existing Slice 1 + Section M green gate is preserved. The `persai-mobile` repo has no lint / typecheck pipeline of its own — the binary verification gate is `cap sync` + Android / iOS builds + the founder live device gate, all run by the founder. The `capacitor.config.ts` change is type-safe under `@capacitor/cli@^8.3.1`'s `CapacitorConfig` declarations (`android.backgroundColor?: string` since 1.1.0, `ios.backgroundColor?: string` since 1.1.0). **Out of scope (deliberate, ADR-076 §"Out of scope across the whole program").** No change to `apps/web` (Slice 1 already covers the SSR-baked theme that the splash now hands off to). No change to the system-bars bridge (Slice 2a already landed). No iOS-side `MainActivity`-equivalent additions for `installSplashScreen()` on pre-API-31 devices — the `android:windowBackground=@color/chrome` fallback in the launch theme covers them, and Z Fold 6 / modern devices use the API 31+ splash path that does not need the install call. No `values-night/styles.xml` light variant — Slice 2 stays one-tone (chrome dark) for the splash on every API level / OS night-mode combination, matching the brand default and the SharedPreferences default in Slice 2a (deferring the night-mode swap is explicitly allowed by ADR-076 §Slice 2 wording «if a light variant is desired»). No iOS Capacitor `installSplashScreen()` or `LaunchScreen` storyboard tooling change beyond the storyboard rewrite. No regeneration of app icons / launcher icons — `mipmap-anydpi-v26/ic_launcher{,_round}.xml` and `drawable/ic_launcher_background.xml` / `drawable-v24/ic_launcher_foreground.xml` stay as the AOSP template (separate concern from the launch theme; tracked outside this slice). **Commit posture.** Per founder rule «комит только в конце ADR» — both repos' working trees stay uncommitted; the persai-mobile changes accumulate alongside the unchanged Slice 2a residue (`MainActivity.java`, `SystemBarsBridge.java`) in `persai-mobile` and the Slice 1 + Section M residue in PersAI. **Awaiting** founder live cap-install gate on Z Fold 6: cold launch (fresh install) shows a chrome-dark frame from the very first frame through the splash logo to the SSR-baked dark `apps/web` paint with no visible white / light flash and no out-of-tone splash; cold launch in light mode still settles into the SSR-resolved light palette without flicker (cookie + client-hint path from Slice 1 covers the theme; the splash itself stays chrome-dark per the brand default). iOS cap-install gate is deferred until the founder runs an iOS build; the storyboard wordmark will read `PersAI` in chrome_light on chrome-dark and the WKWebView container will start chrome-dark.

- **ADR-076 Slice 1 — Cookie-as-truth theme with SSR-baked `<html class>` + Section M `sending`-indicator UX micro-fix (founder ask 2026-04-25 «делаем качественно без legsy и хвостов»; `apps/web` only; verification gate green; awaiting founder live `persai-dev` gate before Slice 2):** the `persai-theme` cookie becomes the authoritative source of theme (`system | light | dark`) with attributes `Max-Age=31536000`, `Path=/`, `SameSite=Lax`, `Secure` in production. **`apps/web/app/layout.tsx`** stays an async Server Component and now reads the cookie via `cookies()` from `next/headers` together with the `Sec-CH-Prefers-Color-Scheme` request header via `headers()`; `resolveServerTheme()` returns `"dark" | "light"` (cookie value if explicit, else hint, else dark default) and the resolved class is composed onto `<html className=…>` together with the Geist Sans/Mono variables; `style={{ colorScheme }}` is set on `<html>` so native scrollbars / form controls / autofill match the resolved palette in the very first byte of HTML. `<meta name="theme-color">` is now a single resolved value (`#161513` dark / `#e0d8c8` light) instead of the previous two-`media`-gated values, so the OS chrome / Capacitor system bar follow the in-app palette regardless of OS preference. `<meta http-equiv="Accept-CH" content="Sec-CH-Prefers-Color-Scheme">` is rendered into `<head>` to opt the document into the client hint; the previous `themeBootstrapScript` (which resolved theme on every load from `localStorage`) is **deleted** and replaced with a tiny `themeFallbackScript` that reads the cookie (NOT `localStorage`), resolves `system` against `matchMedia`, applies the `.light` class + `colorScheme`, syncs `<meta name="theme-color">`, and persists the choice as a cookie if absent — the documented first-visit-without-cookie path for iOS WKWebView and any browser that does not send the hint, not a parallel source of truth. **`apps/web/next.config.ts`** advertises `Accept-CH: Sec-CH-Prefers-Color-Scheme`, `Critical-CH: Sec-CH-Prefers-Color-Scheme`, and `Vary: Sec-CH-Prefers-Color-Scheme` on every response so the very first navigation already retries with the hint included on Chromium WebView (Capacitor Android) / Chrome / Edge, and proxies / CDNs do not collapse dark and light cache variants onto the same key. **`apps/web/app/app/_components/use-theme.ts`** is rewritten so the four synchronisation surfaces are updated atomically on every theme write: cookie (next request is server-resolved), `localStorage` mirror, `<html class>` + `style.colorScheme`, and `<meta name="theme-color">`. `readChoice()` now reads cookie first (authoritative) and falls back to `localStorage` only if the cookie was cleared; first-mount mirrors cookie → localStorage so the two surfaces never drift after the SSR bake. The OS-preference subscription (active while choice is `system`) updates surfaces 3 & 4 only — the cookie value stays `system`. The `<meta name="theme-color">` two-`media` shape and the `localStorage`-driven pre-hydration script are removed in the same change — no transitional/dual-mode bridge. **Section M (presentational micro-fix; lands alongside Slice 1; no API/contract change).** The previous `Loader2` + literal "Sending…" text rendered inside the user bubble is replaced with a quieter delayed off-bubble pattern in `apps/web/app/app/_components/chat-message.tsx`: a local `useEffect` arms `setTimeout(setShowSendingIndicator, 1000)` when `message.status === "sending"` and clears it on unmount or status change; only after 1 s of sustained `sending` does a small `Loader2` (`h-3 w-3 text-text-subtle animate-spin`) fade in to the right of the bubble via `<AnimatePresence>` + `motion.div` with `width 0→22px` + `opacity 0→1` (180 ms ease-out, parity with the AccountFooter popup motion); the bubble naturally shifts left as the spinner takes width. Fast sends (commit < 1 s) produce no visual artifact at all, the user bubble settles silently. `send_failed` reached before the 1 s timer fires never shows the spinner and flows straight to the existing `AlertCircle + Not delivered + Retry/Cancel` block; `send_failed` reached after the spinner is visible removes the spinner via the AnimatePresence exit and surfaces the same `Not delivered` block. Timer lives locally inside the bubble component — no change to `useChat` API, no change to `ChatMessageStatus` union, no global state. The spinner element carries `data-testid="message-sending-indicator"` plus `role="status"` + `aria-label={tSend("sending")}` so screen readers / tests can address it directly. **Files touched.** `apps/web/app/layout.tsx`, `apps/web/next.config.ts`, `apps/web/app/app/_components/use-theme.ts`, `apps/web/app/app/_components/chat-message.tsx`, `apps/web/app/app/_components/chat-message.test.tsx` (new — 5 scenarios: no spinner before 1 s; spinner appears after 1 s of sustained `sending`; spinner disappears on `committed`; spinner never appears when `send_failed` lands before 1 s; spinner removed and `Not delivered` block surfaces when `send_failed` lands after 1 s), `docs/ADR/076-cold-start-visual-continuity-and-bootstrap-pipeline.md` (Slice 1 ledger row flipped to `landed`; `Updated:` line added with date + summary; status flipped from `Proposed` to `Accepted (Slice 1 landed; Slices 2–7 pending)`), `docs/CHANGELOG.md` (this entry), `docs/SESSION-HANDOFF.md` (matching session entry). **Verification gate green** — `corepack pnpm -r --if-present run lint` clean (5 of 5 lint-bearing workspace projects), `corepack pnpm run format:check` clean (`use-theme.ts`, `chat-message.tsx`, `chat-message.test.tsx` were `prettier --write`-fixed during the slice), `corepack pnpm --filter @persai/web run typecheck` clean, `corepack pnpm --filter @persai/api run typecheck` clean, `corepack pnpm --filter @persai/web run test` 105/105, `corepack pnpm --filter @persai/api run test` 0 failed (every node test suite exits with `# fail 0`). **Out of scope (deliberate, ADR-076 §"Out of scope across the whole program").** No change to the `<OfflineGate />` / `offline.html` / `errorPath` / single-slot `sending`/`send_failed` / `useChat` machinery from ADR-075, no change to Clerk's auth model (proxy mode `/clerk-proxy` + Bearer-only `apps/api`), no change to multichannel runtime contract, no change to ADR-074 economics, no SSR caching for authenticated app routes. **Commit posture.** Per founder request «комит только в конце ADR» — changes left uncommitted in the working tree, staged for end-of-ADR-076 batch commit. **Awaiting** founder live `persai-dev` gates: cold load (incognito + fresh Capacitor install) renders DOM with the correct `<html class>` already present (no visible dark→light or light→dark transition); explicit theme toggle in the AccountFooter popup updates cookie + localStorage + DOM-class + theme-color synchronously and reload comes up in the new theme without flash; `system` choice with OS preference change handled in-session via `matchMedia`; landing-page System / Light / Dark toggle keeps working through the same `useTheme()` controller; fast send flow shows no `sending` artifact, slow send (≥ 1 s) shows the small off-bubble spinner that disappears cleanly on commit, and `send_failed` paths render `Not delivered + Retry/Cancel` in both the pre-1 s and post-1 s branches.

- **ADR-076 Slice 2a — Capacitor system-bars theme bridge (founder repro 2026-04-25 «В мобилке при вкл ночного режима тема переключ норм по панель нижняя nav android остается светлой - проверь это в persai-mobile или где - но нужно правильный fix а не залипуха»; code-landed across `persai-mobile` + `apps/web`; verification gate green; awaiting `cap sync` + APK rebuild + founder live mobile gate):** the bottom Android system navigation bar and the status bar are OS chrome, not WebView chrome — `<meta name="theme-color">` does not control them and `Theme.AppCompat.DayNight` (the parent in `persai-mobile/android/app/src/main/res/values/styles.xml`) follows the OS `uiMode`, not the in-app theme choice in `apps/web/app/app/_components/use-theme.ts`. So a user whose OS was in light mode but who picked dark inside PersAI ended up with a dark web surface above a light system nav bar, and vice versa. The fix follows the same architectural shape as the JS-driven Back-button bridge documented in ADR-075 (web origin owns the resolution decision, native shell is a thin executor, no Capacitor plugin between them). **Native side (`persai-mobile`).** New `persai-mobile/android/app/src/main/java/com/persai/app/SystemBarsBridge.java` registers a `@JavascriptInterface` method on the WebView under `window.PersaiNative.setTheme(string)`. The method runs on the UI thread and calls `Window#setStatusBarColor`, `Window#setNavigationBarColor`, and `WindowInsetsControllerCompat#setAppearanceLight{Status,Navigation}Bars` so both bar background and icon contrast match the in-app palette. Color constants `CHROME_DARK = 0xFF161513` / `CHROME_LIGHT = 0xFFE0D8C8` are pinned to the `--chrome` token in `apps/web/app/globals.css` (a code-comment anchor in both files keeps them in lockstep on future palette changes). Every successful `setTheme` call also persists the resolved value into `SharedPreferences("persai_native").system_bars_theme`, so the next launch can read it back. `MainActivity#onCreate` calls `SystemBarsBridge.applyTheme(this, SystemBarsBridge.readStoredTheme(this))` BEFORE the WebView paints (default = `"dark"` on first ever launch), then registers the bridge via `bridge.getWebView().addJavascriptInterface(new SystemBarsBridge(this), "PersaiNative")` so the interface is in the JS context as early as possible — typically before the inline theme-bootstrap script in `apps/web`'s `<head>` runs. The `onStart()` hook (which already configured the `DownloadListener`) is unchanged. **Web side (`apps/web`).** `apps/web/app/app/_components/use-theme.ts:applyResolved` (the single function that mutates `<html class>` / `colorScheme` / `<meta theme-color>`) now also calls `syncNativeSystemBars(resolved)` — a small typed wrapper around `(window as { PersaiNative? }).PersaiNative?.setTheme()` guarded by try/catch so a missing or not-yet-registered bridge degrades to a silent no-op (desktop / browser web stays unaffected). The inline `themeFallbackScript` in `apps/web/app/layout.tsx` was extended with the same call (`if(window.PersaiNative&&typeof window.PersaiNative.setTheme==="function")window.PersaiNative.setTheme(r);`) inside its existing try/catch so the very first paint can also drive the bars when the bridge happens to be registered before the head script runs. **Cold-start flicker eliminated.** The user no longer sees a mismatched flash between the native splash and the first HTML frame: `onCreate` pre-colors from `SharedPreferences` (synchronous, before WebView paints), the head fallback script may set them again (no-op if already correct), and `useTheme` re-applies on hydration through the same `applyResolved`. **Security boundary.** Same as ADR-075 — the WebView is locked to `https://persai.dev` via `server.url` plus the `allowNavigation` whitelist (`persai.dev`, `*.persai.dev`, `accounts.google.com`, `*.googleusercontent.com`). Third-party origins cannot reach `window.PersaiNative`. **Files touched.** `persai-mobile/android/app/src/main/java/com/persai/app/SystemBarsBridge.java` (new), `persai-mobile/android/app/src/main/java/com/persai/app/MainActivity.java` (added `onCreate` override + `addJavascriptInterface` + `Bundle` import), `apps/web/app/app/_components/use-theme.ts` (`PersaiNativeBridge` interface + `syncNativeSystemBars` helper + call from `applyResolved`), `apps/web/app/layout.tsx` (one extra try-block at the tail of `themeFallbackScript`), `docs/ADR/075-mobile-capacitor-webview-shell.md` (new `## System bars theme bridge` section), `docs/ADR/076-cold-start-visual-continuity-and-bootstrap-pipeline.md` (Slice 2 reorganized into 2a-landed / 2b-proposed; ledger updated to `partial`). **Verification gate green** — `corepack pnpm -r --if-present run lint` clean, `corepack pnpm run format:check` clean, `corepack pnpm --filter @persai/web run typecheck` clean, `corepack pnpm --filter @persai/api run typecheck` clean. No new tests in this slice — the bridge contract is one method with two trivial branches and the SharedPreferences round-trip is exercised end-to-end on the live device. **Out of scope (deliberate).** Slice 2b — the splash drawable rewrite (`@drawable/splash` placeholder removal + real PersAI launch drawable on `--chrome` + `values-night/styles.xml` light variant + iOS `LaunchScreen.storyboard` mirror) — stays under ADR-076 Slice 2 and is a separate session. The cookie-as-truth Slice 1 work in `apps/web/app/app/_components/use-theme.ts` (already landed before this slice) is unchanged; the new bridge call hooks into `applyResolved` without altering the cookie / SSR path. **Awaiting** `cap sync` + APK rebuild on `persai-mobile` and one founder live mobile gate (toggle in-app theme to dark while OS is in light → bottom nav bar AND status bar follow on the next theme transition AND across cold-restart).

- **ADR-076 (Proposed) — PersAI cold-start visual continuity & bootstrap pipeline (founder ask 2026-04-25 «как ускорить безопасно работу на сайте и в mob — пока просто проверь и ответь» followed by «делаем качественно без legasy и хвостов»; docs-only landing today; no code change in this slice):** new ADR `docs/ADR/076-cold-start-visual-continuity-and-bootstrap-pipeline.md` documents the architecturally-correct fix for three perceptible cold-start artifacts surfaced by the founder on web + Capacitor — theme flash (dark default paints once before the inline `<head>` script applies `light`; on Capacitor the WebView background defaults to white before HTML), empty-shell pop-in (`AppShell` is `"use client"` and `useAppData` fan-outs six parallel REST calls only after mount, leaving sidebar / footer / chat header empty until they resolve), and avatar pop-in (`AssistantAvatar` runs a Bearer-authenticated `fetch + blob + URL.createObjectURL` pipeline with an in-memory cache that flushes on full reload, so every Capacitor cold-start re-issues the round-trip; the `apps/api` route already returns `Cache-Control: no-cache, must-revalidate`, intentionally bypassing the HTTP cache). The decision is a coherent six-slice program (with a conditional seventh) executed in strict order: **Slice 1** cookie-as-truth theme with SSR-baked `<html class>` (`persai-theme` cookie becomes the source of truth, `apps/web/app/layout.tsx` reads it server-side and writes the resolved class plus `<meta name="theme-color">` matching `--chrome` — `localStorage` becomes a same-origin mirror; first-visit-without-cookie is handled by `Sec-CH-Prefers-Color-Scheme` client hint on Chromium WebView and a single inline-script fallback for iOS WKWebView, no parallel sources of truth); **Slice 2** Capacitor cold-start visual continuity (`android.backgroundColor` and `ios.backgroundColor` matching `--chrome` dark `#161513`, real PersAI launch drawable replacing the missing `@drawable/splash`, `values-night/styles.xml` for the inverted light variant if needed, iOS `LaunchScreen.storyboard` mirror); **Slice 3** RSC bootstrap with a single batch endpoint `GET /api/v1/app/bootstrap` (Bearer-protected; fans out internally via `Promise.allSettled` to the same six application services that today are six separate routes, returning one envelope `{ requestId, sections: { assistant, chats, telegram, notificationPreference, plan, admin } }` where each section is `{ ok: true, data } | { ok: false, error }` so partial failures stay explicit per section), with `apps/web/app/app/layout.tsx` becoming an `async` Server Component that calls `bootstrap` server-side via `auth().getToken()` and passes `initialData` into `<AppShell>`; `useAppData` initializes from `initialData` and never enters `isLoading=true` on first render — the six per-endpoint client wrappers stay alive only as inputs to mutation refreshes; **Slice 4** cookie-auth versioned avatar pipeline (lifecycle state changes `assistant.{draft,published}.avatarUrl` from `https://<api-host>/api/v1/assistant/avatar` to a content-addressed `/api/avatar/<hash>.<ext>` relative URL; new Next.js route handler `apps/web/app/api/avatar/[hash]/route.ts` authenticates via Clerk cookie session and streams bytes server-side with `Cache-Control: private, max-age=31536000, immutable` + `ETag: "<hash>"`; the previous `GET /api/v1/assistant/avatar` route is removed in the same slice — no two-path drift; `AssistantAvatar` collapses to a thin `<img>` with explicit width/height, deleting `AVATAR_BLOB_CACHE`, the `getToken()` flow, and the `useEffect` that drove them); **Slice 5** skeleton contracts only where data is genuinely pending (after Slice 3 the only real pending windows are mid-session refreshes like `reloadChats()` after destructive actions or thread switching; small targeted shimmers there, no global loading wave); **Slice 6** slide-over code-splitting + initial-bundle audit (`AssistantSettings` and `TelegramConnect` move to `next/dynamic({ ssr: false, loading: () => null })`, mounted only when their slide-overs open; one-shot audit of `lucide-react` chunk graph and per-callsite `framer-motion` keep/replace decisions); **Slice 7** Service-Worker PWA shell (conditional, decision after Slice 6, scoped to `apps/web` only with platform support documented separately for Android Chromium WebView vs iOS WKWebView). **Execution rules.** One slice per session, one commit per repo, verification gate (`pnpm -r --if-present run lint` / `pnpm run format:check` / `pnpm --filter @persai/{api,web} run typecheck` / `pnpm --filter @persai/web run test`) must clear before commit, ADR-076 + CHANGELOG + SESSION-HANDOFF updated in the same slice that lands code, no transitional or dual-mode patches preserving the old shape — each slice removes the previous shape in the same change. Out-of-order execution is not allowed: Slice 4 depends on Slice 3 because the new lifecycle envelope ships through `bootstrap`; Slice 2 depends on Slice 1 because the splash colour assumes the SSR-resolved palette. **Mobile alignment.** Capacitor WebView inherits Slices 1, 3, 4, 5, 6 automatically because it loads the same `persai.dev` origin; Slice 2 is the only `persai-mobile`-side change. The single iOS-WebView caveat — `Sec-CH-Prefers-Color-Scheme` client hint support is partial — is addressed in Slice 1 by retaining a tiny inline-script fallback as the documented first-visit path, not as a parallel source of truth. **Status today.** ADR-076 is `Proposed`; this CHANGELOG entry, the ADR file, and the matching SESSION-HANDOFF entry are the only changes in this docs-only slice. The execution ledger inside the ADR records every slice as `proposed`. Verification gate green (lint / format / typecheck / test all pass — docs-only change). **Awaiting:** founder approval to proceed with Slice 1.

- **Pre-launch UI polish 2026 — warm tonal palette + bento desktop frame + sidebar/footer redesign + setup/landing polish + Geist Sans/Mono typography (founder ask 2026-04-25 «какой сейчас в моде стиль UI? мои UI кажется немного шумным» → «сделай для PROD пока я не выкатил в свет чтобы сразу было wow»; presentation-only slice on `apps/web`, no architecture / API / data-model change; verification gate green; awaiting `persai-dev` deploy + 4 founder live UI gates):** the dark palette of the app was rewritten from cool-grey/sage to a warm tonal stack with a new `--chrome` token (`#161513` dark, `#e0d8c8` light) sitting between the outer body frame and the inner panel surface — exposed in `apps/web/app/globals.css` via `@theme inline` so Tailwind utilities `bg-chrome` / `border-chrome` are available everywhere. The shell (`apps/web/app/app/_components/app-shell.tsx`) draws a Cursor-style **bento frame on `md+`** (`md:rounded-2xl md:border md:border-border` on the panel area, `md:gap-2 md:p-2` on the wrapper) and stays full-bleed on mobile so the Capacitor WebView never loses pixels of viewport. **Sidebar redesign** (`apps/web/app/app/_components/sidebar.tsx`): the four-block footer (token meter / integrations / language / profile) is consolidated into one `AccountFooter` row whose tap opens an upward popup containing the same toggles, wrapped in `AnimatePresence` + `motion.div` for slide-up + fade; group labels lost `uppercase tracking-wider` and read sentence-case; "New chat" CTA moved from filled-accent to ghost (`border border-border bg-surface-raised`); active chat row uses `bg-accent/12 text-text`; per-row `lastMessagePreview` removed; on `md+` the sidebar gets `md:rounded-2xl md:border md:border-border` to match the bento frame. **Chat surface polish** — compaction banner colours tokenised to `success` / `warning` palette, the iridescent "Умный" pill (`from-violet-500 via-fuchsia-500 to-amber-400`) replaced with `bg-accent/15 text-accent ring-1 ring-accent/30`, mobile menu button enlarged to `p-2.5 + h-5 w-5` (~25% bigger touch target) with `aria-label`, empty-state prompt cards moved to `rounded-2xl bg-surface-raised/70` with hover tinted by `hover:border-accent/40 hover:bg-surface-raised`, composer (`chat-input.tsx`) gains `rounded-2xl bg-surface-raised`, drops the persistent `inputHint` paragraph (i18n key removed), and on `md+` removes its top border so it merges visually with the bento panel. **Setup flow** (`apps/web/app/app/setup/page.tsx`) — Step-2 / Step-3 `h1` shrunk from `text-3xl md:text-4xl` to `text-2xl md:text-3xl` with `leading-tight`, subtitles reformatted as quiet `<p>` muted body copy, four hardcoded `rgba(102,187,106,…)` glow shadows replaced with `shadow-[0_0_…_var(--accent-glow)]`, the technical `previewPromptHint` paragraph removed from render (i18n key kept as empty string for cache safety), preview CTA renamed `Создать` / `Create` (was `Пересоздать асистента`) and recovery CTA renamed `Восстановить` / `Recover`; `archetypeSectionHint` rewritten to drop the "Voice DNA" jargon. **Assistant settings** right-side slide-over expanded sections gain `pt-2` on the body so content has breathing room above. **Landing page** (`apps/web/app/page.tsx` + new `apps/web/app/_components/landing-theme-toggle.tsx`) — the page was effectively dark-only with hardcoded `bg-emerald-300/[0.07]` / `border-white/8` / `bg-white/[0.03]`; now ships a 3-state System / Light / Dark toggle in the header (reuses the in-app `useTheme()` so a visitor's choice persists into their authenticated session), Aurora halos use `bg-accent/[0.07]`, the platforms pill uses `border-border bg-surface-raised/40 backdrop-blur-sm` (brand-tinted glyphs preserved for Telegram / VK / WhatsApp / MAX), CTA glow uses `var(--accent-glow)` (`shadow-[0_0_48px]` → hover `shadow-[0_0_72px]`), a soft sheen (`from-transparent via-white/20 to-transparent`) animates on hover, and a subtle inline-SVG noise-grain overlay (`mix-blend-overlay opacity-[0.035]`) sits over the page for the "premium printed paper" feel. **Pre-hydration theme bootstrap** in `apps/web/app/layout.tsx`: a synchronous IIFE in `<head>` reads `localStorage.persai-theme` (one of `system|light|dark`), resolves `system` against `prefers-color-scheme`, and applies `documentElement.classList.add("light")` + `documentElement.style.colorScheme` before the first paint — eliminates the dark-over-light (or vice versa) flash on cold load. `<meta name="theme-color">` ships two values gated on `prefers-color-scheme` so the browser / Capacitor system bar always matches `--chrome`. **Typography — Geist Sans (UI) + Geist Mono (code)** replace `next/font/google` `Inter`: `geist` package (MIT, ships local `.woff2` so no Google Fonts roundtrip — important for Capacitor cold-start) added to `apps/web/package.json`; `layout.tsx` applies `${GeistSans.variable} ${GeistMono.variable}` on `<html>` and `bg-chrome font-sans text-text antialiased` on `<body>`; `globals.css` `@theme inline` maps `--font-sans` → `var(--font-geist-sans), system-ui, …` and `--font-mono` → `var(--font-geist-mono), ui-monospace, Menlo, …` so every existing Tailwind `font-sans` / `font-mono` callsite (admin pages, debug panes, badges, code-fences) instantly switches without touching call sites; `.code-block` gets an explicit `font-family: var(--font-mono)` so highlight.js fences render in Geist Mono with the right tracking; Clerk `appearance.fontFamily` updated to `var(--font-geist-sans), system-ui, -apple-system, sans-serif` for visual consistency on sign-in / sign-up surfaces. Native Cyrillic + Latin from one family, no fallback flash on RU. **i18n** — `apps/web/messages/{en,ru}.json` lost `inputHint`, gained `theme` / `language` namespaces for the AccountFooter popup, and rewrote `archetypeSectionHint` / `instructionHint` / `previewPromptHint` / `recreateAssistant` / `recoverAssistant` / `createAssistant` per the polish above. **Files touched** (presentation-only): `apps/web/app/globals.css`, `apps/web/app/layout.tsx`, `apps/web/app/page.tsx`, `apps/web/app/_components/landing-theme-toggle.tsx` (new), `apps/web/app/app/_components/app-shell.tsx`, `apps/web/app/app/_components/sidebar.tsx`, `apps/web/app/app/_components/chat-area.tsx`, `apps/web/app/app/_components/chat-input.tsx`, `apps/web/app/app/_components/chat-message.tsx`, `apps/web/app/app/_components/assistant-settings.tsx`, `apps/web/app/app/setup/page.tsx`, `apps/web/app/sign-in/[[...sign-in]]/page.tsx`, `apps/web/app/sign-up/[[...sign-up]]/page.tsx`, `apps/web/messages/{en,ru}.json`, `apps/web/package.json`, `pnpm-lock.yaml`, plus `canvases/ui-style-polish-2026.canvas.tsx` (design rationale). **Verification gate green** — `corepack pnpm -r --if-present run lint` clean, `corepack pnpm run format:check` clean (six files re-formatted by prettier on first pass and re-checked green), `corepack pnpm --filter @persai/web run typecheck` clean, `corepack pnpm --filter @persai/api run typecheck` clean. No new tests — pure presentation slice; existing component tests re-render through the new tokens. **Out of scope (explicit).** No architecture / API / data-model change; ADR-072 / ADR-073 / ADR-074 / ADR-075 are unaffected. The mobile shell does not need a `cap sync` — all changes live in the web origin loaded over the existing `server.url` contract. **Awaiting** `persai-dev` deploy of `apps/web` + 4 founder live UI gates: light-theme parity on `/` (warm cream chrome, OS status bar matches), mobile menu button hit area on Capacitor, empty-state cards reading as a soft welcome, and the setup flow Step-2 / Step-3 reading better on a narrow viewport with the unambiguous `Создать` CTA.
