New `apps/api/src/modules/workspace-management/application/persai-background-compaction-scheduler.service.ts` mirrors the `PersaiScheduledActionSchedulerService` claim-and-lease pattern (5s poll, 60s claim TTL, exponential retry up to 5 attempts, epoch invalidation across deploys/restarts via the new `background_compaction_scheduler_epoch` column on `PlatformConfigGeneration` and `BumpConfigGenerationService.bumpBackgroundCompactionSchedulerEpoch` / `currentBackgroundCompactionSchedulerEpoch`). The scheduler dispatches each claimed job via the new `InternalRuntimeCompactionClientService` (bearer-authed POST to `POST /api/v1/internal/runtime/sessions/compact-and-extract`, 30s timeout, retryable classification of 408/429/5xx). Job intake is the new `EnqueueBackgroundCompactionJobService` behind the new internal `POST /api/v1/internal/runtime/compaction/enqueue` controller (returns 202 with `{ enqueued, jobId, superseded }`); a duplicate enqueue while a `pending` row still exists for `(assistantId, channel, externalThreadKey)` collapses to `superseded: true` via the `pending_dedupe_key` partial unique index from the scaffolding migration plus the `P2002` short-circuit. New `apps/runtime/src/modules/turns/interface/http/internal-runtime-sessions.controller.ts` accepts the api scheduler's call at `POST /api/v1/internal/runtime/sessions/compact-and-extract` (bearer-authed via `assertRuntimeInternalApiAuthorized`, mirrors the M1 internal hydrate endpoint shape) and always invokes `SessionCompactionService.compactSession` with `trigger: "auto_compaction"` and `autoExtract: true` so threshold semantics still apply and auto-extract follows on the same job in the same process. `apps/runtime/src/modules/turns/session-compaction.service.ts` now loads the latest persisted synopsis via `runtimeStatePostgresService.findLatestSessionCompaction(...)` and feeds its rendered text into the system prompt as "REPLACE this whole synopsis with the updated one that covers prior + this slice" — the persisted shape didn't change (M1's storage was already replace-style at the repository level), only the prompt instruction was missing. The prompt-cache family rename `shared_compaction_summary → rolling_session_synopsis` (`v2`) lands together with the cutover so the new producer is ready when the cache rebuilds; this is the intentional one-time cache-rebuild cost the scaffolding entry called out. New `apps/runtime/src/modules/turns/auto-extract-to-memory.service.ts` runs **one** `auto_extract_to_memory` LLM call (warm friend-voice prompt, `{ items: [{ kind, summary }] }` strict JSON schema, soft cap of 8) over the freshly compacted turn slice, then writes through the existing M1 `writeMemory` internal endpoint so M1's memory-class routing applies automatically; the result lands on `RuntimeCompactionResult.autoExtract` (count + per-kind histogram + accepted entries + dedup-skip / policy-skip counters + provider usage) so smoke traces can see "compaction fired in background, wrote N memories, took T ms" without timestamp correlation. Server-side dedup hardened in `apps/api/src/modules/workspace-management/application/write-assistant-memory.service.ts` via the new `findActiveByNormalizedSummaryAndAssistantId` repository method: an active entry with the same normalized summary returns `{ written: false, code: "duplicate" }` and bumps `last_used_at` on the existing row instead of inserting, which also benefits the model-driven `memory_write` tool (audit event `assistant.memory_write_duplicate`). Tests landed alongside the behavior: `apps/api/test/persai-background-compaction-scheduler.service.test.ts` (claim/lease/retry/non-retryable failure/exhaustion/epoch-changed/stale-claim-reclaim/unexpected-throw), `apps/api/test/enqueue-background-compaction-job.service.test.ts` (parse validation including `runtime_tier` whitelist from `@persai/runtime-contract`, supersede on `P2002`, rethrow on unrelated errors), `apps/api/test/internal-runtime-compaction-enqueue.controller.test.ts` (auth happy/missing/wrong + supersede passthrough), `apps/api/test/write-assistant-memory.service.test.ts` extended with the dedup case, `apps/runtime/test/auto-extract-to-memory.service.test.ts` (deterministic fake LLM exercises accept / pre-write dedup / server-side duplicate / policy denial / soft cap / provider failure / unsupported transport / empty messages), `apps/runtime/test/session-compaction.service.test.ts` extended with the previous-synopsis injection assertion, and `apps/runtime/test/prompt-cache-stable-blocks.test.ts` updated for the `rolling_session_synopsis` family rename. Verification gate this session: `pnpm --filter @persai/runtime-contract typecheck` clean, `pnpm --filter @persai/runtime typecheck` clean, `pnpm --filter @persai/api typecheck` clean, `pnpm --filter @persai/runtime test` clean (auto-extract + session-compaction + cutover + prompt-cache families pass), `pnpm --filter @persai/api test` clean (scheduler + enqueue + controller + write-memory dedup pass). Live acceptance against the founder's `persai-dev` `Custom` plan (`compactionTriggerThreshold = 8000`, `targetContextBudget = 70000`, `keepRecentMinimum = 4`, `autoCompactionWeb = true`) — `long-session-200` token sub-linearity + p95 not regressing, `chitchat-short` p95 + cache hit rate, `multi-session-continuity` regression — runs **after** image publish + Argo CD rollout and lands as a follow-up CHANGELOG closeout entry once measured. The previously documented "scaffolding landed, behavioral implementation deferred" entry below is preserved as the prior state of this slice for traceability.
- **ADR-074 Slice M2 — Background compaction with human-voiced auto-extract (scaffolding landed; behavioral implementation + `persai-dev` smoke acceptance deferred to follow-up session):** the additive scaffolding required for M2's behavioral half is now in place but every change in this commit is intentionally idle (producer-less / consumer-less) so live `persai-dev` behavior is unchanged. `packages/runtime-contract/src/index.ts` flips `PERSAI_RUNTIME_CONTEXT_HYDRATION_PRESET_DEFAULTS.balanced.autoCompactionWeb` and `.rich.autoCompactionWeb` from `false` to `true` (note: the codebase preset name is `rich`, not `premium` as the M2 prompt and ADR text use; same tier, naming-only deviation). The same file adds the new `RuntimeCompactionAutoExtractResult` interface (`attempted`, `written`, `dedupSkipped`, `policySkipped`, `invalidSkipped`, `kindCounts`, `entries: Array<{kind, summary}>`, `durationMs`, `reason`, `usage`) and an optional `autoExtract?: RuntimeCompactionAutoExtractResult | null` field on `RuntimeCompactionResult` so the next session's smoke trace renderer can dump every extraction's `kind` + `summary` for founder eyeball review without correlating timestamps. `apps/api/prisma/schema.prisma` adds the `AssistantBackgroundCompactionJob` model + `AssistantBackgroundCompactionJobStatus` (`pending`/`in_progress`/`completed`/`failed`) and `AssistantBackgroundCompactionJobTrigger` (`post_turn`/`manual`) enums, with back-relations on `Assistant` and `Workspace`, and the matching reversible migration `apps/api/prisma/migrations/20260422010000_adr074_m2_background_compaction_jobs/migration.sql` creates the table + a unique partial index over `pending_dedupe_key` for supersede-on-enqueue, plus a `(status, retry_after_at, created_at)` poll index, an `(assistant_id, channel, external_thread_key, created_at DESC)` history index, and FK constraints to `assistants` (CASCADE) + `workspaces` (RESTRICT). `docs/ADR/074-humanity-and-cost-polish-program.md` Slice M2 section gains a "Status — scaffolding landed, behavioral implementation deferred" block enumerating exactly what landed and exactly what the next session must add (in dependency order: api scheduler service mirroring `PersaiScheduledActionSchedulerService` claim/lease/retry/supersede shape; api enqueue endpoint on `:3002`; api → runtime trigger client; runtime `AutoExtractToMemoryService` with human-friend voice prompt + soft cap 8 + write-through M1; `SessionCompactionService` modification to feed the previous synopsis into the next compaction call's system prompt; `TurnExecutionService.finalizeAcceptedTurnWithPostTurnEffects` fire-and-forget enqueue replacing the in-band `await` per Principle 5 "no shadow paths"; `prompt-cache-stable-blocks` family rename `shared_compaction_summary` → `rolling_session_synopsis` with `v1 → v2` version bump — intentionally NOT in this scaffolding commit because it would invalidate live OpenAI/Anthropic prompt caches without delivering any new behavior; `WriteAssistantMemoryService` lexical-dedup hardening with new `findActiveByNormalizedSummary` repository method; five test files covering the new behaviors; live smoke against `persai-dev` `Custom` plan covering `long-session-200` token sub-linearity + p95 not regressing, `chitchat-short` p95 + cache hit rate, and `multi-session-continuity` regression). The split mirrors the M1 closeout precedent (M1 was also delivered in two sessions: code-landed → live-accepted) and was made instead of attempting a one-shot push because M2's file count is roughly 2× M1's. Verification gate this session: `pnpm --filter @persai/api prisma:generate` clean, `pnpm --filter @persai/api typecheck` clean, `pnpm --filter @persai/runtime typecheck` clean, `pnpm --filter @persai/runtime-contract typecheck` clean. Full local `pnpm test` is queued for the next session once the behavioral half lands and there is something new to lock.
- **ADR-074 Slice M1 — Durable memory closeout / live-accepted on `persai-dev`:** Slice M1 is flipped from "code-landed, awaiting smoke" to closed / live-accepted. The image for commit `9c730220` was published, pinned into `infra/argocd/persai-dev/values-dev.yaml` by the bot (`0ad9dd8`), and rolled out by Argo CD across `api`, `runtime`, and `web`. The Prisma migration `20260421140000_adr074_m1_durable_memory_class` finished cleanly on the live database (backfill produced `core fact = 9`, `core preference = 7`, `contextual null = 796` cluster-wide). The new `POST /api/v1/internal/runtime/memory/hydrate-for-turn` route on `API_INTERNAL_PORT=3002` was confirmed both by `RoutesResolver` startup logs and by a real runtime → API call returning `200` in `217ms` on the first turn. The two committed M1 acceptance scenarios were then run end-to-end against `https://api.persai.dev` (public ingress) plus `kubectl port-forward svc/api-internal 13002:3002` (internal listener for receipts polling) on assistant `b635d40d-ced6-428d-a68b-7395463b2db9`: `multi-session-continuity` ran `12/12` turns OK with total tokens **−33.67%** (`108_256` vs baseline `163_201`), p95 latency `−3_673ms`, and a clean cross-session recall trace where session 2 used `knowledge_search` + `knowledge_fetch` to retrieve the planted `Atlas`, `Helio`, and `retention` facts on the matching cue (not by blanket dumping the contextual tail); `chitchat-short` ran `8/8` turns OK with total tokens **−22.67%** and the explicit P1 cache invariant held — cached input went from `36_864 / 56_466 = 65.3%` (baseline) to `36_864 / 43_568 = 84.6%` cache hit rate (a `+19.3pp` improvement, well above the `±2pp` acceptance bar) with the absolute cached-token count numerically identical, proving contextual rotation does NOT invalidate the cached `system + core + shared compaction summary` prefix. Live database verification on the test assistant after the smoke runs: classification distribution matches the policy (`memory_write` `kind=fact` / `kind=preference` → `memory_class=core`; `kind=open_loop` → `memory_class=contextual`; web-chat memory → `memory_class=contextual, kind=null`); the `MEMORY_CORE_HARD_CAP=15` overflow rule fired correctly, demoting oldest `core` rows down to `contextual` (`core fact=9, core preference=6, contextual fact=1, contextual preference=3` post-smoke, vs `core fact=9, core preference=7` pre-smoke); `last_used_at` was bumped on `60` distinct rows in the 20-minute smoke window, confirming `HydrateMemoryForTurnService.bumpLastUsedAt(...)` is being called for every hydrated turn. Qualitatively, the proactive `memory_write` `usage_guidance` rephrase produced an unprompted `memory_write` for the Barcelona-retreat fact in addition to the planted `Запомни… retention` cue, validating the humanity-bonus intent without requiring users to operate the memory subsystem. Baselines under `scripts/smoke/baselines/` were intentionally NOT rewritten to preserve the pre-M1 reference point for downstream slices (M2 / M3) that will need to compare against the pre-M1 world. The previously documented "code-landed, awaiting smoke" entry below is preserved as the prior state of this slice for traceability. Closeout details, including the rollout/CI runs, exact deltas, DB queries, and the `kubectl port-forward svc/api 3001:3001` flake-vs-`https://api.persai.dev` workaround, are in `docs/SESSION-HANDOFF.md` and `docs/ADR/074-humanity-and-cost-polish-program.md`.
- **ADR-074 Slice M1 — Durable memory: core + relevance-retrieved tail (code-landed, awaiting `persai-dev` smoke acceptance):** durable memory is now split into two real classes at write-time and rendered as two distinct prompt blocks at hydrate-time, so the assistant stops paying input tokens for the long tail on every turn while still keeping identity-defining facts always-on. `apps/api/prisma/schema.prisma` and `apps/api/prisma/migrations/20260421140000_adr074_m1_durable_memory_class/migration.sql` introduce `AssistantMemoryRegistryClass` (`core` | `contextual`), `AssistantMemoryRegistryKind` (`fact` | `preference` | `open_loop`), a nullable `last_used_at` for staleness scoring, plus indexes for "list active core" and "search active contextual" reads, with a one-shot backfill from existing `sourceType` / `sourceLabel` rows so the live `assistant_memory_registry_items` table is migrated in place. `apps/api/src/modules/workspace-management/domain/memory-class-policy.ts` now owns the classification rule (`fact`/`preference` → `core`, `open_loop` → `contextual`, `web_chat` → `contextual`, Workspace Memory → `core`) and the hard cap `MEMORY_CORE_HARD_CAP = 15` with oldest-demoted overflow. `WriteAssistantMemoryService`, `ManageAssistantWorkspaceMemoryService`, and `RecordWebChatMemoryTurnService` now all set `memoryClass` and `kind` correctly when writing, and `WriteAssistantMemoryService` consults `countActiveCoreByAssistantId` + `demoteOldestCoreByAssistantId` on the write path so the core block stays bounded without ever surfacing the cap to the user. `ReadAssistantKnowledgeService.searchMemory` now accepts a `memoryClass` filter and returns `summary` / `memoryClass` / `kind` in the result metadata; the new `HydrateMemoryForTurnService` and `InternalRuntimeMemoryHydrationController` (`POST /api/v1/internal/runtime/memory/hydrate-for-turn` on the `API_INTERNAL_PORT=3002` listener) wrap that into a single internal endpoint that returns the always-on core entries + the relevance-retrieved contextual tail and bumps `last_used_at` on every hydrated entry in one batch. `apps/runtime/src/modules/turns/persai-internal-api.client.service.ts` gained a typed `hydrateMemoryForTurn` client and `apps/runtime/src/modules/turns/turn-context-hydration.service.ts` now calls it instead of reading durable memory directly, then composes two separate assistant messages: `durable_memory_core` (always present, bounded, byte-stable across turns) and `durable_memory_contextual` (per-turn relevance, omitted when empty). `apps/runtime/src/modules/turns/prompt-cache-stable-blocks.ts` was refactored to register `durable_memory_core` as a stable family in `STABLE_BLOCK_FAMILIES` and to expose `formatDurableMemoryContextualBlock` + `isDurableMemoryContextualMessage` as deliberately non-stable helpers, so the contextual block does NOT contribute to the prompt-cache key — preserving P1's cached prefix even though contextual content rotates per turn. `apps/api/prisma/bootstrap-preset-data.ts` `memory_write` `usage_guidance` was rephrased from a restrictive "remember when the user says 'remember'" to a proactive "this is your continuous notebook — write whenever you learn something stable" framing, and the misleading reference to a non-existent `memory_forget` tool was removed in favor of telling the model to capture corrective notes and let the user manage memories through the Memory Center UI. The Memory Center UI in `apps/web/app/app/_components/assistant-settings.tsx` now shows two new badges per entry — `memoryClass` (`core` / `contextual`) and `memoryKind` (`fact` / `preference` / `open loop`) — plumbed through `packages/contracts/openapi.yaml` (`AssistantMemoryRegistryClass` + `AssistantMemoryRegistryKind` schemas, `AssistantMemoryRegistryItemState.memoryClass` + `.kind`) and bilingual copy in `apps/web/messages/{en,ru}.json`; promote/demote controls were intentionally NOT added (founder principle 1: classification is a coded outcome, not a user setting). New tests in `apps/api/test/hydrate-memory-for-turn.service.test.ts`, `apps/runtime/test/prompt-cache-stable-blocks.test.ts`, and updates to `apps/api/test/write-assistant-memory.service.test.ts` + `apps/runtime/test/turn-context-hydration.service.test.ts` + `apps/runtime/test/turn-execution.service.test.ts` lock the new write-time classification + overflow logic, the two-block hydration shape, and the cache-key invariant that contextual rotation does not invalidate the core+shared-summary stable prefix. Final smoke acceptance against `persai-dev` (`multi-session-continuity`, `chitchat-short`) is the next step and will land as a follow-up CHANGELOG entry once measured.
- **ADR-074 Slice V1 — Voice DNA scaffold (closed / live-accepted):** the assistant's voice is now a first-class editable layer rather than an implicit traits-only persona. Four bilingual archetypes (`warm-quiet`, `playful-sharp`, `calm-deep`, `dry-witty`) live in `persona_archetypes`, are seeded from `apps/api/prisma/persona-archetype-data.ts`, can be edited at runtime through `/api/v1/admin/persona-archetypes/*`, and are modulated per turn by the existing slider traits through `voice-dna-modulator.ts`. Publish now snapshots both `snapshotArchetypeKey` and `snapshotVoiceDna`, while materialization prefers the live archetype and falls back to the snapshot only if needed. The setup wizard now exposes a dedicated 4-archetype picker backed by `GET /api/v1/assistant/persona-archetypes`, and `/admin/presets` now includes both the `Voice DNA Archetypes` editor and V1 migration tools for prompt templates (`Insert Voice DNA block` on `soul`, plus per-template `Reset to default`). The default `soul` template consumes structured Voice DNA placeholders, the admin route uses `POST /api/v1/admin/persona-archetypes/:key/reset-to-default`, and the supporting API/unit-test coverage is in place. Final acceptance for V1 was completed by the founder through live UI validation on `persai-dev`; the closeout session also re-confirmed live runtime readiness (`/api/v1/assistant/runtime/preflight`) and the live archetype surface (`/api/v1/assistant/persona-archetypes`).
- **ADR-074 Slice P1 — live-dev acceptance against image `e01bb5d` (warm cache, vs S0 baselines under `scripts/smoke/baselines/`):** `chitchat-short` total tokens −4.4% / cached +9.7% / p95 −1408ms / 8 ok; `long-session-200` total tokens −24.5% / avg-per-turn −25% / p95 −49% (24869ms→12587ms) / 29 ok; `tool-heavy-search` total tokens −29.5% / avg-per-turn −29.5% / 5 ok with the same 2/4 expected-tool-hit ratio as S0 baseline. The first cold-cache `chitchat-short` after the rollout (artifacts `chitchat-short-2026-04-20T21-11-12-614Z`) showed cached=6144 only on turn 8: that is the expected one-time provider-side prefix warmup after the bundle hash flipped because the new stable-prefix content has no prior OpenAI cache; the warm rerun (`chitchat-short-2026-04-20T21-26-58-779Z`) is the canonical P1 acceptance. The original ADR-074 P1 "≥5x input token reduction" target was overstated for our actual prefix size — removing `heartbeat_block` and `tools_catalog_block` shrank the cacheable prefix itself, so the realistic structural ceiling on P1 alone is the ~25% per-turn input reduction we measured on `long-session-200`. Subsequent slices (P2 retrieval ceilings, P3 web auto-compaction, P5 lazy tools) compose on top of this; ADR-074 P1 is closed and the baselines under `scripts/smoke/baselines/` are intentionally NOT overwritten — they remain the pre-P1 reference for downstream cost slices.
- **ADR-074 Slice P1 — stable prefix engineering (cached system prompt + developer-message tail):** the cached system prompt that goes to OpenAI/Anthropic on every ordinary turn is now intentionally byte-stable across turns so provider-native prompt caching can stay hot. The default `system` prompt template in `apps/api/prisma/bootstrap-preset-data.ts` no longer interpolates `{{heartbeat_block}}`, and the default `tools` template no longer interpolates `{{tools_catalog_block}}` (native provider tool definitions already carry full descriptions, so the markdown duplication was pure cache-buster). `apps/api/src/modules/workspace-management/application/compile-prompt-constructor.service.ts` now passes `heartbeat_block`, `route_control_block`, and `tools_catalog_block` as `null` when interpolating any custom template, so admin-customized templates still drop those placeholders cleanly via `interpolateTemplate`'s null-line stripping; the legacy fallback concatenation also no longer carries `heartbeat`. `packages/runtime-bundle/src/index.ts` mirrors that in the bundle fallback `systemPrompt` / `stablePrefix`. `packages/runtime-contract/src/index.ts` adds an optional `developerInstructions` field on `ProviderGatewayTextGenerateRequest` documented as the canonical home for per-turn tail content that must NOT invalidate the cached prefix (routing/execution-mode hints today; per-turn time fields and other dynamic context in later ADR-074 slices). `apps/runtime/src/modules/turns/turn-execution.service.ts` now builds the request so `systemPrompt` is only the cached `bundle.promptConstructor.ordinary.systemPrompt`, and the previous routing-guidance + heartbeat content is concatenated into `developerInstructions` instead. `apps/provider-gateway/src/modules/providers/openai/openai-provider.client.ts` projects `developerInstructions` as a final `role: "developer"` input item appended after history and any tool-history exchange, and `apps/provider-gateway/src/modules/providers/anthropic/anthropic-provider.client.ts` projects it as a second `text` block on the `system` array (legacy single-string `system` is preserved when only `systemPrompt` is set, to minimize behavioural drift). Tests updated: `apps/api/test/compile-prompt-constructor.service.test.ts` now locks the new ADR-074 P1 invariants — `systemPrompt` MUST NOT contain heartbeat or per-turn tool-catalog markdown, the `promptDocuments.heartbeat` document still carries the heartbeat text for the runtime developer-message renderer, and changing only the heartbeat does not change the `systemPrompt` / `stablePrefix.hash` byte-for-byte; `apps/runtime/test/turn-execution.service.test.ts` was updated so the routing-hint assertions (`Selected execution mode: …`, `Assistant knowledge retrieval is likely needed before answering`, `Fresh external information is likely needed`, `## Early Routing Hints`) now look at `developerInstructions` and explicitly assert their absence from `systemPrompt`. The expected operator-side follow-through is one fresh `pnpm smoke:run --scenario chitchat-short --scenario long-session-200 --scenario tool-heavy-search` against `persai-dev` to capture the post-P1 token deltas vs. the committed S0 baselines under `scripts/smoke/baselines/`.
- **ADR-074 Slice S0 — final smoke polish (`toolInvocations` truth, UTF-8 scenarios, clean re-baselines):** the smoke harness now documents and relies on the runtime-side `toolInvocations` trace as the primary source of tool counts, with `toolCallsSource` making the fallback to billable-only `usage.entries[].toolCode` explicit when older receipts are encountered. This closes the false `Tools: <none>` hole on `tool-heavy-search`, where inline `web_search` / `web_fetch` activity could be real in chat history but invisible in the summary. The starter JSON scenarios under `scripts/smoke/scenarios/` were also re-saved as clean UTF-8 so Russian prompts no longer round-trip through mojibake during smoke-driven chats, and fresh live `persai-dev` baselines for `chitchat-short` and `tool-heavy-search` were recorded at `ok=N failed=0`.
- **ADR-074 Slice S0 — live-dev hardening of smoke harness:** the S0 harness was wired against `persai-dev` end-to-end and made green on the live API. Three real defects from the initial S0 commit were fixed: (1) `scripts/smoke/lib/api-client.ts` was hitting `${apiBaseUrl}/assistant/chat/web` without the `/api/v1` prefix, so every turn returned `404 Cannot POST /assistant/chat/web` — the public chat paths now correctly use `/api/v1/assistant/chat/web` and `/api/v1/assistant/chat/web/stream`. (2) The internal smoke-receipts endpoint lives only on the dedicated internal listener (`API_INTERNAL_PORT=3002`, see `apps/api/src/main.ts`'s `routeByListenerPort` middleware), but the harness was talking to the public listener on `3001` and getting a hard 404 from the listener split rather than from NestJS routing — `scripts/smoke/lib/workspace.ts` now exposes a separate `apiInternalBaseUrl` (default `http://127.0.0.1:3002`, env override `SMOKE_API_INTERNAL_BASE_URL`) and `api-client.ts` uses it for `/api/v1/internal/smoke/turn-receipts` only; live use requires a second `kubectl port-forward svc/api-internal 3002:3002`. (3) The `requestId` returned by `POST /assistant/chat/web` is the **HTTP tracing id**, not the `runtime_turn_receipts.requestId` written by the runtime, so the original receipt poll never matched anything — `scripts/smoke/lib/api-client.ts` now exposes `findReceiptForThreadAfter(externalThreadKey, afterCursorIso)` and `harness.ts` captures a cursor moments before each turn and correlates by `externalThreadKey` (== `surfaceThreadKey`) + `createdAt > afterCursor`, which is unambiguous because the harness sends turns sequentially per thread. The same slice also adds `defaultThinkAfterMs` at scenario level (`scripts/smoke/lib/scenario.ts` + `harness.ts`) and bumps every starter scenario JSON to `defaultThinkAfterMs: 8000` so paced traffic stays under `ABUSE_USER_SLOWDOWN_REQUESTS_PER_MINUTE=8` and does not get cut by `rate_limited` mid-scenario, while skipping the post-think pause after the last turn of each session to avoid wasting time. `scripts/smoke/README.md` now documents the new internal port-forward step and the rate-limit pacing rationale, and `run-scenario.ts --help` lists `SMOKE_API_INTERNAL_BASE_URL`. With this in place, `chitchat-short` runs 8/8 OK with full token capture from the live `persai-dev` API as a Clerk-authenticated user, producing the first real `summary.json` baseline (avg ~7.1k tokens/turn, p50 ~3.7s).
- **ADR-074 Slice S0 — smoke harness foundation:** the repo now has a real CLI smoke harness for objective per-turn token/tool/latency measurement against `apps/api`. New internal endpoint `GET /api/v1/internal/smoke/turn-receipts` (`apps/api/src/modules/workspace-management/interface/http/internal-smoke-receipts.controller.ts` + `application/read-smoke-turn-receipts.service.ts`, gated by `PERSAI_INTERNAL_API_TOKEN`) reads `runtime_turn_receipts.resultPayload` and returns mapped `usageAccounting` (input/cached/output/total tokens), aggregated `toolCalls`, `turnRouting` (mode + executionMode), `autoCompaction` (tokens before/after), and supports filtering by `assistantId` + optional `requestId` / `afterCursor` / `limit`. New workspace package `@persai/smoke` (`scripts/smoke/`) provides `pnpm smoke:run --scenario <id>` and `pnpm smoke:run-all` with six starter scenarios — `onboarding`, `chitchat-short`, `long-session-200`, `tool-heavy-search`, `multi-session-continuity`, `emotional-long` — driving real `POST /assistant/chat/web` and `/assistant/chat/web/stream` turns against the live API as a Clerk user (`SMOKE_USER_BEARER`), then correlating each turn's `requestId` against the internal receipts endpoint to assemble per-turn `trace.json` and aggregate `summary.json` (totals, p50/p95/p99 latency, token breakdown, tool counts, routing modes, auto-compaction triggers) under `scripts/smoke/artifacts/<runId>/`. The harness writes/diffs against `scripts/smoke/baselines/<id>.summary.json` so subsequent ADR-074 slices (P1 stable prefix, V1 voice DNA, M1/M2/M3 memory + compaction, L1/R2/R3 tool loop) can prove "input tokens ↓ ≥5x" and "no tool regression" with one command instead of subjective rereads. Focused tests in `apps/api/test/internal-smoke-receipts.controller.test.ts` cover happy-path mapping, `requestId`/`afterCursor`/`limit` filter propagation, limit clamping, validation errors, and unauthorized rejection. Default `SMOKE_API_BASE_URL` is `http://127.0.0.1:3001` (pure-local) but the harness is also live-dev compatible after `kubectl port-forward` per `docs/LIVE-TEST-HYBRID.md`.
- **Trial plan lifecycle hardening - rollout-safe activations, auto-trialing on apply, saveable trial drafts:** `apps/api/src/modules/workspace-management/application/seed-tool-catalog.service.ts` now only backfills `planCatalogToolActivation` for the existing default `starter_trial` plan when the plan has zero activations; any admin-edited tool activation (e.g. enabling `image_generate` or raising `web_search` daily limits through `/admin/plans`) is no longer silently overwritten with the hardcoded `STARTER_TRIAL_TOOL_POLICY` on every API pod rollout. `apps/api/src/modules/workspace-management/application/manage-admin-workspace-subscription.service.ts` now looks up the target plan through `AssistantPlanCatalogRepository.findByCode` and, when the plan is marked `isTrialPlan=true` with a positive `trialDurationDays` and the admin did not pass any of `status` / `trialStartedAt` / `trialEndsAt` explicitly, auto-fills `status="trialing"`, `trialStartedAt=now`, and `trialEndsAt=now + trialDurationDays * 24h`, so the `/admin/ops` one-click `Apply workspace subscription` actually produces a trialing subscription instead of an `active` row with null trial windows on a plan that is cataloged as a trial. `apps/web/app/admin/plans/page.tsx` now auto-fills `trialDurationDays=14` the moment the operator toggles the `Trial` checkbox (if the number field was empty) and disables the `Save` / `Save changes` button with an inline `Trial plan needs trialDurationDays > 0` hint while the trial duration remains empty or non-positive, so `parseTrialDuration` can no longer reject the whole plan form with a cryptic 400 after the roundtrip. Focused tests extend `apps/api/test/seed-tool-catalog.test.ts` to lock the new idempotent backfill semantics and `apps/api/test/manage-admin-workspace-subscription.service.test.ts` to lock trial auto-defaulting, explicit-admin-override precedence, and non-trial-plan behavior.
- **Web stream cadence watchdog with one safe retry + API logger flush fix:** `apps/api/src/main.ts` now explicitly calls `app.flushLogs()` after `app.init()` because the API uses `app.init()` + manual `createServer().listen()` instead of `app.listen()`, and `bufferLogs: true` was leaving every `Logger.log/.warn` from services (including the new `web_stream_timing` telemetry) buffered forever in production. The previous slice's slow-motion telemetry was therefore landed but invisible in `apps/api` pod stdout; this fix unblocks the entire web-stream observability surface end-to-end. On top of that, `apps/api/src/modules/workspace-management/application/cadence-watchdog.ts` (new) introduces a small always-on `CadenceWatchdog` that detects two stall shapes during a streaming web turn — a hard "silent" gap with no deltas for `silentMs` after arming, and a sustained "slow_avg" inter-delta average over a rolling window — and `apps/api/src/modules/workspace-management/application/stream-web-chat-turn.service.ts` now drives one provider-stream attempt at a time through a new `streamRuntimeAttempt` helper inside a bounded retry loop (`WEB_TURN_MAX_STREAM_ATTEMPTS=2`). When the watchdog fires before any tool/media side effect, the in-flight runtime stream is aborted via a combined `AbortSignal`, a `stream_reset` SSE event is emitted to the client, and a fresh upstream attempt starts; structured `web_stream_stall_detected/attempted/recovered/unrecovered` log lines are emitted regardless of the `/admin` Trace toggle since stall detection is critical even when the rich `web_stream_timing` line is off. `apps/api/src/modules/workspace-management/interface/http/assistant.controller.ts` now wires an `onStreamReset` callback into the SSE writer, `apps/web/app/app/assistant-api-client.ts` recognizes the new `stream_reset` event in the SSE parser and exposes an `onStreamReset` handler, and `apps/web/app/app/_components/use-chat.ts` clears any pending streamed text/thought (and the corresponding assistant message body) when the event arrives, so the user sees the partial slow stream replaced by the retried output instead of a silent hang or a duplicated tail. `apps/api/test/cadence-watchdog.test.ts` (new) locks silent-stall, slow-avg, single-firing, and dispose semantics with a deterministic fake clock, and `apps/api/test/stream-web-chat-turn.service.test.ts` was hardened so the existing `web_stream_timing` regex matches the actual structured log line instead of test-reporter output.
- **Web stream slow-motion telemetry behind admin Trace toggle:** `apps/api/src/modules/workspace-management/application/stream-web-chat-turn.service.ts`, `apps/api/src/modules/workspace-management/application/stream-native-web-chat-turn.service.ts`, `apps/api/src/modules/workspace-management/interface/http/assistant.controller.ts`, `apps/runtime/src/modules/turns/interface/http/turns.controller.ts`, `apps/runtime/src/modules/turns/turn-execution.service.ts`, `apps/runtime/src/modules/turns/provider-gateway.client.service.ts`, `apps/provider-gateway/src/modules/providers/interface/http/provider-text-generation.controller.ts`, plus three new `stream-writer-instrumentation.ts` helpers (one per app) now emit a richer `web_stream_timing` line with per-delta cadence (`interDeltaMaxMs`, `interDeltaP95Ms`, sample count), post-tool first-delta delays, tool round counts, and SSE/NDJSON writer backpressure stats (write count, backpressure events, max/p95 drain ms) end-to-end across `web -> api -> runtime -> provider-gateway`. The new telemetry is gated on the existing `OverviewLatencyTraceService` Trace ON/OFF toggle on `/admin` and only activates when `x-persai-trace: on` is propagated downstream, so production logs stay quiet by default while operators can flip the toggle to capture the next intermittent “slow motion” web stream and pin it to a specific stage (SSE backpressure, runtime tool refresh, provider-gateway writes, or upstream cadence) instead of one opaque delay. `apps/runtime` also now logs `[turn-stream-refresh]` with `refreshProviderRequestMessagesMs` after durable compaction so the heavy synchronous re-hydration between tool rounds is visible in the same trace window.
- **Telegram webhook timeout + safe media-copy fix:** `infra/helm/templates/api-service.yaml`, new `infra/helm/templates/api-backendconfig.yaml`, and `infra/helm/values*.yaml` now give `api` the same long-running GCLB `BackendConfig` protection already used for `web`, so `/telegram-webhook` is no longer stuck on the default `~30s` backend timeout path. The same fix also hardens `apps/api/src/modules/workspace-management/application/media/media-delivery.service.ts` so repersisting a `persai_object_storage` artifact only deletes the original object when it is an ephemeral `runtime-output` blob, preventing live chat-attachment objects under `assistant-media/.../chats/...` from being deleted out from under later hydration/delivery.
- **Telegram delivery/profile polish after native cutover:** `apps/api/src/modules/workspace-management/application/telegram-bot.client.service.ts` now suppresses the extra plain-text Telegram reply when media was already delivered and that media already carries a visible caption, avoiding the duplicate “file + same text again” artifact on the live bot path. The same follow-through also restores real publish-time Telegram bot profile sync in `apps/api/src/modules/workspace-management/application/publish-assistant-draft.service.ts`: active Telegram bindings now update bot name through `setMyName`, and uploaded assistant avatars are pushed through Telegram's native bot profile photo API instead of only patching local binding metadata.
- **Provider stream cadence hardening for web chat:** `apps/provider-gateway/src/modules/providers/interface/http/provider-text-generation.controller.ts` no longer batches consecutive `text_delta` events behind a fixed timer window before writing NDJSON to runtime. The gateway now forwards provider deltas immediately, removing one artificial pacing seam from the live `provider -> runtime -> api -> web` path that could make already-slow upstream token cadence look like a broken “slow motion” web stream.
- **Files tool retry hardening for save flows:** `apps/runtime/src/modules/turns/runtime-files-tool.service.ts` now accepts `filename` as a compatibility fallback save target for `files.write` and `files.write_and_send` when a model omits `path`, so the runtime can complete the first tool call instead of forcing a second retry loop. The same follow-through strengthens model-facing guidance in `apps/runtime/src/modules/turns/native-tool-projection.ts`, `apps/api/prisma/tool-catalog-data.ts`, and `apps/api/src/modules/workspace-management/application/runtime-tool-policy.ts` to keep `path` as the canonical save location while `filename` remains only the delivery-name override.
- **Assistant workspace redesign slice - cleanup/delete semantics, cleaner file listings, and final delivery-honesty persistence:** `packages/runtime-contract/src/index.ts`, `apps/runtime/src/modules/turns/native-tool-projection.ts`, `apps/runtime/src/modules/turns/runtime-files-tool.service.ts`, and `apps/sandbox/src/sandbox.service.ts` now expose a real `files.delete` action with recursive directory delete support and root-safety checks, while default `files.list` output now groups entries into cleaner `workspace` / `uploads` / `artifacts` sections instead of dumping service-noise paths raw. The same follow-through also moves the final delivery-honesty correction to the actual web delivery boundary: `apps/api/src/modules/workspace-management/application/final-delivery-honesty.ts`, `send-web-chat-turn.service.ts`, `stream-web-chat-turn.service.ts`, and the assistant-chat repository now correct stored assistant text only after `MediaDeliveryService` proves whether any attachment was really delivered.
- **Admin plan quota truth refresh - explicit `Knowledge storage (MB)` replaces the stale visible workspace-disk knob:** `apps/api` plan-management types/services, `packages/contracts/openapi.yaml`, regenerated `@persai/contracts`, and `apps/web/app/admin/plans/page.tsx` now surface `knowledgeStorageBytesLimit` as the current plan-owned storage control for indexed knowledge sources. The primary Admin Plans UI now shows `Knowledge storage (MB)` directly instead of keeping the older `Workspace disk (MB)` as the main visible operator control, while preserving backend compatibility for the underlying field.
- **Native web stream latency-trace hardening:** `apps/api/src/modules/workspace-management/application/stream-web-chat-turn.service.ts` and `apps/api/src/modules/workspace-management/interface/http/assistant.controller.ts` now keep one trace across `prepare`, replay claim, SSE `started`, runtime request, and first delta; `apps/runtime/src/modules/turns/turn-execution.service.ts` now attaches structured `stream_turn` runtime trace stages such as `prepare.*`, `provider_headers_received`, `first_provider_event`, and `first_text_delta`; and `apps/runtime/src/modules/turns/provider-gateway.client.service.ts` now logs elapsed time to provider headers so the next real slow-stream case can be pinned to API prep, runtime prep, upstream headers, or token generation instead of being treated as one opaque delay.
- **Assistant workspace redesign slice - atomic `files.write_and_send` plus delivery-honesty guard:** `packages/runtime-contract/src/index.ts` now defines `write_and_send` as a first-class `files` action, and `apps/runtime/src/modules/turns/runtime-files-tool.service.ts` now uses one atomic path that persists the file, keeps the canonical `fileRef`, and queues outbound delivery in the same tool result instead of depending on a second model decision. The same slice updates model-facing `files` guidance in `apps/runtime/src/modules/turns/native-tool-projection.ts`, `apps/api/prisma/tool-catalog-data.ts`, and `apps/api/src/modules/workspace-management/application/runtime-tool-policy.ts` to prefer `files.write_and_send` for “create/save and immediately send” requests, and `apps/runtime/src/modules/turns/turn-execution.service.ts` now fail-closes delivery claims by appending an explicit correction when the model says a file was sent but the completed turn produced no delivered artifact. Focused runtime/API tests, lint, typecheck, and format checks were rerun for the new atomic path.
- **Assistant workspace redesign slice - remove redundant files mount seam and harden explicit mount cleanup:** `apps/runtime/src/modules/turns/runtime-files-tool.service.ts` no longer sends `files.read` / `files.write` / `files.edit` through sandbox jobs with ambient `mountedFileRefs` or target `fileRef` mount dependency; the canonical files path now executes against the hydrated assistant workspace by resolved `relativePath`. `apps/sandbox/src/sandbox.service.ts` also now scopes explicit mounted refs to the current `assistantId + workspaceId`, removes stale `assistant_files` rows when a mounted blob is missing, skips stale ambient mounts safely, and fails required explicit mounts structurally with `file_ref_not_found` instead of crashing the pod. Focused runtime/sandbox tests and typechecks were rerun for the changed paths.
- **Assistant workspace redesign slice - prod cleanup for legacy plan activations and stale workspace blobs:** `apps/api/src/modules/workspace-management/infrastructure/persistence/prisma-assistant-plan-catalog.repository.ts` now filters Admin Plans tool activations against the canonical current tool catalog and only syncs plan activations for current live tool codes, while `apps/api/prisma/migrations/20260419233000_remove_legacy_plan_file_tool_activations/migration.sql` physically deletes historical `read_file` / `write_file` / `edit_file` / `send_media_to_user` plan activation rows from DB truth. The same slice also hardens `apps/sandbox/src/sandbox.service.ts` so assistant workspace hydrate fails closed on missing object-storage blobs: stale `assistant_files` rows are removed from canonical truth, broken blobs are skipped, and the local workspace is rebuilt from the remaining accessible files instead of crash-looping the sandbox pod. Focused API/sandbox tests plus lint/typecheck were rerun for the changed paths.
- **Assistant workspace redesign slice - final Step 20 files.send seam collapse:** `apps/runtime/src/modules/turns/runtime-files-tool.service.ts` now resolves `files.send` end to end instead of delegating to a separate `RuntimeSendMediaToUserService`, `packages/runtime-contract/src/index.ts` no longer defines a standalone `send_media_to_user` result shape, and `apps/runtime/src/modules/turns/turns.module.ts` no longer registers a separate send-media provider. The same slice also moves removed split public file-tool cleanup out of startup bookkeeping into `apps/api/prisma/migrations/20260419220000_deactivate_removed_legacy_public_file_tools/migration.sql`, letting `apps/api` stop carrying explicit legacy file-tool deactivation code in the active control-plane path. Focused runtime coverage was folded into `apps/runtime/test/runtime-files-tool.service.test.ts`, so the active Step 20 runtime path is now one canonical `files` service for `search/get/read/write/edit/send`.
- **Assistant workspace redesign slice - sandbox residue cleanup and clean internal files execution:** `apps/api/prisma/schema.prisma` no longer models `SandboxFileRef`, `apps/api/prisma/migrations/20260419203000_drop_sandbox_file_refs_residue/migration.sql` drops `sandbox_file_refs` from current DB truth, and `apps/runtime` plus `apps/sandbox` now execute internal file work through one `files` sandbox job code with explicit `action` payloads instead of `read_file` / `write_file` / `edit_file`. `apps/api/src/modules/workspace-management/application/resolve-admin-ops-cockpit.service.ts` now counts persisted outputs from canonical `assistantFiles`, and focused runtime/sandbox/API tests now lock the clean active path. This moves the repo from “architecturally still carrying sandbox-era file residue” to “ready for live Step 20 smoke after migration apply and deploy.”
- **Assistant workspace redesign slice - multi-pod assistant workspace lease:** `apps/api/prisma/schema.prisma` and `apps/api/prisma/migrations/20260419190000_assistant_workspace_lease_foundation/migration.sql` now add a real `assistant_workspace_leases` table, while `apps/sandbox/src/sandbox.service.ts` now acquires, renews, and releases a Postgres-backed lease before mutating any assistant workspace. The active sandbox path now fails closed on lease loss, keeps `persist/delete` behind live lease ownership, invalidates stale pod-local workspace caches with a state marker derived from canonical `assistant_files`, and `apps/sandbox/test/sandbox.service.test.ts` now proves same-workspace contention, expired-lease reclaim, cross-workspace parallelism, and failure reset back to persisted truth. `apps/runtime/src/modules/turns/sandbox-client.service.ts` also extends completion waiting to account for queued-after-contention sandbox work instead of timing out on the new serialized path.
- **Assistant workspace redesign slice - durable assistant workspace landing:** `apps/sandbox/src/sandbox.service.ts` no longer runs sandbox jobs in a fresh per-job tmp workspace that is deleted after each call. The active sandbox path now uses one assistant/workspace-scoped local session root, serializes jobs per assistant/workspace, restores that workspace from canonical `AssistantFile` rows on cold start, persists changed files back into `assistant_files`, deletes removed paths from current assistant workspace truth, and keeps stable file ids by updating existing assistant-file rows in place for the same relative path. `apps/sandbox/test/sandbox.service.test.ts` now proves `write -> separate read job -> edit with stable fileRef -> cold restore -> read` directly.
- **Assistant workspace redesign slice - split public file-tool alias collapse:** the control-plane/runtime file model no longer keeps `read_file`, `write_file`, `edit_file`, or `send_media_to_user` alive as public tool aliases. `apps/api/prisma/tool-catalog-data.ts` now keeps only canonical `files` + `exec` + `shell` in the active public sandbox-related catalog, startup/manual seeding now deactivates stale DB rows for the removed legacy public file tools, admin plan/policy surfaces no longer carry special hidden-file filters for them, and `apps/runtime/src/modules/turns/turn-execution.service.ts` no longer dispatches those legacy names directly. This removes a real control-plane/runtime alias layer; the remaining big gap is durable assistant workspace behavior, not more file-tool renaming.
- **Assistant workspace redesign slice - AssistantFile live cutover:** the active runtime/sandbox file plane no longer runs through `SandboxFileRef` compatibility reads or dual-writes. `apps/runtime/src/modules/turns/runtime-assistant-file-registry.service.ts` now resolves file refs only from `assistant_files`, `apps/sandbox/src/sandbox.service.ts` now mounts/persists/completes sandbox files only through `AssistantFile`, and `apps/sandbox/test/sandbox.service.test.ts` plus focused runtime tests now lock the canonical-only path. This makes `AssistantFile` the actual live file-id truth for the active `files` path, while durable assistant workspace/session behavior and final schema/control-plane cleanup remain open.
- **Assistant workspace redesign slice - clean Prompt Constructor file vocabulary:** admin prompt-tool editing now stays on the clean public model instead of carrying split legacy file-tool names forward. `apps/web/app/admin/presets/page.tsx` now orders and filters the file surface as `files`, `exec`, `shell`, and `apps/api/src/modules/workspace-management/application/manage-admin-tool-prompt-metadata.service.ts` now rejects direct metadata edits for legacy public file tool codes such as `read_file` and `send_media_to_user`.
- **Assistant workspace redesign slice - assistant-file sandbox result-path hardening:** the previous `AssistantFile` foundation slice had a real enforcement gap on the live sandbox HTTP path: `apps/sandbox` was already persisting canonical `AssistantFile` rows, but completed job polling still serialized `SandboxFileRef.id` because `pollJob()` only read `job.fileRefs`. `apps/sandbox/src/sandbox.service.ts` now prefers `SandboxJob.assistantFiles` when returning completed `files[]`, falls back to legacy file refs only for older jobs/compatibility, and `apps/sandbox/test/sandbox.service.test.ts` now locks both canonical-first and legacy-fallback behavior.
- **Assistant workspace redesign slice - assistant file registry foundation:** the repo now has a real canonical `AssistantFile` data model instead of only a runtime seam over `SandboxFileRef`. `apps/api/prisma/schema.prisma` and `apps/api/prisma/migrations/20260419153000_assistant_file_registry_foundation/migration.sql` add/backfill `assistant_files`, `apps/runtime` now resolves public/runtime file refs from `AssistantFile` first with legacy fallback only for compatibility, and `apps/sandbox` now persists sandbox outputs into `AssistantFile` while returning assistant-file ids to runtime/tool consumers. This is a meaningful product/infra step toward the target `files + assistant registry` model, but it is not the durable workspace end state yet: sandbox execution still uses per-job workspaces and `SandboxFileRef` still exists as an internal compatibility layer.
- **Assistant workspace redesign slice - assistant-level file registry seam:** runtime file resolution no longer has three separate direct `sandbox_file_refs` access paths. `apps/runtime` now has `RuntimeAssistantFileRegistryService` as one assistant/workspace-scoped seam for file lookup, search, attachment-backed file registration, and runtime item mapping; `RuntimeFilesToolService`, attachment hydration, and media resend/delivery resolution now all depend on that one seam. This is still an internal migration/prep slice rather than the final file-registry product landing: the backing store remains `SandboxFileRef`, but runtime code now has one place to swap when the real assistant file model lands.
- **Assistant workspace redesign slice - unified `files` public surface:** the native runtime now has a canonical public `files` tool with `search/get/read/write/edit/send` actions, wired through `RuntimeFilesToolService` and projected to the model instead of the older public `read_file` / `write_file` / `edit_file` / `send_media_to_user` split. Control-plane/tooling vocabulary also starts matching that model: the tool catalog now includes `files`, prompt-constructor ordering prefers `files`, admin plan editing hides the legacy public file tool rows, and runtime tool-policy materialization maps old inventory rows onto runtime `files` as a compatibility seam while keeping `shell` / `exec` separate. This is still a public-surface migration slice, not the full end state: the backing registry remains `SandboxFileRef`-based and the durable assistant workspace is not landed yet.
- **ADR-073 Step 20 sandbox continuity + attachment fileRefs:** the sandbox path no longer forgets its own files between model-visible sandbox tool calls inside one turn. `apps/runtime` now preserves produced `fileRef`s in turn state and remounts them into later sandbox jobs, so flows like `write_file -> shell/exec/read_file` operate on the same workspace contents instead of silently restarting from empty state. The same hardening also makes attachment resend behavior more honest: sandbox tool results now expose top-level `fileRefs`, `TurnContextHydrationService` lazily canonicalizes existing chat attachments into `sandbox_file_refs`, and attachment summaries shown to the model now include direct `fileRef`s so `send_media_to_user` can resend older user/assistant files without filename guessing. A separate sandbox fix also prevents missing executables from crashing the whole sandbox pod by converting `spawn ... ENOENT` into a structured `process_spawn_failed` job result.
- **ADR-073 Step 20 sandbox persistence migration fix:** live `persai-dev` sandbox requests were failing with Prisma `P2021` because the `SandboxJob` / `SandboxFileRef` schema existed in `apps/api/prisma/schema.prisma` but the corresponding database migration had never been added. `apps/api/prisma/migrations/20260419010000_step20_sandbox_persistence_foundation/migration.sql` now creates the missing `sandbox_job_status` / `sandbox_file_origin` enums plus the `sandbox_jobs` and `sandbox_file_refs` tables, indexes, and foreign keys so the live sandbox service can persist jobs and file refs instead of returning `sandbox_failed` `500`s on first tool execution.
- **ADR-073 Step 20 sandbox live-test prep wiring:** `apps/web` `Prompt Constructor` now keeps the Step 20 sandbox/delivery tools in the same UI ordering as the backend prompt-constructor catalog, so their admin-editable model descriptions and usage guidance stay visible beside the older tools instead of drifting to fallback order. The same prep slice also adds `sandbox` to the dev Helm/image-publish path with a real service/deployment/env wiring (`RUNTIME_SANDBOX_BASE_URL=http://sandbox:3013`), updates live-test docs to include sandbox readiness plus the first honest web smoke contract, and refreshes ADR/roadmap truth so Step 20 is no longer described as fully deferred after the code already landed the baseline.
- **ADR-073 Step 20 sandbox ops cockpit truth:** `apps/api` `ResolveAdminOpsCockpitService` and `apps/web` `Admin > Ops` now surface assistant-scoped sandbox operator truth instead of leaving it implicit in stored rows only. The cockpit now exposes the effective active sandbox policy, daily sandbox-job usage/remaining quota counters, and recent `SandboxJob` telemetry including blocked reasons, persisted file counts, and recorded `resourceUsage` peaks; `packages/contracts/openapi.yaml` plus regenerated `@persai/contracts` were updated to keep that admin payload honest, and `apps/api/test/resolve-admin-ops-cockpit.service.test.ts` now covers the new mapping.
- **ADR-073 Step 20 sandbox process-tree guardrails:** `apps/sandbox/src/sandbox.service.ts` now enforces `maxConcurrentProcesses`, `maxCpuMsPerJob`, and `maxMemoryBytesPerJob` against the full `exec` / `shell` process tree instead of leaving those plan/admin/runtime-contract fields as paper policy. The same slice also records peak process count, peak CPU ms, peak memory bytes, and process duration in persisted `SandboxJob.resourceUsage` rows, while `apps/sandbox/test/sandbox.service.test.ts` now covers process-tree fanout, memory-limit, and CPU-budget rejection directly.
- **ADR-073 Step 20 sandbox/media delivery checkpoint:** the current Step 20 branch now has the first real local baseline for sandbox-owned file/process execution, plan-owned sandbox guardrails, canonical `SandboxFileRef` persistence, and the separate `send_media_to_user` tool seam across `apps/api`, `apps/runtime`, `apps/sandbox`, `packages/runtime-contract`, `packages/runtime-bundle`, and Admin Plans. The same follow-through also removes the earlier Telegram split-brain outbound media path: `MediaDeliveryService` now passes a real channel target into adapters, `TelegramMediaAdapter` is a live outbound adapter instead of a no-op placeholder, `handle-internal-telegram-turn.service.ts` no longer performs direct media side-send itself, and Telegram media delivery now preserves `caption` on the actual Bot API upload path. Later bounded fixes on top of that seam now also keep `send_media_to_user` honest for already-produced current-turn artifacts by avoiding duplicate artifact-cap counting and applying later overrides by artifact id, while `apps/sandbox` now treats canonical mounted `fileRef` inputs more honestly by allowing `read_file` via `fileRef` alone and by not re-persisting unchanged mounted inputs as fresh sandbox outputs. Focused runtime/API/sandbox verification now covers those local semantics directly, including a mini native runtime loop proof for `write_file -> produced fileRef -> send_media_to_user -> final artifact` plus explicit API-boundary proof that web persists the returned artifact through `MediaDeliveryService` and Telegram routes the same artifact through the shared delivery seam once, with `mediaAlreadyDelivered` preventing duplicate Bot API sends. The latest guardrail follow-through also turns two previously soft policy fields into real enforcement: sandbox jobs are now blocked up front once `sandboxJobsPerDay` is exhausted, and `send_media_to_user` now enforces `web`/`Telegram` outbound byte caps against the final combined artifact set for the turn rather than only spot-checking each artifact in isolation.
- **ADR-073 Step 19 core closeout + final-tail reorder:** active repo-truth docs now treat deploy/restart/pod-replacement recovery and the current `/admin` `System Overview` pod-status visibility as completed on the native path, based on already-landed code and bounded live rollout evidence. The only remaining scale-related follow-through is now the final bounded load-readiness proof plus any rollout-speed/image-pull cleanup, explicitly kept as the last post-ADR-072 program step instead of an active blocker for the main path.
- **Early router live validation + provider stream batching follow-through:** `persai-dev` is now confirmed on the post-router-fix images (`api` / `web` / `runtime` at `da05e06`), and bounded live checks confirmed the earlier one-off web-turn `runtime_bundle_hash_mismatch` failure is no longer reproducing on the observed path after rollout. The same follow-through also tightened transport behavior for occasional “slow motion” text streams by batching consecutive provider-gateway `text_delta` chunks before flushing them across the remaining runtime/API/browser hops, reducing pathological micro-delta fanout without changing tool/result boundaries.
- **Step 19 pod-truth repair + session-backed web proxy auth:** `infra/helm/templates/api-deployment.yaml` now injects full `runtime-headless.<namespace>.svc.cluster.local` / `provider-gateway-headless.<namespace>.svc.cluster.local` discovery names so `/admin` `System Overview` can resolve real per-pod runtime/provider-gateway endpoints instead of falling back to false `opaque` / `0/2 ready endpoints` when Node DNS rejects the short names. The same pack also teaches `apps/web` `app/api/v1/[[...path]]/route.ts` to mint a fresh Clerk bearer from the current server-side session when the caller omitted `Authorization`, reducing one-minute token friction for same-origin browser-session-backed smoke tooling, and aligns active proxy config truth by updating `apps/web/Dockerfile` plus `docs/LIVE-TEST-HYBRID.md` to use `PERSAI_WEB_API_PROXY_TARGET=http://...:3001` without the duplicated `/api/v1` suffix.
- **Step 19 live deploy-recovery confirmation:** the current runtime rollout-recovery fix is now validated on the live `persai-dev` path, not only in local verification. The normal `main -> Dev Image Publish -> values-dev pin -> Argo CD rollout` flow was observed through completion on `6de0f36`, both new `runtime` pods reached `Ready`, entered service, and handled real turn traffic without reproducing the earlier `runtime_bundle_missing` / `503` deploy-time failure, so the main `Step 19` deploy blocker is now considered closed on the observed dev rollout path. The remaining rollout residual is long image-pull / convergence time rather than bundle warm recovery.
- **ADR-073 lifecycle closeout + Step 19 readiness framing:** repo-truth docs now close the remaining create/recreate lifecycle slice on the active path. The explicit setup wizard, centered/polished setup UI, and explicit post-publish handoff into the welcome chat are now treated as the accepted lifecycle contract for the current path, while the lack of a separate backend lifecycle command and the local-until-publish uploaded-avatar preview behavior are no longer kept open as blockers for this slice. The same docs sync also sharpens `Step 19` as deploy/restart/pod-replacement recovery plus bounded load-readiness proof for the native path, with `/admin` `System Overview` called out as the operator surface for honest discovered pod status/readiness and fleet-pressure truth.
- **Early turn router rollout + admin/UI follow-through:** the active path now uses a configurable early `turn_routing` layer with deterministic precheck plus an optional cheap classifier, driven by admin-managed `routingFastModelKey`, `routerPolicy`, and `router_classifier` prompt state. `Admin > Runtime` now exposes per-category trigger editing for `continue`, `retrieval`, `reasoning`, `premium writing`, and `tool/browse` precheck hints instead of a raw JSON-only override field, and web chat can surface the latest shadow routing choice to the assistant owner/admin as a compact under-message badge like `premium (llm)` or `reasoning (precheck)` via a minimal `turnRouting { mode, executionMode, source }` transport snapshot. Explicit smart/deep-mode turns still clamp to `premium_reply` or `reasoning`, but active repo-truth docs no longer describe hidden `route_control` as the current routing core.
- **ADR-073 Economics Slice C prod closeout:** the active knowledge plane is no longer documented as `pattern_only`. `apps/api` now persists durable retrieval observability through Prisma `KnowledgeRetrievalEvent` / `KnowledgeRetrievalRollup`, `read-assistant-knowledge.service.ts` now serves a real bounded hybrid retrieval path across assistant-private and global knowledge (including uploaded global documents), `runtime-knowledge-access` now publishes `ragMode: "hybrid"`, and Admin Knowledge now has first-class `/api/v1/admin/knowledge-sources*` list/upload/delete/reindex/observability/connectors surfaces plus a real admin dashboard in `apps/web`. The same closeout also moved retrieval budgets/helper controls into plan-managed policy, added an explicit governance seam and workspace-quota enforcement for admin global-knowledge writes, regenerated OpenAPI/contracts for the new admin knowledge surface, refreshed ADR/program/docs truth around the landed Slice C baseline, and reran full repo lint/format/typecheck/test verification before closing the slice.
- **ADR-073 Slice B completion + admin business economics metrics:** the active prompt-cache-first context architecture is now closed on the current path instead of remaining an open design note. `apps/runtime` now treats stable cache prefixes as explicit versioned block families (`ordinary_prompt`, `durable_memory`, `shared_compaction_summary`) when building ordinary/deep OpenAI cache keys, `TurnContextHydrationService` now formats hydrated durable-memory/shared-summary prefixes through those shared stable-block helpers, and `/admin/business` now exposes rolling averaged completed-turn economics from persisted runtime receipts (`avg input`, `avg cached input`, `avg output`, `avg total`, cache-hit turn rate, cache-share percent, average usage steps) so operators can see real cache behavior without live log tailing.
- **ADR-073 Slice B hydrated stable-prefix routing:** ordinary/deep OpenAI cache routing now also fingerprints the leading hydrated stable context blocks that matter on real turns, not just the compiled ordinary system shell. `TurnExecutionService` now derives `prompt_cache_key` from the materialized ordinary stable prompt hash plus any leading `durable memory` / shared-compaction-summary assistant messages, and it recomputes that key when post-tool compaction refreshes the hydrated message list so cached-input routing stays aligned with the real long-lived prefix.
- **ADR-073 Slice B ordinary stable-prefix materialization:** the runtime bundle now materializes an explicit stable-prefix record for the compiled ordinary prompt, and ordinary-turn OpenAI cache routing now keys off that prompt-owned identity plus turn-variant state instead of relying only on coarse bundle metadata. `CompilePromptConstructorService` and `packages/runtime-bundle` now persist `ordinary.stablePrefix { text, hash }`, while `apps/runtime` uses that materialized prompt identity when building cache keys for ordinary/deep turns so Slice B moves one step closer to real prompt-family/block ownership without changing user-facing warmth or tone.
- **ADR-073 Economics Slice B cache-routing baseline:** the active OpenAI text path now carries provider-side prompt-cache hints instead of waiting for a full prompt-assembly rewrite before any live economics gain is possible. `packages/runtime-contract` now supports text-request `promptCache` metadata, `apps/runtime` now derives stable OpenAI `prompt_cache_key` plus explicit in-memory retention hints for ordinary/deep turns and shared compaction work, and `apps/provider-gateway` now forwards those hints to the OpenAI Responses API while keeping other providers untouched. A live `persai-dev` probe also confirmed that the current active path can already realize large cached-input reuse on repeated long prefixes (`0 -> 6912 cachedInputTokens` on back-to-back `gpt-5.4-mini` requests), while ADR-073 remains honest that stable prompt-block materialization, broader helper-family minimization, and first-class observability are still open follow-through inside Slice B.
- **ADR-073 Economics Slice A ready + live hardening follow-through:** repo-truth docs now mark the first economics slice as landed on the active path: plan-scoped `normal` / `premium` / `reasoning` / hidden `system-tool` / optional `retrieval` slots, the configurable early `turn_routing` layer, explicit deeper-thinking mode, and honest per-call `input` / `cached input` / `output` accounting are now treated as complete, with `Slice B` prompt-cache-first context architecture as the next active economics step. The same follow-through pack also hardens live behavior by normalizing Unicode-hyphen model ids across control-plane/runtime/provider-gateway seams, teaching the browser to ignore `NEXT_PUBLIC_API_BASE_URL=localhost` in live and fall back to same-origin `/api/v1`, accepting `admin.plan.delete` in the dangerous-action step-up challenge parser, polishing the chat header toggle, chat badge wording, and Clerk avatar fallback behavior, and clarifying in ADR-073 that knowledge-search helper work should use the plan-owned `retrieval` slot with the smallest viable task-specific prompt instead of paying for the full conversational system shell.
- **ADR-073 economics architecture refresh:** `docs/ADR/073-post-adr072-residue-and-polish-program.md` and `docs/ROADMAP.md` now preserve the updated four-part economics direction explicitly: plan-scoped model slots for `normal` / `premium or reasoning` / `system-tool` work, prompt-cache-first context assembly with provider-native cached input as the main savings lever, knowledge correction around current `pattern_only` retrieval plus a later retrieval-specialized model path, and honest hidden-work accounting across `input`, `cached input`, and `output`. The active execution plan was also regrouped into larger economics slices so future sessions do not lose this contract.
- **ADR-073 explicit recreate/recover setup path:** the setup wizard no longer hides recreate/recover behind a `POST /assistant` `409 already existed` fallback. `apps/web` now detects an existing assistant on entry, switches into an explicit `recover` or `recreate` mode, reuses the existing assistant record during preview/publish without retrying create, and keeps the final CTA/user copy honest about whether the user is creating, recovering, or recreating. Focused setup web coverage now protects both the `recover existing draft` and `recreate after reset` flows.
- **ADR-073 user UI polish + custom Clerk account flows:** user-facing surfaces are now denser and clearer across the app. `assistant settings` now has a balanced desktop layout, a real primary `Save` CTA, simplified voice selection, a clearer behavior/instructions editor, collapsed advanced sliders, a fixed uploaded-avatar shape, paged memory, and collapsed task panels. Chat/sidebar UX now adds explicit `Deleting...` feedback, a smaller compaction banner with 20-message snooze semantics, and collapsed integrations with a live green indicator. Custom account/auth screens now support editable profile fields, avatar upload, password change, and a real custom Clerk forgot-password flow reachable from both `sign-in` and `sign-up`, with focused web tests covering the new recovery path.
- **ADR-073 post-ADR-072 program baseline:** added `docs/ADR/073-post-adr072-residue-and-polish-program.md` as the active program ADR after the Step 18 native-path closeout. The new ADR pulls the remaining ADR-072 work into one ordered program: create/recreate lifecycle polish, user UI polish, memory/knowledge/cache/model-routing economics, Step 19 deploy/recovery hardening, and the deferred Step 15a/Step 20 follow-through. Active docs, runbooks, and the roadmap now point to ADR-073 instead of acting as if ADR-072 is still the live execution program.
- **ADR-072 Step 18 closeout status sync:** active UI/control-plane/runtime cleanup is now complete. The last live `legacy_openclaw_default` provider-settings mode was neutralized to `unconfigured_default`, repo-truth Prisma no longer models the dead `platform_runtime_provider_settings.optimization_policy` field, the remaining `openclaw-*` assistant capability/channel helper file paths and focused API tests were renamed to neutral assistant/channel/capability naming, and the last live `openclawSecretRef` compatibility alias was removed from active code paths. Step 19 scale-hardening is now the next planned execution step.
- **ADR-072 Step 18 admin runtime page cleanup:** `/admin/runtime` no longer renders the stale `Sandbox security` / per-tier sandbox matrix block, and the corresponding admin runtime contract no longer returns `tierSecurityPolicies` or the old `optimizationPolicy` payload. Follow-up cleanup also removed the stale `Heartbeat`, `Context Pruning`, `OpenAI Tuning`, old compaction threshold editors, and the last legacy web compaction message-count override after verifying they no longer drive the active native runtime path. The page now keeps provider routing, model catalog, and API keys only; native context pressure stays plan-owned through `runtime.contextHydration`, while `runtime.sharedCompaction` remains an internal runtime contract only. Browser autofill/autocorrect is disabled on editable fields, and the layout uses a denser `System Overview`-style layout instead of the older roomy control-panel cards.
- **ADR-072 Step 18 admin overview multi-pod cleanup:** `/admin` `System Overview` no longer exposes the old pod selector / sticky-route debug UX or the stale `Web Runtime Shadow Compare` block. The page now probes and pins discovered `api` pods behind the service, aggregates latency/request/process totals across that discovered fleet, fans the `Trace` toggle out across discovered pods, annotates merged trace samples with their source pod, and replaces the old `Runtime Tiers` matrix with a native runtime fleet/Step 19 view so the active admin surface stops pretending the primary runtime model is pod-local or tier-shaped.
- **ADR-072 Step 18 pre-UI infra/runtime cleanup:** `infra/helm` no longer renders `openclaw-*` workloads, services, service accounts, HPAs, or PDBs; `bot.persai.dev/telegram-webhook` now stays explicitly tied to `api.telegramWebhook` instead of an `openclaw` values gate; native dev secrets now read from neutral `persai-runtime-secrets`; and non-UI `apps/api` materialization helper schemas/classes now use neutral assistant-channel/assistant-capability naming instead of `persai.openclaw*`. Focused API tests, `@persai/api` typecheck, and `helm template ... -f infra/helm/values-dev.yaml` passed for this cleanup slice, which is now closed in repo truth with Step 19 next.
- **ADR-072 Step 17 legacy schema/document cleanup:** repo-truth docs now track neutral `assistant_config` / `assistant_workspace` plus `assistant_config_document` / `assistant_workspace_document`, document `assistantConfig` / `assistantWorkspace` as bounded compatibility views beside authoritative `runtimeBundle`, note that active request-path runtime model override now reads `runtimeBundle`, and mark `Step 17` complete with `Step 18` next.
- **ADR-072 Step 16 active OpenClaw removal:** `apps/api` no longer ships the OpenClaw runtime adapter/facade/module wiring, adapter-only API env/config examples were removed, and the remaining active production seams now stay on PersAI-owned boundaries. Web/Telegram/media delivery use native runtime or object storage only, workspace memory now lives on the assistant memory registry, avatar upload/download now lives on PersAI media object storage, chat delete/reset/admin delete no longer call OpenClaw cleanup hooks, and legacy scheduled-action rows can only be cancelled instead of pretending pause/resume still work through a retired scheduler bridge. Focused `tsx` verification plus `@persai/api` typecheck were rerun for the Step 16 closeout.
- **ADR-072 Step 19 deploy/reapply scale-hardening requirement:** the ADR now treats post-deploy chat degradation and mandatory fleet-wide `reapply all` as an explicit `Step 19` blocker. `Slice 8`, the `Step 19` ledger note, and the detailed Step 19 migration notes now require routine deploy/restart recovery without global manual reapply, separation of published/materialized/warm states, and PersAI-owned self-healing bundle warm recovery instead of normal-ops mass reapply.
- **ADR-072 late-stage order realignment:** repo-truth planning docs now move sandbox off the primary production path. The main late-stage order is now active OpenClaw removal, legacy schema/document cleanup, UI/control-plane/runtime audit cleanup, `10000+` user scale hardening, and only then the isolated sandbox service. `Step 15a` is now explicitly deferred behind cleanup plus scale hardening, while `docs/API-BOUNDARY.md` and `docs/TEST-PLAN.md` now point future attach-by-ref/file-authority work at the deferred `Step 20` sandbox boundary.
- **ADR-072 Step 15b production Prompt Constructor landing:** admin Prompt Constructor is now a real production control plane instead of a renamed preset page. `apps/api` now compiles one structured `promptConstructor` bundle for ordinary turns and onboarding/recreate first-turns, setup preview consumes that compiled onboarding prompt instead of local hardcode, and `apps/runtime` now reads compiled system prompt output instead of rebuilding tool guidance in-place. Per-tool model descriptions and usage guidance are now admin-editable through `GET/PATCH /api/v1/admin/tools/metadata(:toolCode)`, feed runtime tool policy compilation, and drive native provider tool definition wording. Active lifecycle/API surfaces also moved off `openclawBootstrapDocument/openclawWorkspaceDocument` naming into neutral `assistantConfigDocument/assistantWorkspaceDocument`, while focused API/runtime tests cover compiler output, tool metadata admin flow, native tool projection, and compiled prompt runtime usage.
- **ADR-072 Step 15b production prompt-constructor baseline:** admin prompt editing now moves to neutral prompt-constructor ownership with API route cutover to `GET/PATCH /api/v1/admin/prompt-templates(:id)` (no dual-route mode), full template coverage including previously hidden `HEARTBEAT` and first-turn `BOOTSTRAP` sections, and runtime materialization now loading those sections from the same prompt-template source instead of hardcoded-only generation. Prompt-template reads now self-heal missing default rows on existing DBs and writes use upsert semantics for stable admin edits. Setup/settings EN/RU wording also aligns recreate semantics with explicit destructive scope (chats, memory, tasks, published versions, materialized runtime bundles/specs, media artifacts).
- **ADR-072 T15-7 closeout + sandbox boundary cleanup:** repo-truth docs now close `T15-7` and `Step 15` honestly after the already-landed quota/prompt/admin follow-through. The stray `Sandbox tool matrix` row was moved out of the Step 15 tool-slice ledger into the sandbox section, and `persai_workspace_attach` is now explicitly treated as migration-only truth whose future replacement is post-sandbox attach-by-ref follow-through on top of canonical `fileRef` authority rather than part of the sandbox tool matrix itself.
- **ADR-072 T15-7 quota truth cleanup:** the current native `quota_status` / plan-visibility contract now stays limited to the real PersAI-owned buckets (`token`, `active chats`, `media`, `knowledge`) instead of surfacing OpenClaw-backed `workspace_storage_bytes` as if it were part of Step 15 native quota truth. Admin Plans copy/tests/OpenAPI/generated contracts were cleaned up together so current operator/user/model-facing quota surfaces all speak the same honest vocabulary.
- **ADR-072 T15-7 admin quota visibility panel:** Admin Plans now uses the already-landed `AdminPlanVisibilityState` contract instead of keeping it dark. The page now shows the current workspace effective plan and all bucket-aware quota rows, with `workspace_storage_bytes` explicitly rendered as `limit only / usage unavailable`, and focused API coverage now asserts the expanded admin `usagePressure` plus `quotaBuckets` shape.
- **ADR-072 T15-7 full quota visibility landing:** `apps/api` now resolves one shared PersAI-owned quota snapshot for live token/chat/media/knowledge visibility plus an honest `workspace_storage_bytes` limit-only row until Step 16 metrics exist, `quota_status` now returns those buckets end to end through `packages/runtime-contract` and `apps/runtime`, and `packages/contracts` / `apps/web` now expose the same `quotaBuckets` vocabulary on user/admin visibility instead of leaving broader quota surfaces dark after the first tool-only landing.
- **ADR-072 T15-7 native `quota_status` landing:** `packages/runtime-contract`, `apps/runtime`, and `apps/api` now land the first executable `T15-7` follow-through after the docs-first contract cleanup. Native runtime now projects and executes the canonical system tool `quota_status` through the existing PersAI internal quota seam, bundle/tool-policy parity remaps current inventory `persai_tool_quota_status` onto that canonical runtime contract, model-facing prompt/admin runtime guidance now use the canonical name, and migration-only `persai_workspace_attach` is hidden from the Step 15 model surface instead of lingering as a raw path helper.
