- **ADR-072 T15-7 contract reconciliation:** repo-truth docs now open `T15-7` on a clean target contract before code follow-through begins. `docs/ADR/072-persai-native-multichannel-runtime-replacement.md`, `docs/API-BOUNDARY.md`, `docs/TEST-PLAN.md`, and `docs/SESSION-HANDOFF.md` now keep live quota inspection as a separate PersAI-native `quota_status` system tool instead of folding it into `knowledge_* source="subscription"`, and they treat current inventory `persai_workspace_attach` as migration-only truth rather than a steady-state raw path-based Step 15 helper, reserving future live file discovery plus attach-by-ref for post-sandbox follow-through on top of canonical `fileRef` authority.
- **ADR-072 T15-6b closeout status sync:** repo-truth docs now close `T15-6b` honestly after the landed follow-through pack. `docs/ADR/072-persai-native-multichannel-runtime-replacement.md`, `docs/SESSION-HANDOFF.md`, and `docs/TEST-PLAN.md` now treat storage/index/upload/list/delete/reindex, multi-namespace `knowledge_search` / `knowledge_fetch`, explicit `memory_write`, bounded richer hydration, plan-owned `runtime.contextHydration`, plan-driven compaction UX, and ranking polish as the completed `T15-6b` scope, and they point the next honest Step 15 follow-through at `T15-7`.
- **ADR-072 T15-6b ranking polish follow-through:** `read-assistant-knowledge.service.ts` now ranks document, memory, chat, preset, subscription, and global hits through a structured scorer with deterministic ordering, title/filename/locator boosts, better per-source weighting, length normalization, duplicate collapse, and stronger snippet extraction. The highest-value private namespaces (`document`, `memory`, `chat`) now also get a lightweight local hybrid rerank plus bounded diversification and relative recency blending, and focused API coverage plus `@persai/api` typecheck now cover the ranking refactor.
- **ADR-072 T15-6b plan-owned context policy baseline:** Admin Plans now expose a real `contextPolicy` surface that materializes into native `runtime.contextHydration`, so per-plan context behavior is no longer trapped in fixed heuristics. The runtime bundle now carries `preset`, token budget, compaction trigger, minimum recent-history floor, knowledge-hydration budget, and per-surface auto-compaction flags as server-owned truth, while focused API/runtime tests and generated contracts were updated so the control-plane UI, bundle materialization, and runtime validation stay aligned.
- **ADR-072 T15-6b plan-driven compaction UX follow-through:** web compaction UX no longer suggests compression from reply latency. Native turn completion now surfaces explicit `autoCompaction` token deltas, the web banner now reflects plan-driven context pressure and recent successful auto-compaction, and Telegram now sends a short post-reply notice only after real post-turn auto-compaction succeeds. OpenAPI/contracts, EN/RU copy, runtime/API/web tests, and the runtime-to-API result mapping were updated together so this new behavior is observable end to end.
- **ADR-072 T15-6b bounded richer hydration baseline:** ordinary native turns no longer rely only on the old fixed recent-message slice. `apps/runtime` now preserves a bounded cross-conversation durable-memory context alongside reusable shared-compaction summaries before trimming recent canonical history, so current prompt assembly keeps explicit human-memory continuity even when the blunt message cap would otherwise drop it. Focused runtime hydration tests and typechecks now cover the preserved prefix behavior on ordinary, capped, fallback, and compaction-reuse paths, while richer ranking/retrieval polish remains later `T15-6b` follow-through.
- **ADR-072 T15-6b preset/subscription/global knowledge baseline:** native runtime `knowledge_search` / `knowledge_fetch` now also work for `source="preset"`, `source="subscription"`, and `source="global"` so the unified knowledge plane now reaches assistant config/preset docs, the current effective subscription/plan state, and the first PersAI-global product corpus. `apps/api` now reads current materialized preset/runtime-bundle documents, bootstrap preset templates, effective subscription plus plan entitlement/tool-activation state, and platform-owned product/tool/plan documents through the same bounded reference-first search/fetch seam, while runtime bundle config/validation, tool projection, and focused API/runtime tests were updated together so these namespaces are real end to end. Richer ranking and context-hydration replacement remain the next `T15-6b` follow-through.
- **ADR-072 T15-6b prior-chat transcript read baseline:** native runtime `knowledge_search` / `knowledge_fetch` now also work for assistant-user-private `source="chat"` over canonical `AssistantChatMessage` rows, so prior-chat recall lands on the same unified private knowledge plane as uploaded documents and durable memory. `apps/api` now searches canonical chat messages by bounded references and returns bounded transcript windows around the selected message instead of replaying whole chats, while runtime bundle/config validation, tool projection, and focused API/runtime tests were updated together so the new namespace is real end to end. Shared/preset/subscription knowledge, PersAI-global knowledge, richer ranking, and context-hydration replacement remain later `T15-6b` follow-through.
- **ADR-072 T15-6b explicit `memory_write` + private memory read baseline:** native runtime now projects an always-on bounded `memory_write` tool so the model can explicitly persist one durable fact, preference, or open loop through a real PersAI-owned validator/audit path instead of hidden answer-side effects. `apps/api` now exposes an internal runtime memory-write seam backed by the assistant memory registry with policy enforcement, audit events, and the new `memory_write` source type, and `knowledge_search` / `knowledge_fetch` now also work for the first assistant-user-private `source="memory"` backend over active memory-registry rows. Focused API/runtime tests and typechecks cover the new write/read seams end to end, while prior-chat retrieval and broader shared/global namespaces remain the next `T15-6b` follow-through.
- **ADR-072 T15-6b document retrieval + delete follow-through:** the next honest `T15-6b` slice is now landed on top of the knowledge-source storage baseline. Assistant knowledge-source management now includes public `delete` alongside `upload` / `list` / detail-status / `reindex`, releasing reserved knowledge quota and deleting the stored object on removal. Native runtime `knowledge_search` / `knowledge_fetch` are now real for the first `document` source over indexed uploaded assistant knowledge through PersAI internal API search/fetch seams, returning lightweight references and bounded excerpt windows instead of raw file reads. Shared/global namespaces, prior-chat retrieval, and explicit durable `memory_write` still remain later follow-through.
- **ADR-072 T15-6b knowledge-source storage/index baseline:** `apps/api` now has the first honest PersAI-owned knowledge-source surface for Step 15. Assistant-scoped uploaded workspace knowledge now persists in dedicated knowledge object-storage paths with separate knowledge-storage quota/accounting, Prisma models/migration for source and chunk rows, and public `upload`, `list`, per-source status/detail, and `reindex` endpoints plus generated contracts. Reset assistant and admin-delete-user now also purge knowledge-source rows/files and release knowledge quota, while focused API tests cover quota accounting, upload/list/get/reindex behavior, and cleanup semantics. The broader `T15-6b` slice remains in progress: user-visible delete, `knowledge_search` / `knowledge_fetch`, private prior-chat indexing, shared/global namespaces, and explicit durable `memory_write` flows are still follow-through.
- **ADR-072 `T15-6` closeout:** the Step 15 media slice is now honestly closed on one shared PersAI-native media boundary. `image_generate`, `image_edit`, `tts`, and `video_generate` all run end to end through native runtime -> provider-gateway -> object storage -> channel delivery, web chat keeps one stronger live status instead of appending a badge chain, Telegram maps media tools onto real Bot API chat actions, long-running media turns derive their timeout from worker policy instead of the old fixed 90-second cap, prompt-plus-reference-image `video_generate` now works through provider-side reference-image normalization, and Admin Plans now expose the bounded per-plan `videoGenerateModelKey` selector (`sora-2` / `sora-2-pro`) that materializes into the server-owned runtime bundle seam `toolCredentialRefs.video_generate.modelKey`.
- **ADR-072 media status UX follow-through:** web chat no longer stacks a portyanka of tool/runtime status badges during one assistant reply. `apps/web` now keeps one stronger live status per assistant message and leaves only the last relevant status at the end of the turn, while `apps/api` moves native Telegram turns onto the runtime stream path so `sendChatAction` heartbeats can follow real `tool_started` / `tool_finished` events. Telegram now maps `tts` to voice recording, `video_generate` to video recording, image tools to photo upload, and switches to the final outbound upload action before media delivery.
- **ADR-072 T15-6 native `video_generate` baseline:** `video_generate` is now the fourth landed media worker tool inside Step 15 and reuses the same native worker/provider-gateway/object-storage/media-delivery path as the earlier media tools. `packages/runtime-contract` now defines the typed video request/result contracts, `apps/api` now materializes `video_generate` as a first-class plan-managed worker tool that reuses the shared `tool_image_generate` credential seam, `apps/provider-gateway` now exposes `generate-video` with a bounded OpenAI `sora-2` create/poll/download loop, and `apps/runtime` now projects/executes `video_generate` for both prompt-only and prompt-plus-current-turn-reference-image flows with quota gating plus persisted video artifacts. Focused API/provider/runtime tests and repo-truth docs now cover the landed video path.
- **ADR-072 T15-6 native `image_edit` source/reference refinement:** `image_edit` now stays honest on live user flows: `apps/runtime` projects it only for explicit edit intent, current-turn image hydration now exposes numbered `image #1`, `image #2`, and so on for model clarity, the native request contract now carries `sourceImageIndex` plus optional `referenceImageIndex`, common two-image prompts such as "like the second photo" / "как на втором фото" now conservatively resolve to `image #1` as the edited source plus `image #2` as the visual reference when the rest of the request is clear, and the OpenAI provider prompt now explicitly tells the model to edit only the source image while treating the second image as a reference for style/appearance/environment cues. Focused provider/runtime tests and repo-truth docs were refreshed, while `video_generate` remains the next `T15-6` follow-through.
- **ADR-072 T15-6 native `tts` baseline:** `tts` is now the second landed media worker tool inside Step 15. Admin Tool Credentials now carry provider-specific TTS secrets plus a primary-provider selector, assistant draft/publish state now carries an assistant-scoped `voiceProfile`, `apps/provider-gateway` now exposes `generate-speech` with `ElevenLabs` / `Yandex SpeechKit` / `OpenAI` adapters over PersAI-resolved secrets, and `apps/runtime` now projects/executes native `tts` with tone steering, provider fallback, and persisted audio `RuntimeOutputArtifact`s. Focused provider/runtime tests and typechecks now cover the speech seam while `image_edit` and `video_generate` remain later `T15-6` follow-through.
- **ADR-072 T15-6 native `image_generate` baseline:** `image_generate` is now the first landed media worker tool in Step 15. `packages/runtime-contract` defines the native request/result contract plus provider-gateway `generate-image` seam, `apps/provider-gateway` executes OpenAI `gpt-image-1` through PersAI-resolved tool secrets, `apps/runtime` projects and executes the tool with quota/credential gating and persists generated images to PersAI object storage as `RuntimeOutputArtifact`s, and `apps/api` now maps native runtime artifacts through send/stream/Telegram/media-delivery paths instead of failing when runtime returns media. This opens `T15-6` on the smallest honest baseline while `tts`, `image_edit`, and `video_generate` remain follow-through inside the slice and `T15-6b` stays separate.
- **ADR-072 T15-5 closeout + assistant follow-up hardening:** bounded live validation plus the post-validation retry/prompt hardening now close `T15-5 — Reminder and scheduled action plan tools` honestly. Hidden assistant-side scheduled actions now fork a fresh retry idempotency key after failed native turns instead of replaying a doomed failed receipt forever, the hidden scheduled-action prompt now explicitly teaches `check -> decide -> create immediate audience="user" follow-up only when the condition is met`, and repo-truth docs now move the next active Step 15 family to `T15-6 — Media generation and editing plan tools`.
- **ADR-072 T15-5 scheduled_action hard rename + assistant background actions:** the product-facing reminder tool is now canonically `scheduled_action` with no compatibility alias. `apps/runtime` now tells the model about explicit `audience="user" | "assistant"` semantics, humane delayed follow-up usage, and the rule that assistant-side background actions cannot directly push the user; `apps/api` now persists `audience`, `actionType`, and `actionPayload` on task rows, routes hidden assistant actions through a private native runtime turn instead of user-visible chat delivery, and keeps ordinary reminder delivery on the shared user-facing path. The settings UI now shows assistant-side scheduled actions in a separate subdued panel so background work stays visible without cluttering the main reminder list.
- **ADR-072 T15-5 native reminder scheduler cutover:** new reminders no longer create hidden legacy cron jobs under the hood. `apps/api` now persists reminder schedule/payload state directly on PersAI task rows, captures bounded reminder context snapshots at create time, and runs due reminders through a PersAI-owned scheduler loop with a global rollout-resettable scheduler epoch, expiring claims, and retry delay before finalizing delivery through the shared reminder delivery core. This makes the active reminder/task UI path pre-prod ready for live validation on native due-time pickup while keeping legacy `cron-fire` compatibility only for older callback rows during rollout.
- **ADR-072 T15-5 reminder delivery-core extraction:** `POST /api/v1/internal/cron-fire` is no longer the only place where reminder fanout semantics live. `apps/api` now has a shared PersAI-owned reminder delivery service that handles summary cleanup, inbound capability/quota fallback rendering, Telegram-vs-web routing, and web fallback delivery, while `HandleInternalCronFireService` is reduced to a legacy trigger adapter for replay safety plus task-registry sync. This makes the current reminder/task UI path code-ready for bounded live validation without re-exposing raw `cron` semantics, while hidden internal `cron` still remains the temporary due-time trigger source.
- **ADR-072 T15-5 native reminder executor seam:** `apps/runtime` now projects and executes the product-facing `scheduled_action` surface (`create`, `list`, `pause`, `resume`, `cancel`) as a real native worker tool instead of leaving the tool dark after bundle materialization. The native reminder path reuses PersAI internal `/api/v1/internal/runtime/tasks/items` and `/control` seams, tool history now returns structured reminder results, and the API reminder control service accepts clean native `conversationContext` for Telegram target resolution while hidden internal `cron` and the legacy due-time callback path remain internal-only follow-through.
- **ADR-072 T15-5 reminder worker-contract baseline:** native tool materialization now classifies `scheduled_action` as a `worker` plan tool and includes it in `runtime.workerTools` as the `scheduled_action` family with explicit state-mutation, timeout, confirmation, and failure metadata. This opens `T15-5` on the shared worker contract without yet claiming a finished native reminder executor or PersAI-owned due-time pickup, and hidden internal `cron` stays internal-only.
- **ADR-072 native web stream tool sequencing hardening:** native tool-capable web streaming now keeps user-visible text and tool lifecycle in honest order. `apps/runtime` separates assembled assistant text from delivered stream text so buffered pre-tool prefixes recovered from provider `tool_calls.result.text` are flushed as real `text_delta` events before `tool_started`, and the web delivery path now flushes pending buffered text before tool/compaction/runtime activity markers so already-produced assistant text is not visually delayed behind `summarize_context` / `compact_context` lifecycle events.
- **ADR-072 T15-4 native browser executor closeout:** `browser` is now a real PersAI-native tool path instead of a dark contract placeholder. `apps/provider-gateway` now owns `POST /api/v1/providers/browser-action` backed by Browserless `/function`, `apps/runtime` now projects and executes `browser` when worker policy + credential + supported provider agree, and the bounded native browser contract is now the honest `snapshot | act` surface with quota/provider gating, timeout propagation, and structured page snapshot/tool-history results.
- **ADR-072 T15-4 browser credential + contract baseline:** PersAI now has a real `browser` control-plane-to-bundle seam instead of a dead UI gap. Admin Tool Credentials now includes `tool_browser` for the hidden `Browserless` backend, `browser` now requires that credential in the catalog, materialization carries the configured Browserless reference into `toolCredentialRefs.browser`, and the native runtime bundle now also carries typed `runtime.browser` provider/action/confirmation metadata with warm validation. `browser` still stays worker-only and dark on the active model-visible path until a real dispatch/executor slice lands, but the Browserless key path is now real and future browser/media worker slices build on one honest baseline.
- **ADR-072 T15-4 shared worker-tool contract baseline:** the native runtime bundle now carries a typed `runtime.workerTools` block for the current worker-policy surface (`browser`, `image_generate`, `tts`, hidden internal `cron`) instead of leaving each future worker family to invent its own async metadata. `MaterializeAssistantPublishedVersionService` now derives explicit worker family/outcome/timeout/confirmation/provider-routing/failure metadata from the current worker `toolPolicies`, and `RuntimeBundleRegistryService` now rejects warmed bundles that omit current worker-policy coverage or map `runtime.workerTools` entries onto non-worker tools. This opens `T15-4` honestly as a shared worker baseline while real browser dispatch/executor work remains later follow-through.
- **ADR-072 T15-3b native web-tool closeout:** bounded live validation on the freshly applied native path now confirms `T15-3b` end-to-end. `web_search` succeeds on the live native executor path across the new runtime/provider-gateway/internal-API seam, and `web_fetch` also becomes model-visible and executes once its separate Firecrawl credential is configured and reapplied. This closes the Step 15 web-retrieval slice honestly and moves the next active tool family to `T15-4 — Browser and web-interaction plan tools`.
- **ADR-072 native web-tool internal API wiring fix:** Helm source-of-truth now injects `PERSAI_API_BASE_URL` and `PERSAI_INTERNAL_API_TOKEN` into both `runtime` and `provider-gateway`, so the native `web_search` / `web_fetch` path can actually consume tool daily limits and resolve assistant-scoped tool secrets on live deployments instead of failing closed with `PersAI internal API base URL is not configured.` The missing wiring only surfaced once Step 15 tools started using the new native quota/secret seam.
- **ADR-072 shared compaction structured-output reliability follow-through:** native shared compaction now caps provider output with a bounded `maxOutputTokens` budget and retries exactly once when the returned durable summary fails structured validation. `compact_context` / `summarize_context` still fail closed for poisoned output, but sporadic provider-side JSON/schema misses no longer force an immediate permanent skip on the first bad attempt.
- **ADR-072 T15-6b human memory and namespaced knowledge planning:** ADR-072 now inserts an explicit `T15-6b — Human memory and namespaced knowledge sources` slice after `T15-6` and before `T15-7`. The plan now cleanly separates session memory, cross-session human memory, PersAI-managed knowledge sources, and Step 16 sandbox access; future `knowledge_search` / `knowledge_fetch` are now tied to that slice instead of a vague deferred branch, workspace/sandbox files are only authoring/ingest inputs rather than the runtime source of truth, and durable human-memory writes are explicitly planned as bounded tool/validator flows instead of hidden side effects of ordinary assistant text.
- **ADR-072 T15-3b native `web_search` provider-selection parity:** native `web_search` now honors the full current admin/control-plane provider surface instead of a `Tavily`-only subset. `apps/provider-gateway` routes `POST /api/v1/providers/web-search` through `Tavily`, `Brave`, `Perplexity`, and `Google (Gemini)` with PersAI internal secret resolution plus normalized untrusted-result metadata, and `apps/runtime` now projects/executes `web_search` for every currently supported bundle `providerId` (`null -> tavily`, `brave`, `perplexity`, `google`) while preserving daily-limit enforcement plus explicit unsupported-provider skips. Focused provider/runtime tests now cover multi-provider routing, non-default provider projection/execution, quota-denied behavior, and unsupported-provider guards, so the slice is ready for bounded live validation after `reapply`.
- **ADR-072 T15-3b native `web_fetch` baseline:** `apps/provider-gateway` now exposes `POST /api/v1/providers/web-fetch` backed by Firecrawl with PersAI internal secret resolution plus normalized external-content/untrusted-source metadata. `apps/runtime` now projects and executes `web_fetch` as a separate first-class tool when inline policy + credentials allow it, consumes the tool daily limit through the internal API before the provider call, and returns structured fetched/skipped tool results inside the existing sync/stream tool loop. `web_fetch` now shares the active `T15-3b` surface with native `web_search`, while bounded live validation of the combined native web-tool path remains the next honest follow-through.
- **ADR-072 T15-3a shared runtime hardening:** the shared PersAI-native tool runtime now has honest tool-aware sync and stream behavior. `apps/provider-gateway` streams OpenAI/Anthropic `tool_calls`, `apps/runtime` runs a real bounded stream tool loop with lease-safe compaction execution plus `tool_started` / `tool_finished` events, and the API/web stream path forwards that lifecycle without disabling model-visible tools on stream turns. `knowledge_search`, `knowledge_fetch`, `persai_workspace_attach`, and `persai_tool_quota_status` still remain gated off the ordinary model-visible path until real PersAI-native executors exist, so `T15-3a` closes cleanly while later helper exposure/admin follow-through moves to `T15-7`.
- **ADR-072 Step 15 web-tool correction:** ADR-072 now makes `web_search` and `web_fetch` explicit first-class Step 15 plan tools with separate PersAI-native executors and provider/API seams instead of treating them as part of a `knowledge_*` layer. `T15-3b` now means `Web search and fetch plan tools`, while `knowledge_search` / `knowledge_fetch` remain in ADR-072 as the deferred future knowledge layer that stays disconnected until a real PersAI-native knowledge backend exists. The master Cursor guidance now explicitly forbids hiding `web_search` / `web_fetch` behind `knowledge_*`.
- **ADR-072 T15-3 tool transport baseline:** the native runtime/provider boundary is no longer text-only for Step 15 tools. `packages/runtime-contract` now carries machine-readable tool definitions/choice/history/call/result contracts, `apps/runtime` projects `summarize_context`, `compact_context`, `knowledge_search`, and `knowledge_fetch` from bundle truth (`toolPolicies`, `runtime.sharedCompaction`, `runtime.knowledgeAccess`) into a bounded synchronous tool loop, shared compaction now returns structured post-tool state that later reasoning can reuse, and `apps/provider-gateway` now validates/maps OpenAI + Anthropic tool-aware sync calls. Knowledge execution remains explicitly truthful but partial for now: unimplemented native sources return structured skipped/source-unavailable results, `browser` stays separate, and sandbox stays out of scope.
- **ADR-072 T15-3 knowledge access contract baseline:** the native runtime contract/bundle now carry a typed `runtime.knowledgeAccess` block with canonical `knowledge_search` / `knowledge_fetch` tool names, explicit `inline|worker` execution modes, `ragMode: "pattern_only"`, and the preserved current `web_search` / `web_fetch` / `memory_search` / `memory_get` alias + credential mapping. `MaterializeAssistantPublishedVersionService` now emits that block, `RuntimeBundleRegistryService` warm validation rejects knowledge-layer drift from the preserved tool-policy surface, and focused API/runtime tests plus typechecks close the first contract-only `T15-3` landing while executor/user-path wiring stays later work.
- **ADR-072 T15-2 rollout closeout:** dev rollout and live validation now close `T15-2` honestly. Web manual compaction/state/banner and Telegram shared auto summarize are running on native runtime truth after `reapply`, and the suspected "double OpenAI request" on Telegram was traced to the internal shared-compaction summarize call from the previously applied bundle rather than a duplicate inbound turn.
- **ADR-072 T15-2 shared compaction completion:** native runtime turn execution now reuses the shared compaction service for Telegram owner auto summarize, later native turns now hydrate from the latest durable `runtime_session_compactions` summary instead of replaying already-compacted history, and the public web compaction banner now also suggests compression when rolling reply latency crosses the shared `7000ms` threshold. `T15-2` is now complete; the next Step 15 tool slice is `T15-3`.
- **ADR-072 T15-3 unified knowledge layer planning:** ADR-072 now fixes the clean target for search/RAG/memory retrieval as one knowledge-access layer instead of several duplicated tools. The target contract is `knowledge_search` + `knowledge_fetch`; `RAG` is explicitly a usage pattern rather than a separate tool, `memory_search` / `memory_get` map to `source=memory`, `web_search` / `web_fetch` map to `source=web`, and `browser` stays separate.
- **ADR-072 T15-2 native web compaction state cutover:** public `GET /api/v1/assistant/chats/web/:chatId/compaction` now reads native runtime session truth through new internal `POST /api/v1/turns/session/resolve`, so web compaction state/banner reads no longer depend on the old OpenClaw web session-state API. The old API-side OpenClaw-only web compaction/session-state methods were removed; Telegram/auto callers and durable summary reuse remain later `T15-2` follow-up.
- **ADR-072 T15-2 native web manual compaction cutover:** public `POST /api/v1/assistant/chats/web/:chatId/compact` now calls native runtime `POST /api/v1/turns/compact` through new `CompactNativeWebChatSessionService`, preserves the existing assistant API response shape plus `compaction_unavailable` conflict behavior, and no longer depends on the old OpenClaw-only web compaction API. `GET /api/v1/assistant/chats/web/:chatId/compaction`, banner-state reads, Telegram auto summarize, and durable summary reuse remain later `T15-2` follow-up.
- **ADR-072 T15-2 dark native compaction seam:** `apps/runtime` now exposes internal `POST /api/v1/turns/compact` for the first provider-backed shared compaction path. It resolves the active session plus warmed bundle from runtime-owned state, hydrates older canonical web/Telegram history, appends `runtime_session_compactions`, and bumps session compaction counters, while the live web/Telegram user paths remain on their existing seams until a later T15-2 cutover.
- **ADR-072 T15-2 shared compaction contract baseline:** the native runtime bundle now carries a typed `runtime.sharedCompaction` block that fixes the shared system-tool names (`summarize_context`, `compact_context`), projects the current web compaction threshold knobs from admin runtime policy, carries the shared web latency suggestion threshold (`7000ms`), and includes the assistant-scoped Telegram `autoCompactionEnabled` flag. `MaterializeAssistantPublishedVersionService` now derives that block during materialization, `RuntimeBundleRegistryService` validates it on warm, and ADR-072 now marks `T15-2` as in progress with the contract baseline landed before executor wiring.
- **ADR-072 native prompt/lifecycle UI planning:** ADR-072 now treats admin/setup UX as part of the target architecture instead of a cleanup tail. The target architecture now requires PersAI-native prompt/lifecycle surfaces, adds a dedicated `Step 15b` to replace `Bootstrap Document Presets` with native prompt editing, and makes `create`, `setup preview`, `publish`, `reapply`, `reset`, and `recreate` flow through one shared native bundle/prompt-template pipeline before final OpenClaw removal.
- **ADR-072 T15-1 native tool policy baseline:** the native runtime bundle now carries explicit `toolPolicies` metadata for every current tool with `system|plan|internal` kind, `allowed|forbidden` usage, and `inline|worker|sandbox` execution mode. `MaterializeAssistantPublishedVersionService` now renders `TOOLS.md` from that same policy list, and `RuntimeBundleRegistryService` rejects warmed bundles whose `toolAvailability` names tools without matching explicit policy metadata. ADR-072 now marks `T15-1` complete and points Step 15 to `T15-2` next.
- **ADR-072 Step 15 current-tool baseline:** ADR-072 now starts Step 15 with `T15-0 — Current tool inventory baseline` so future sessions must preserve the real existing PersAI tool surface before redesigning execution. The ADR now names the current catalog/UI/runtime truth (`web_search`, `web_fetch`, `image_generate`, `tts`, `browser`, `memory_search`, `memory_get`, `reminder_task`, `persai_workspace_attach`, `persai_tool_quota_status`, hidden `cron`), references the concrete source files for tool credentials, reminder/cron bridge behavior, and runtime `TOOLS.md` projection, and adds an explicit current-to-Step-15 parity map so later slices cannot silently drop or rename today's tool surface. The Step 15 ledger now marks `T15-0` complete and preserves the bounded baseline that later tool-policy and executor slices build on.
- **ADR-072 Step 15 tool slice planning:** ADR-072 now explicitly splits Step 15 into tool slices so future sessions do not treat “all tools” as one giant milestone. The plan now distinguishes `system tools`, `plan tools`, and `sandbox tools`, makes tool-usage policy explicit for model/runtime behavior, keeps shared summarization/compaction as a first-class system capability, preserves Telegram `auto summarize`, keeps the web compaction banner trigger when rolling latency crosses `7s`, and treats search/RAG plus media generation/editing as separate tool tracks. Sandbox/file/process tools remain deferred to Step 16.
- **ADR-072 Step 14 Telegram native text/group cutover:** `HandleInternalTelegramTurnService` now sends Telegram direct/group turns straight to native `apps/runtime` execution with proper `RuntimeConversationAddress` identity and shared canonical-history hydration. The remaining Telegram-only `/compact` and compaction-hint seam was removed instead of being carried into the target architecture; shared compaction/tooling is explicitly deferred to Step 15. Live dev Telegram validation now closes Step 14, and the repo also prepares a dev-only peer abuse-threshold tune plus explicit abuse-guard logging to reduce false-positive Telegram rate-limit replies during rapid chat testing.
- **ADR-072 Step 13 Telegram adapter closeout:** public `/telegram-webhook/:assistantId` traffic no longer acts as a tier-aware reverse proxy into OpenClaw. `apps/api` now verifies the assistant-scoped Telegram webhook secret, parses Telegram message/member updates, enforces owner-only and group mention/reply semantics, syncs Telegram groups/chat targets locally, downloads inbound files directly from the Telegram Bot API, persists canonical Telegram user/assistant messages and attachments in PersAI, and sends outbound text/media via the Telegram Bot API. The old internal Telegram ingress/controller path and internal Telegram group/chat-target callback endpoints were removed once the API-side adapter took ownership. The remaining follow-up moves to Step 14: replacing the legacy execution seam inside `HandleInternalTelegramTurnService` with native runtime turns.
- **ADR-072 Step 15a native web TTS planning:** ADR-072 now carries an explicit planned sub-step for native web TTS streaming/output. The plan now fixes that live web voice output must be delivered as a channel output capability on the native web path, not treated as a post-turn attachment-only fallback.
- **ADR-072 Step 12 native STT cutover:** `apps/api` voice/media transcription now streams multipart audio to `apps/runtime`, `apps/runtime` forwards that audio to `apps/provider-gateway`, and `apps/provider-gateway` executes OpenAI `gpt-4o-mini-transcribe` directly. The OpenClaw request-time STT seam is removed, and the neutral runtime facade drops the dead upload/delete/transcribe media tails that are no longer used after the PersAI-owned attachment cutover.
- **ADR-072 Step 11 attachment staging closeout:** Step 11 now closes with PersAI-owned attachment lifecycle, rollback-safe staged uploads, current-turn image/PDF provider input under an explicit request-size budget, and extraction-first canonical handling for non-PDF document formats so native chat no longer replays binary history payloads on later turns.
- **ADR-072 Step 11 current-turn multimodal attachments:** `apps/runtime` now downloads current inbound image attachments from PersAI object storage and sends them to OpenAI/Anthropic as real image input blocks, while `apps/api` expands canonical document extraction to `json`, `pdf`, `txt/md/csv`, `doc/docx`, and `xls/xlsx` so native web turns can use real attachment content instead of filename/mime-only metadata on the hot path.
- **ADR-072 Step 11 staged-upload rollback hardening:** failed web staged uploads now roll back their transient empty staging message, merge cleanup can delete legacy orphan placeholder rows left by older failures, and `apps/runtime` now skips attachment-less empty placeholders during native history hydration so one failed attachment attempt no longer poisons later turns in the same web chat.
- **ADR-072 Step 11 native attachment hydration follow-through:** native web sync/stream turns now pass raw user text plus attachment refs while `apps/runtime` hydrates current and historical attachment summaries from canonical `assistant_chat_message_attachments` rows. Direct web uploads and staged uploads now persist usable preview/transcription metadata in canonical attachment records, so native attachment context no longer depends on API-only prompt enrichment for the native path while the temporary Step 10 `legacy|shadow|native` seam still exists.
- **ADR-072 Step 11 PersAI-owned attachment staging cutover:** active web/inbound attachment binaries now persist in PersAI-owned object storage instead of the OpenClaw workspace media endpoints. `ManageChatMediaService`, `InboundMediaService`, and `MediaDeliveryService` now write attachment copies through a dedicated PersAI media storage seam; hard-delete/reset/admin-delete now clean up PersAI media objects; and native web turn requests now carry object-key attachment refs while the current attachment semantics remain API-enriched text plus bounded temporary source seams for STT and legacy runtime-owned tool artifacts.
- **ADR-072 Step 10 web cutover closeout:** repository truth now records Step 10 as complete after the bounded `shadow` window, recent canonical web history hydration, the OpenAI assistant-history serialization fix, the dev-mode switch to `native`, and one successful post-cutover live validation pass on the ordinary web chat path. The next migration work moves to Step 11 attachment staging, while the temporary `legacy|shadow|native` route modes remain only as cleanup/fallback seams.
- **ADR-072 Step 10 dev native web cutover config:** `infra/helm/values-dev.yaml` now sets both `PERSAI_WEB_CHAT_SYNC_RUNTIME_MODE` and `PERSAI_WEB_CHAT_STREAM_RUNTIME_MODE` to `native`. The bounded `shadow` window already proved recent canonical history hydration and OpenAI assistant-history serialization are healthy enough for semantic parity, so dev now moves the ordinary web chat path onto PersAI native runtime without per-request fallback back to OpenClaw.
- **ADR-072 Step 10 OpenAI assistant-history stream fix:** `apps/provider-gateway` no longer serializes every OpenAI Responses message as an `input_text` content block. The gateway now sends the current text-only history as plain string message content, which keeps recent assistant history valid on the OpenAI stream path and fixes the false `runtime_unreachable` shadow failures caused by provider-side `400 Invalid value: 'input_text'` errors after native history hydration landed.
- **ADR-072 Step 10 native web chat history hydration:** `apps/runtime` now assembles provider `messages[]` for web turns from recent canonical `assistant_chats` / `assistant_chat_messages` context instead of sending only the newest inbound message. The current inbound user turn still uses the API-enriched text payload, system chat markers are skipped, and the same hydration path now applies to both native `createTurn` and `streamTurn` so Step 10 shadow/native parity is no longer blocked by an obviously context-free runtime request shape.
- **ADR-072 Step 10 dev shadow window config:** `infra/helm/values-dev.yaml` now sets both `PERSAI_WEB_CHAT_SYNC_RUNTIME_MODE` and `PERSAI_WEB_CHAT_STREAM_RUNTIME_MODE` to `shadow` so the next honest dev rollout keeps OpenClaw as the user-visible primary path while capturing native parity evidence through `web_runtime_shadow_compare`, `web_runtime_route`, and Admin Overview `webRuntimeShadowComparisons`. This is intentionally temporary rollout truth for one bounded validation window, not the final cutover state.
- **ADR-072 Step 10 shadow comparison admin overview read model:** `WebRuntimeShadowComparisonService` now keeps a bounded pod-local in-memory sample list alongside `web_runtime_shadow_compare` logs, `GET /api/v1/admin/overview/dashboard` returns `webRuntimeShadowComparisons`, and `/admin` renders recent sync/stream parity samples so the next bounded dev `shadow` window can be inspected without a separate prep deploy or log-only spelunking.
- **ADR-072 Step 10 web route modes + shadow comparison seam:** replaced the Step 9 boolean web cutover flags with explicit sync/stream runtime modes: `PERSAI_WEB_CHAT_SYNC_RUNTIME_MODE` and `PERSAI_WEB_CHAT_STREAM_RUNTIME_MODE`, each with `legacy|shadow|native`. `shadow` keeps OpenClaw as the user-visible primary path while `apps/api` queues one native comparison run and logs `web_runtime_shadow_compare`; `native` preserves the Step 9 no-fallback rule and `web_runtime_route` observability. Base Helm values now default both web routes to `legacy`, while dev preserves the already-validated native behavior with `native`.
- **ADR-072 Step 9 bounded live native stream smoke:** dev now also runs the flagged native stream path with `PERSAI_NATIVE_RUNTIME_WEB_STREAM_ENABLED=true`, and a bounded authenticated smoke of `POST /api/v1/assistant/chat/web/stream` returned `started`, multiple `delta`, `runtime_done`, and `completed` with final assistant content exactly `native stream smoke ok`. Replay with the same `clientTurnId` returned the same `chatId` and `assistantMessageId` without duplicate persistence, and a bounded abort after the first `delta` preserved partial assistant output plus the expected interruption system marker. This closes the last Step 9 live-validation gap and moves the next work to Step 10 web shadow/cutover.
- **ADR-072 Step 9 API stream native cutover flag:** `apps/provider-gateway` now exposes `POST /api/v1/providers/stream-text`, `apps/runtime` now exposes `POST /api/v1/turns/stream`, and `apps/api` can route `POST /api/v1/assistant/chat/web/stream` to the native runtime when `PERSAI_NATIVE_RUNTIME_WEB_STREAM_ENABLED=true`. The API stream boundary keeps canonical replay/message persistence, SSE event ownership, and quota/media handling, skips legacy bootstrap consumption on native success, aborts runtime fetches when the client disconnects, and fails honestly instead of silently falling back to OpenClaw when the stream flag is enabled.
- **ADR-072 Step 9 dev GitOps rollout + bounded live sync smoke:** the normal `main -> CI -> Dev Image Publish -> Argo CD` path now deploys the current Step 9 baseline for `apps/api`, `apps/runtime`, and `apps/provider-gateway` together on dev GKE. Dev is running the native sync cutover env (`PERSAI_NATIVE_RUNTIME_WEB_SYNC_ENABLED=true`, `PERSAI_RUNTIME_BASE_URL=http://runtime:3012`, `PERSAI_PROVIDER_GATEWAY_BASE_URL=http://provider-gateway:3011`), bounded authenticated live validation of `POST /api/v1/assistant/chat/web` returned `native sync smoke ok`, `assistant/runtime/preflight` returned `live: true, ready: true`, and replay with the same `clientTurnId` returned the same chat/message ids without duplicating persisted chat history. This validates the flagged native sync web path on real dev infrastructure while `POST /api/v1/assistant/chat/web/stream` and the default web UX cutover remain later Step 9 work.
- **ADR-072 Step 9 API sync native cutover flag:** `apps/api` now has a dedicated `SendNativeWebChatTurnService`, and `POST /api/v1/assistant/chat/web` can route sync web turns to the native `apps/runtime` `POST /api/v1/turns/create` seam when `PERSAI_NATIVE_RUNTIME_WEB_SYNC_ENABLED=true`. The API path keeps canonical replay/message persistence and quota/accounting ownership, skips legacy bootstrap consumption on native success, and fails honestly instead of silently falling back to OpenClaw when the flag is enabled. `RuntimeTurnRequest` / `TurnExecutionService` also now carry optional `providerOverride` / `modelOverride` so quota-degraded sync turns preserve current semantics on the native path.
- **ADR-072 Step 9 dark sync createTurn seam:** `apps/provider-gateway` now exposes `POST /api/v1/providers/generate-text` over warmed OpenAI/Anthropic clients, `apps/runtime` now exposes text-only dark `POST /api/v1/turns/create` through `TurnExecutionService`, and runtime readiness/metrics now depend on real provider-gateway readiness through `RUNTIME_PROVIDER_GATEWAY_BASE_URL` / `RUNTIME_PROVIDER_GATEWAY_TIMEOUT_MS`. This starts Step 9 by consuming the Step 8 session-state package without cutting live web traffic over yet; `streamTurn`, attachment handling, API-side web routing, and removal of the temporary Step 7 API `unset => skip` seams remain later Step 9 work.
- **ADR-072 Step 8 in-flight accepted-turn claim seam:** `apps/runtime` now uses a bounded Redis in-flight accepted-turn marker to narrow the last Step 8 pre-receipt race. `RuntimeStateRedisService` atomically checks for an existing in-flight marker and acquires the session lease together, `SessionLeaseService` now exposes `claimLeaseForAcceptedTurn(...)` plus marker cleanup, and `TurnAcceptanceService` now returns explicit `in_flight` instead of collapsing same-idempotency retries into generic `busy` during the lease-acquired / receipt-not-yet-persisted window. This closes the remaining Step 8 internal replay-ordering gap without adding any HTTP surface or request-time execution path.
- **ADR-072 Step 8 lease heartbeat seam:** `apps/runtime` now has the first bounded lease-renewal path for long-running accepted turns. `RuntimeStateRedisService` can atomically compare-and-renew a session lease TTL, `SessionLeaseService` now exposes `renewLease(...)`, and `TurnLeaseHeartbeatService` gives the turn lifecycle an explicit `renewed` vs `lost` heartbeat result without adding any HTTP surface. This keeps lease ownership explicit inside Step 8 so upcoming native streaming work does not have to rely only on passive TTL expiry.
- **ADR-072 Step 8 turn finalization seam:** `apps/runtime` now has `TurnFinalizationService` as the paired internal Step 8 seam for terminal turn state. It marks `runtime_turn_receipts` as `completed` / `interrupted` / `failed`, updates `runtime_sessions` summary fields, and releases the held Redis session lease in one bounded runtime-owned contract. The ordering is explicit: terminal receipt is persisted first, session summary update happens next, and the lease is released only after terminal receipt persistence, so replay safety stays primary while Step 8 still remains fully internal and dark.
- **ADR-072 Step 8 turn acceptance orchestration seam:** `apps/runtime` now has a first internal `TurnAcceptanceService` that composes `SessionStoreService`, `SessionLeaseService`, and `IdempotencyService` for one bounded native-turn acceptance lifecycle. The ordering is now explicit and cleaner for the final architecture: resolve/ensure session, check replay, acquire the session lease, then create the accepted turn receipt. This keeps Step 8 inside the runtime boundary without adding any web/Telegram HTTP surface yet, and avoids leaving a stray accepted receipt behind when the session is already busy.
- **ADR-072 Step 8 session resolve/lease/idempotency boundary:** `apps/runtime` now has the first runtime-owned session-state service layer over the Step 6 Postgres/Redis foundation. `SessionStoreService` resolves and ensures `runtime_sessions` while treating Redis conversation-session pointers as best-effort hot-path hints, `SessionLeaseService` owns explicit Redis lease acquire/release, and `IdempotencyService` claims or replays logical turns through durable `runtime_turn_receipts` plus Redis receipt markers. No web or Telegram traffic is cut over yet, but Step 8 is now honestly in progress instead of remaining only a planned ledger item.
- **ADR-072 Step 7 bundle/provider warm flow:** `apps/runtime` bundle warm/invalidate endpoints now own the real Step 7 runtime state flow instead of only mutating the Step 5 local cache. Warm requires `materializedSpecId` plus `runtimeTier`, persists `runtime_bundle_states.last_warmed_at`, clears `invalidated_at`, and writes Redis bundle warm markers; invalidate clears matching local cache entries plus Postgres/Redis bundle state; and follow-up hardening keeps shared-state writes ahead of local cache mutation with compensation on late failures. `apps/api` apply/reapply now triggers assistant-wide runtime invalidate + current-bundle warm through temporary explicit `PERSAI_RUNTIME_BASE_URL` wiring and also pushes provider-gateway warmup through temporary explicit `PERSAI_PROVIDER_GATEWAY_BASE_URL` wiring. `apps/provider-gateway` catalog state is now seeded from bootstrap config only until the first control-plane apply warmup arrives, after which `GET /api/v1/providers/catalog` reports the control-plane model snapshot instead of a bootstrap-only authority. Both explicit `unset => skip` activation seams remain temporary and are queued for removal in Step 9 when native web execution makes runtime/provider-gateway configuration mandatory.
- **ADR-072 Step 6 runtime-state foundation:** completed the shared runtime-state foundation for the PersAI-native execution plane. Prisma now defines `runtime_bundle_states`, `runtime_sessions`, `runtime_session_compactions`, and `runtime_turn_receipts`; `apps/runtime` now owns concrete Postgres persistence services plus Redis coordination services for session leases, conversation-session pointers, turn-receipt/idempotency markers, and bundle warm markers; and runtime config now validates `DATABASE_URL` plus `RUNTIME_STATE_REDIS_URL`. `assistant_materialized_specs.runtime_bundle*` remains the authoritative compiled bundle artifact, so Step 6 closes the shared-state foundation without cutting request traffic over or creating a second bundle-document authority.
- **ADR-072 Step 5 runtime shell:** added `apps/runtime` as the dark PersAI-native runtime-service boundary with `loadRuntimeConfig`, `/health`, `/ready`, `/metrics`, and bounded `/api/v1/bundles/warm` + `/api/v1/bundles/invalidate` seams over an in-memory native-bundle registry. The shell validates native bundle hash/metadata before caching, exposes runtime observability counters, keeps `executionEnabled: false`, and deliberately avoids request-time turn execution or distributed session state until later ADR-072 steps land.
- **ADR-072 Step 4 provider gateway shell:** added `apps/provider-gateway` as the first dark-service execution-plane component with real OpenAI and Anthropic provider modules, bootstrap catalog projection, explicit warmup boundary, and `/health`, `/ready`, `/metrics`, `GET /api/v1/providers/catalog`, and `POST /api/v1/providers/warmup` seams. Added `loadProviderGatewayConfig` in `packages/config`, focused gateway tests, and a temporary bootstrap catalog/config seam confined to the new service until Step 7 replaces it with PersAI control-plane warm/invalidate input.
- **ADR-072 Step 3 neutral runtime facade:** added `assistant-runtime.facade.ts` as the PersAI-native application runtime seam, converted `assistant-runtime-adapter.types.ts` into an internal `OpenClawRuntimeBridge`, and introduced `OpenClawAssistantRuntimeFacade` so current services/controllers route through one neutral boundary while legacy OpenClaw payload translation stays trapped at the edge. Updated the workspace-management DI wiring plus focused facade/app-service tests so later native runtime slices can replace the executor behind this seam instead of continuing to grow OpenClaw-shaped contracts across the app layer.
- **ADR-072 Step 2 runtime bundle persistence:** added `packages/runtime-bundle` with the first PersAI-native `AssistantRuntimeBundle` compiler, deterministic bundle document/hash helpers, and additive persistence on `assistant_materialized_specs` via `runtime_bundle`, `runtime_bundle_document`, and `runtime_bundle_hash`. `MaterializeAssistantPublishedVersionService` now dual-writes the native bundle beside legacy `openclawBootstrap` / `openclawWorkspace` artifacts while keeping the active request-time executor and legacy `contentHash` path unchanged.
- **ADR-072 Step 1 runtime contract package:** added `packages/runtime-contract` with the first PersAI-native shared runtime contracts for runtime tiers, conversation addresses, bundle refs, attachments/artifacts, session resolve/compaction, turn requests/results/stream events, and health/readiness status. This establishes the native runtime vocabulary before bundle persistence or request-time cutover work begins.
- **Cursor continuity rule for ADR-072:** added `.cursor/rules/adr072-runtime-continuity.mdc` as an always-on Cursor rule for the PersAI-native runtime replacement program. New Cursor sessions must now read the ADR-072 source-of-truth pack, continue from the latest handoff/ledger checkpoint, stay within one smallest executable step, and update handoff/changelog/ADR ledger before ending the session.
- **SR10a sandbox-key propagation hotfix:** follow-up live validation showed the assistant-scoped `sandboxSessionKey` fix was only partially wired, so the approved OpenClaw fork now also carries that key through the embedded runner attempt/compaction paths. New web chats should now stop allocating distinct Docker sandboxes solely because the value was dropped before native runtime execution.
- **OpenClaw sandbox propagation pin advance:** `infra/dev/gitops/openclaw-approved-sha.txt` now points to `c94e6d55d83a864640b4065fb9b8af49e9e728b4`, the fork revision that closes the remaining `sandboxSessionKey` propagation gap found during post-deploy live probes. Do not hand-edit `infra/helm/values-dev.yaml`; let CI rebuild and repin the dev image from the approved SHA.
- **SR10a stable web sandbox reuse + final runtime split traces:** the approved OpenClaw fork now reuses one assistant-scoped sandbox for normal web turns instead of tying Docker sandbox identity to each chat id, while also emitting fine-grained `agent_turn.sandbox.*` and `agent_turn.openai_ws.*` stages so fresh-vs-warm latency can be explained with real runtime evidence rather than one opaque `sandbox_resolved` / `first_delta` gap.
- **OpenClaw latency-fix pin advance:** `infra/dev/gitops/openclaw-approved-sha.txt` now points to `2451e5c40426ef04b9323dbd76fa6ddc9a146ada`, the fork revision that adds stable web sandbox reuse, deeper sandbox/OpenAI transport tracing, and the PersAI bridge plumbing for the new sandbox identity seam. Do not hand-edit `infra/helm/values-dev.yaml`; let CI rebuild and repin the dev image from the approved SHA.
- **SR10a runtime latency trace deepening:** the approved OpenClaw fork now emits internal `agent_turn.*` trace stages for the pre-first-delta path (`sandbox_resolved`, skills/bootstrap prompt assembly, tool runtime setup, session/context-engine open, `prompt_enter`) so slow web turns can be localized inside native runtime execution instead of being lumped into one opaque `attachment_context -> first_delta` gap.
- **OpenClaw latency-investigation pin advance:** `infra/dev/gitops/openclaw-approved-sha.txt` now points to `0c8099ce7c7075a8ac811ab4a4c1c6abb7924f89`, the fork revision that adds the internal-stage instrumentation and syncs the fork patch verifier/docs for that native trace seam. Do not hand-edit `infra/helm/values-dev.yaml`; let CI rebuild and repin the dev image from the approved SHA.
- **Web manual-only compaction + Telegram user auto-compaction toggle:** PersAI now disables automatic threshold compaction for web runtime turns so the web product follows manual `Compact now` semantics, while Telegram gets a user-facing `autoCompactionEnabled` setting in the existing config panel. Telegram auto-compaction defaults to **on**, materializes into OpenClaw runtime bootstrap, and Telegram `/compact` hints now appear only when the user has turned auto-compaction **off**.
- **OpenClaw compaction policy pin advance:** `infra/dev/gitops/openclaw-approved-sha.txt` now points to `ca3f4408485aba842d53c74ec447748606fed0df`, the fork revision that adds runtime support for surface-specific `autoCompactionEnabled` overrides and the paired docs/tests for that behavior. Do not hand-edit `infra/helm/values-dev.yaml`; let CI rebuild and repin the dev image from the approved SHA.
- **Admin runtime: compaction banner message-count toggle:** `optimizationPolicy.compaction` now includes `suggestCompactionByMessageCount` (default `false`). **Admin → Runtime → Compaction** exposes a checkbox so operators can re-enable the legacy “long thread by message count” hint when needed; otherwise the web compaction banner follows **session token estimates only** (short messages no longer trigger the hint by count alone). OpenAPI/contracts regenerated; OpenClaw fork accepts the optional field in strict `agents.defaults.compaction` so bootstrap validation does not reject PersAI governance payloads.
- **ADR-071 audit status correction:** the current codebase now shows real slices 1-5 wiring for heartbeat, context economy, OpenAI tuning, admin runtime controls, and compaction UX through the intended PersAI/OpenClaw seams. The optimization track is still not perfectly clean yet because Helm/runtime-pool optimization defaults remain as a transitional infra baseline instead of a fully retired second authority, and the cheaper dedicated compaction-model path mentioned in the ADR is still not delivered.
- **OpenClaw optimization pin advance:** `infra/dev/gitops/openclaw-approved-sha.txt` and `infra/helm/values-dev.yaml` now point to `dfa95c5eb83a27d5679e599f2fb390bf8671c00d`, the pushed fork revision that completes the runtime-side optimization-policy layering and slice 1-5 execution-path cleanup. The dev image digest is cleared so CI can rebuild and repin the matching OpenClaw image.
- **Slice 4 admin runtime polish controls:** `Admin > Runtime` now acts as the real control-plane page for system runtime policy instead of a narrow provider-routing form. Persisted admin-managed runtime settings include `heartbeat`, `contextPruning`, `compaction`, and `OpenAI` tuning policy alongside the system provider/model catalog, and those settings now materialize into PersAI bootstrap/governance payloads and OpenClaw request-scoped runtime config overlays. The UI keeps fallback explicit as a runtime-failure fallback only, keeps plan model choice in Plans, and enforces that both system and plan model selections come only from the admin-managed available model catalog.
- **Slice 3 OpenAI tuning policy wiring:** PersAI runtime settings now drive OpenAI-specific runtime knobs end-to-end instead of only defining Helm baselines. `responsesServerCompaction`, `openaiWsWarmup`, `fastMode`, and `serviceTier` now flow from admin-managed runtime policy through materialized bootstrap/internal settings into OpenClaw web/chat/stream/heartbeat/cron execution paths, while Helm keeps only deployment-safe pool defaults.
- **Slice 2 context economy wiring:** PersAI runtime settings now drive `contextPruning` and `compaction` end-to-end instead of stopping at pool config generation. Admin-managed policy is materialized into bootstrap/governance, then applied as an effective OpenClaw config overlay for runtime chat, preview, heartbeat, and isolated cron/reminder execution so long-running chats can shed stale tool-result weight before bootstrap/persona trimming is attempted.
- **Slice 1 heartbeat hygiene wiring:** PersAI now stops materializing a contentful default `HEARTBEAT.md`, and heartbeat policy is no longer only a Helm/static baseline. The disabled shared-pool heartbeat baseline (`every: "0m"`, `target: "none"`, `lightContext: true`, `isolatedSession: true`) remains rendered in pool config, while OpenClaw heartbeat also refreshes PersAI admin-managed runtime settings and rebuilds its scheduler/config overlay from that control-plane truth so one implicit shared `agent:main` heartbeat no longer owns the SaaS runtime path.
- **OpenClaw SaaS optimization docs-first baseline (ADR-071):** added `docs/ADR/071-openclaw-saas-context-and-runtime-optimization.md` to make heartbeat hygiene, context economy, OpenAI tuning policy, admin/runtime optimization controls, compaction UX, and deferred bootstrap budgeting an explicit PersAI-owned control-plane program. Updated `OPENCLAW-SAAS-RUNTIME-PLAN.md`, `SCALING-READINESS-PLAN.md`, `ROADMAP.md`, `TEST-PLAN.md`, `ARCHITECTURE.md`, and `API-BOUNDARY.md` so the repo now has one queued post-`SR10` optimization track with a fixed order: heartbeat first, bootstrap last.
- **SR10a end-to-end latency trace baseline:** Admin Overview now owns one bounded trace toggle for slow-turn investigation across PersAI and OpenClaw. PersAI captures stage timings for Telegram, web sync, and web stream turn paths, forwards one `X-Persai-Overview-Trace-Id` to the OpenClaw runtime bridge, and merges returned runtime stages into the same in-memory sample shown in `/admin`. The Overview trace panel now separates PersAI stages from OpenClaw runtime stages and highlights the longest stage so the next SR10 runtime optimization pass can target a measured bottleneck instead of guessing. This slice deliberately avoids persistent telemetry or a second runtime-side enablement path. The approved OpenClaw fork pin advances to `63bebfddcb4e6d41e67500226735aa64bf443efd`.
- **SR10 load-test harness baseline:** added `scripts/loadtest/run-sr10.cjs`, `scripts/loadtest/sr10.example.json`, and `scripts/loadtest/README.md` as the first runnable repo-local `SR10` pack for the practical `100 / 500 / 1000` execution ladder. The harness drives real PersAI seams (`web sync`, `web stream`, internal Telegram turn, staged attachment, voice transcription), writes per-run JSON evidence, snapshots admin overview before/after each phase when admin auth is provided, and stops automatically on gate failures instead of pretending later tiers are valid. This is tooling/evidence preparation only and does **not** claim that canonical `SR10` capacity proof (`1000 / 3000 / 5000`) has been completed.
- **Scaling-readiness control layer (ADR-070):** added `docs/ADR/070-scaling-readiness-program-and-clean-delivery-discipline.md` as the umbrella governance ADR for the `1000–5000` online-user readiness program. Added `docs/SCALING-READINESS-PLAN.md` as the canonical execution plan with `SR0`-`SR10` slice order, Cursor-agent handoff protocol, clean-delivery rules, and deploy/verification cadence. `ROADMAP.md`, `TEST-PLAN.md`, and `SESSION-HANDOFF.md` are now aligned to that program baseline.
- **SR1 closure baseline:** added `docs/SR1-OBSERVABILITY-BASELINE.md` as the minimal operational runbook for closing `SR1`. The baseline now explicitly defines API `/health` / `/ready` / `/metrics` observation, the first required alert set, and the current honest OpenClaw-side signal truth: `/healthz`, `/readyz`, guarded readiness details, startup/readiness logs, Telegram failure logs when enabled, and PersAI `runtime_route` lines as live routing proof. `TEST-PLAN.md`, `SESSION-HANDOFF.md`, `SCALING-READINESS-PLAN.md`, and `ROADMAP.md` were updated accordingly so `SR1` can close and the next active slice becomes `SR2`.
- **SR2 workload rollout baseline:** Helm chart truth for `api`, `web`, and OpenClaw runtime pools now makes rollout assumptions explicit instead of relying on Kubernetes defaults. The chart now carries explicit deployment strategy, `minReadySeconds`, `revisionHistoryLimit`, and workload `resources`, plus default-disabled `HorizontalPodAutoscaler`, `PodDisruptionBudget`, and `topologySpreadConstraints` seams. Base `values.yaml` also now defines explicit `ingress` defaults so both base and env-specific chart renders are valid.
- **SR2b first disruption / placement baseline:** the first enabled `SR2` disruption baseline now applies to `web`: `replicaCount: 2`, `PodDisruptionBudget minAvailable: 1`, and topology spread across hostname and zone. `web` autoscaling remains explicit but disabled, and `api` plus OpenClaw pools are still intentionally left outside enabled multi-replica/disruption claims until their behavior is justified and verified in the target environment.
- **SR2 closure baseline:** `api` now also carries the same bounded disruption/placement baseline as `web` (`replicaCount: 2`, `PodDisruptionBudget minAvailable: 1`, hostname+zone topology spread). `SR2` now closes with explicit rollout/disruption/placement truth for the control-plane workloads, explicit-but-disabled HPA assumptions, and an explicit non-claim that OpenClaw pool topology is **not** the same thing as proven multi-replica runtime correctness.
- **SR3 thread-creation race hardening:** API chat-thread bootstrap no longer assumes a single process wins `find -> create` cleanly on unique `surfaceThreadKey`. `PrismaAssistantChatRepository` now exposes `findOrCreateChatBySurfaceThread(...)` and treats Prisma `P2002` conflicts as the expected concurrent-create case by falling back to the already-created chat row. The touched web/telegram/reminder bootstrap paths now use that atomic seam instead of raw `find -> create` logic.
- **SR3b adapter preflight pressure hardening:** `OpenClawRuntimeAdapter` no longer re-runs `/healthz` + `/readyz` on every nearby runtime call. Preflight now uses a short TTL cache plus in-flight dedup per runtime tier, and runtime-side failure classes invalidate the cached state so the next request rechecks live readiness instead of trusting stale success.
- **SR3c shared Prisma client baseline:** the API process no longer opens separate Prisma clients for identity-access vs workspace-management. `WorkspaceManagementPrismaService` now resolves as an alias to the shared `PrismaService` singleton, reducing duplicate connection-pool pressure without changing the higher-level API service/repository contracts.
- **SR3d distributed peer abuse baseline:** `peerKey`-based inbound abuse throttling is no longer kept only in process-local memory. The touched peer window now persists in Postgres via `assistant_abuse_peer_states`, and peer-attempt registration uses an atomic upsert path so the Telegram abuse guard does not silently reset when the next request lands on another API replica.
- **SR3e distributed abuse counter closing pass:** user-level and assistant-level abuse counters no longer depend on `find -> compute -> upsert` under burst contention. The touched abuse registration path now runs inside a serializable Postgres transaction with retry on `P2034`, so shared abuse state increments remain honest across competing API replicas without changing the higher-level abuse policy.
- **SR4 session continuity ceiling baseline:** OpenClaw readiness now treats PersAI runtime `multi_replica` session mode as not yet supported by code, not as an operator-declarable healthy state. The runtime code confirms that Redis-backed apply/spec storage shares only apply metadata; session store continuity, workspace continuity, execution ordering, and restart handoff for a single runtime session are still process-local or per-host concerns, so `/ready` remains `not ready` for that mode.
- **SR4 delivery pin update:** PersAI dev gitops now pins the approved OpenClaw fork to `7cb2c4b360a57b4523d775b67b11a11189fbe9bb`, matching the committed single-replica runtime contract, queue backpressure signal, and stricter workspace cleanup bypass guard.

### Changed

- **SR10-pre-ui admin dashboard restructuring (closed 2026-04-07):**
  - **Admin Overview** (`/admin`): system-wide runtime dashboard with p50/p95/p99/max latency (web/TG/all routes), active users (15min window), active web chats, all three runtime tier preflight status with flap tracking, queue pressure (in-flight/peak/rps), storage pressure (token budget + media), sandbox health (RSS/heap/external/arrayBuffers/CPU), process uptime, auto-derived warnings. Minimalist collapsible UI.
  - **Ops Cockpit** (`/admin/ops`): 5 users/page with search. Per-user Quota & Usage card (token budget, media storage, active web chats with progress bars), chat stats (total/active/archived), channel bindings (provider/surface/state).
  - **Business** (`/admin/business`): platform-wide aggregates from `appUser.count()` (all registered users). KPI strip: Users, Assistants, Messages + threads, Channels, Plans Used, Apply OK%. Users-by-plan distribution (includes users without assistants). Quota pressure, channel adoption, publish/apply health, plan catalog config.
  - New backend endpoints: `GET /admin/overview/dashboard`, `GET /admin/business/platform`. Extended `GET /admin/ops/cockpit` with `quotaUsage`, `chatStats`, `channels`. Extended `PlatformHttpMetricsService` with peak in-flight requests and process start time.
  - **Avatar fix**: assistant emoji avatar centering in chat bubbles.
- **SR9c dual quota pre-check for uploads (Variant B):** uploads now check BOTH media upload budget (`mediaStorageBytesUsed`) AND workspace disk availability (sandbox `du -sb` via OpenClaw) before accepting user files. OpenClaw fork adds `GET /api/v1/runtime/workspace/storage-usage` endpoint; PersAI adapter calls it before upload. Web shows localized banner (`workspace_storage_full`), Telegram sends guaranteed system notice. Admin UI labels renamed: "Media upload budget (MB)" / "Workspace disk (MB)" with tooltips. Both quotas remain independently configurable per plan.

### Fixed

- **ADR-073 split preview/welcome prompts + explicit welcome-chat trigger:** admin Prompt Constructor now exposes two separate hidden first-turn templates: one for setup/recreate preview character testing and one for the real post-publish welcome chat. Runtime materialization now compiles separate `previewTurnPrompt` and `welcomeTurnPrompt` fields into the bundle, setup preview uses the preview-only prompt, and live welcome turns use the welcome-only prompt with the old locale-specific hardcoded greeting kept only as a fallback for older/missing bundles. Setup/recreate still routes explicitly into `thread=welcome&welcome=1`, and `apps/web` still avoids auto-creating a welcome chat merely because an existing account happens to have zero chats after manual deletion.
- **ADR-073 reset runtime-state cleanup + desktop lifecycle polish:** assistant reset no longer fails on `runtime_bundle_states_materialized_spec_id_fkey`. Reset and admin user deletion now clear assistant-scoped runtime state rows (`runtime_turn_receipts`, `runtime_session_compactions`, `runtime_sessions`, `runtime_bundle_states`) before deleting materialized specs and published versions, so recreate/reset cleanup stays aligned with the native runtime state model. The desktop assistant settings slide-over was widened and rebalanced so the main name/avatar block and action buttons stop stacking into a narrow single-column “portyanka”, setup personality editing now uses a cleaner two-column desktop layout, and personality sliders in both setup and settings now move in discrete `10`-point steps with clearer current-value display.
- **ADR-073 setup lifecycle duplicate-write reduction:** the setup wizard now treats the successful step-3 preview persistence as the authoritative draft sync before publish, so final create no longer repeats `POST /me/onboarding`, `POST /assistant`, and the full draft patch after a successful preview. Final create now only uploads/patches a custom avatar when needed, then publishes and routes into the explicit welcome-chat handoff. Focused web regression coverage now protects both uploaded-avatar and preset-avatar flows.
- **ADR-072 T15-6 native `tts` stabilization:** the initial native `tts` baseline now also closes the main live root causes behind avoidable provider fallback churn. Assistant voice normalization/materialization now filters incompatible provider/voice combinations before they reach the runtime bundle, the provider chain now stays deterministic instead of jumping unpredictably across multiple providers, assistant voice UI is aligned to the active primary provider with gender-filtered choices plus a live ElevenLabs voice picker, and Yandex speech generation now suppresses unsupported `voice + role` hint pairs such as `jane + friendly` instead of forwarding them upstream and failing with avoidable `400` responses.
- **ADR-072 T15-6 Telegram native media delivery handoff:** Telegram outbound replies no longer try to download the transient runtime-output object after `MediaDeliveryService` re-persists native media into canonical assistant-chat storage. `HandleInternalTelegramTurnService` now rewrites outbound media to the persisted assistant attachment object keys before the Telegram bot sender runs, which fixes live `image_generate` delivery to Telegram without reopening the media architecture.
- **ADR-072 shared compaction stability hardening:** native shared compaction now keeps explicit runtime semantics for `main_turn`, `tool_loop_followup`, `manual_compaction`, and `auto_compaction` instead of inferring behavior from channel/instructions. A same-turn durable `compact_context` now suppresses redundant post-turn auto compaction, follow-up provider calls rebuild context from refreshed compaction state instead of stale pre-compaction history, durable reusable state is accepted only as validated `persai.runtimeSessionCompaction.v2`, invalid/assistant-like outputs and old poisoned rows are ignored on reuse, and post-compaction session token state now resets to `currentTokens=null` / `totalTokensFresh=false` so stale accounting does not retrigger compaction decisions.
- **ADR-072 Step 4 provider-gateway tsconfig resolve fix:** the new `apps/provider-gateway/tsconfig.json` now extends `../../packages/tsconfig/nest.json` via a stable relative path instead of the package-style `@persai/tsconfig/nest.json` reference, avoiding IDE/tsserver resolution errors in the new dark-service app while keeping the Step 4 code and build behavior unchanged.
- **Admin overview tail visibility + bootstrap consume tier routing:** `/admin` percentile aggregation no longer truncates web/runtime latency buckets at `5s`, so `10s+` spikes stay visible during validation, and `consumeBootstrapWorkspace(...)` now targets the real `runtimeTier` instead of silently defaulting to the free shared pool for web/Telegram follow-up bootstrap consumption.
- **Web manual compact false error:** NestJS defaults `POST` to **201 Created** when `@HttpCode` is omitted; `POST /assistant/chats/web/:chatId/compact` therefore returned **201** while the web client and OpenAPI expect **200**, so `compactChat()` threw before reading the body and showed a compaction failure banner even when OpenClaw succeeded. The compact route now sets **`@HttpCode(200)`** (kubectl-confirmed `status":201` on success before the fix).
- **Compaction unavailable vs generic chat error:** when OpenClaw returned `409` / `ok: false` for manual web or Telegram compaction, PersAI surfaced `invalid_response` as a **500** and the web client showed the generic “Chat could not complete this turn.” The adapter now uses `compaction_unavailable`, maps to **409** with code `compaction_unavailable`, `POST /assistant/chats/web/:id/compact` wraps errors with `toAssistantInboundHttpException`, and the web UI shows localized compaction-specific copy instead of a failed chat turn.
- **Telegram `/compact` language:** workspace locale is normalized (`ru`, `ru-*` → Russian). Skip reasons from OpenClaw (e.g. “Already compacted”) are localized for Russian replies instead of English prefixed with Russian boilerplate.
- **Web chat manual compaction UX:** after “Compress now”, a previous generic turn-failure banner could stay visible because `issue` was not cleared on success; manual compaction activities were omitted from the timeline when they had no `afterMessageId`. Successful compact now clears the stale error, links the activity to the last message when possible, and appends orphan activities so the token before/after line is visible. **OpenClaw dev pin** advances to `c4be65eef08e23a7128e032625214811abe2c741` for the companion strict-schema compatibility commit.
- **Telegram `/compact` vs compaction hints:** hints told users to send `/compact`, but PersAI treated it as a normal inbound turn, so nothing deterministic happened and the model reply was easy to miss. Internal Telegram turns now recognize `/compact` (optional `@BotName` suffix) and call OpenClaw `POST /api/v1/runtime/chat/channel/compact`, replying with a short outcome message (including token estimates when returned). This needs the OpenClaw fork revision that adds that route (`8bbc9e222edbf5a642bba8004a2486cd4076c078`); dev `openclaw-approved-sha.txt` advances to match so CI can rebuild/re-pin the image.
- **SR10a admin overview pod debug routing:** `/admin` now keeps `Auto (sticky)` as the default multi-pod diagnostics path while also allowing one-shot service probing and manual pinning to a discovered `api` pod for direct pod-local comparison. This stays scoped to admin overview debugging only and does not change the underlying non-aggregated telemetry semantics.
- **SR10a admin overview multi-pod honesty/stickiness:** `/admin` no longer presents pod-local overview telemetry as if it were one cluster-wide truth when `api` runs with multiple replicas. The admin overview payload now reports the serving API instance identity, the UI labels the pod-local scope explicitly, and the web `/api/v1` proxy keeps `/admin/overview/*` sticky to one reachable `api` pod when possible so `Trace ON/OFF`, refresh, and recent in-memory trace samples stay aligned during one investigation session.
- **SR10a post-trace stabilization:** after the bounded latency-trace rollout exposed two runtime-facing regressions under active diagnosis, the dev web proxy now preserves SSE streaming semantics for `/api/v1/*` event-stream responses, and the approved OpenClaw fork pin advances to `c735051385f8bb5d1cc8b14b559edff75ff4ac33`, which stops retryable PersAI Telegram timeouts from surfacing as unhandled rejections that kill the OpenClaw worker process.
- **Token budget exhausted error UX:** when the monthly token budget is exceeded, the abuse rate limiter was surfacing it as generic `rate_limited` ("Requests are temporarily limited"). Now detects `quota_pressure_temporary_block` reason and throws a specific `token_budget_exhausted` conflict error. Frontend and Telegram show a dedicated "Monthly token budget has been exhausted" message matching the tool daily limit style.
- **Admin ops auth middleware bug:** `plan-override` and `workspace-subscription` routes (POST/DELETE) were not registered in `ClerkAuthMiddleware.forRoutes()`, causing all requests to these endpoints to return 401. This blocked the admin "Apply test plan" and "Apply workspace subscription" actions entirely. Fixed by adding the 4 missing route registrations to `identity-access.module.ts`.
- **SR9c media storage quota user-facing UX:** media storage quota errors now return structured HTTP 409 responses with `media_storage_quota_exceeded` code and `usedMb`/`limitMb` details instead of generic `BadRequestException`. Web chat displays a localized banner (EN/RU) showing exact storage usage and guidance. Telegram inbound media errors now include usage figures in the LLM prompt so the agent can explain the situation to the user. Removed dead legacy fallback code in `inbound-media.service.ts` and fixed `uploadChatAttachment` to use structured error parsing. Verified that voice recording and assistant-generated image paths handle quota correctly without crashes.
- **SR9 billing/quota concurrency package:** completed the bounded `SR9a`-`SR9f` code-pass set for commercial correctness under concurrency. Assistant plan override changes now dirty materialization state, token and media quota ledgers use serializable capped apply paths, touched media uploads roll back retained blobs when the object no longer fits, active web chat creation uses a serializable under-cap seam on both send and staged-upload paths, workspace subscription sync now has an idempotent persist-and-dirty propagation seam, and internal runtime tool quota `consume` now enforces the current server-side daily limit instead of trusting a stale runtime-supplied one. Canonical `SCALING-READINESS-PLAN.md`, `ROADMAP.md`, `TEST-PLAN.md`, `SESSION-HANDOFF.md`, `API-BOUNDARY.md`, ADR-054, and the touched supporting ADR/docs were updated to keep `SR9` honest while the package awaits one deploy/live evidence wave before deciding whether `SR10` can open.
- **SR8 operational closure baseline:** `SR8` is now closed operationally after one deploy plus one bounded live validation window across the touched replay seams.
